# Roadmap reference: reconciliation, tiers, and build history

This is the deeper reference behind the lean status board in `docs/working/CONSENSUS_ROADMAP.md` (which is now JUST the is-X-done board). It holds the ground-truth order-of-work reconciliation, the Tier A through E sequencing, the derive-from-fundamentals audit, and the dated build-history sections. Read the status board first; come here for the reasoning and the history. Nothing here is the live tracker; the board is.


This reconciles the three ordering artifacts in the repo against what is built in code, into one authoritative sequence, each item cited to where its gate lives. It is a synthesis for the owner to sign off on, not a maintained document; nothing here is committed until you approve it.

The three sources it reconciles:

- **`ROADMAP.md`**, the near-term critical path to a living, talking world (milestones M0 through M4).
- **`docs/design.md` Part 60**, the full implementation staging (Stage 0 through Stage 14).
- **`docs/audit.md` Section 3**, the research backlog: every open item tagged `R-XXX` with its site (`Part N`), its prerequisites, and its couplings, plus the resolved-item record (Part 62).

The reconciliation was checked against a direct read of every crate's modules, tests, and the calibration manifest, so "done" below means built and proven in code, not merely planned.

## The headline reconciliation (read this first)

The build did not follow Part 60's stage numbers in order. It followed the research-gate dependency order instead, front-loading the determinism bedrock, the reasoning-and-being core, the physics substrate, and the embodiment stack, because those are the pieces the emergent design cannot be proven without. The consequence is that the actual frontier is best read as a research-gated dependency graph plus the `ROADMAP.md` M-slice, and Part 60's stage numbers are a topic index rather than a build order.

Three divergences the ground-truth read exposes, stated plainly so the sign-off is honest:

- **The code is ahead of `ROADMAP.md`'s prose.** `ROADMAP.md` still says the deep being model is "absent" and the map is "entirely unbuilt." Neither holds: the being model (genome, intrinsic beliefs, axioms, value profile) is wired end to end through `seed_dawn_populations`, and the map generates, classifies biomes, builds a level-of-detail quadtree, and renders in a windowed viewer, proven bit-identical by `crates/world/tests/zoom.rs`. `ROADMAP.md`'s "Where we are" section is stale and should be refreshed.
- **The code is ahead of the audit's bookkeeping in the determinism cluster.** The audit still lists `R-CMD-ORDER` among the open determinism items, but the mechanism is built (`crates/core/src/command.rs`: `CommandBuffer`, `EventQueue`, the total ordering key). This is the same "mechanism built, item open until consolidated" state that `R-LANG-TYPOLOGY` is in. The audit's resolved count (28) undercounts what code proves; a consolidation pass is owed for `R-CMD-ORDER`, `R-LANG-TYPOLOGY`, and the canonical-walk and reduce helpers.
- **The physics substrate and embodiment stack are built ahead of their nominal Part 60 stage.** Five physics floors (biology, mechanical, fluids, chem-optics, electricity-and-magnetism) and the full homeostasis-to-controller-to-evolve embodiment chain exist and are tested, though Part 60 places the physics substrate as a Stage 14 concern. They are substrate, proven in isolation, not yet integrated into a running world tick.

So the single biggest truth for sequencing: the engine is a deterministic, serial, CPU, promoted-tier core with a viewable generated map, a deep cognition-and-language core, and a broad shelf of tested-but-not-yet-integrated substrate modules. What stands between it and a running world is not more substrate. It is **owner calibration**, **integration into the canonical runner**, and then the **parallel, persistence, and made-world** tracks.


## Tier A: done (built and proven, research resolved)

Each of these is implemented in code with a determinism or behavioural test, and its research question is resolved in Part 62 unless noted.

- **The determinism bedrock.** Q32.32 `Fixed`, the per-entity counter RNG and the canonical draw-keying schema (`R-RNG-COORD`, site Part 3.2, record 62.15, `ROADMAP.md` M0), the canonical-state boundary that makes a float in canon a compile error (Part 58), the state hash (Part 3.5), the id registry with save-side id continuity, and the append-only event log. Gate met: `crates/core/tests/determinism.rs` holds one-seed-one-world across thread counts.
- **The command and event-queue substrate.** `CommandBuffer` and `EventQueue` with the total ordering key (`R-CMD-ORDER`, site Part 4.3 and 57). Mechanism built; the audit item awaits consolidation (see the headline divergence).
- **The GPU canonical-arithmetic and transcendental path** (`R-GPU-CANON-PIN`, resolved, record 62.23, Part 3.4/5.4). Fixed-point multiply and divide and the full transcendental set (exp, ln, powf, powi, and the CORDIC sin, cos, atan, asin) are built as CubeCL `#[cube]` kernels in `crates/gpu` and proven bit-identical to the `crates/core` `Fixed` oracle on the RTX 5090 (`crates/gpu/tests/stage0_gate.rs`, `transcendental_gate.rs`), alongside the fixed-point diffusion field (tile-invariant, matching the CPU bench at about 22x, `diffusion_gate.rs`), all with a no-float source guard (`canon_guard.rs`). The cross-backend determinism gate proves the Stage 0 arithmetic (multiply and divide) bit-identical across three independent CubeCL codegen paths, CUDA (NVRTC), the CPU backend (MLIR/LLVM), and the wgpu Vulkan/SPIR-V backend (cubecl-spirv, run here on lavapipe), all matching the oracle (`cross_backend.rs`). The transcendentals do not yet cross-backend on the non-CUDA paths: on the CPU backend they trip an upstream `cubecl-cpu` constant-propagation panic, and on wgpu the box's only Vulkan adapter is lavapipe (software), too slow for the large unrolled transcendental shaders (though SPIR-V Int64 is supported, proven by a native-i64 probe that ran in milliseconds), so their cross-backend confirmation awaits a cubecl-cpu fix or a hardware Vulkan device. The general u128 `Fixed::sqrt` GPU primitive is now built (a 96-bit limb isqrt in `crates/gpu/src/prim.rs`, bit-identical to the oracle over the full magnitude sweep; asin keeps its faster domain-limited u64 isqrt), and the shared limb primitives (multiply, divide, isqrt) are consolidated in `prim.rs` instead of copied per kernel. Gate remaining: the transcendental cross-backend confirmation (a hardware Vulkan device or a cubecl-cpu fix) and a true multi-vendor hardware device run (a discrete GPU across Metal, DX12, ROCm).
- **GPU-vs-CPU offload map (scoped, `docs/working/GPU_CPU_OFFLOAD_MAP.md`).** A subsystem survey classified every engine compute workload GPU / HYBRID / CPU-parallel / CPU-serial against a five-property framework (domain size, flattenability, control-flow uniformity, arithmetic intensity vs transfer, order-independence). Landed: the diffusion kernel, the perceive notice-roll spike, the runner field-step kernel (clamped-Neumann + relaxation, matching `Field::step`), and worldgen noise + fused biome classify, all bit-identical on the 5090 (`crates/gpu`). Prioritised offload roadmap: finish the temperature field kernel (matches `diffusion_bench`, NOT the runner `Field::step` yet: needs a clamped-Neumann + relaxation variant), then worldgen noise + fused biome (the cleanest standalone win), then a fused resident being-kernel (controller + homeostasis + body-thermal, unlocks the field offload). BEING-KERNEL ARITHMETIC COMPLETE (`crates/gpu/src/being.rs`): `gpu_body_thermal` (#72), `gpu_sat_mul` (#75, a blind-audit-caught overflow bug fixed), `gpu_activate` (#76, the controller activation with a two-limb 128-bit saturating accumulator), `gpu_metabolize` (#78, the homeostasis drain), all bit-identical on the 5090 and each blind-audited. Remaining on the GPU track: fuse the four over one resident being buffer + the reaction-norm matvec + wire into `World::tick`, all SCALE-GATED (the dev map sits below the launch threshold, so these pay only on a large world, which is gated on the reserved-value calibration above)., then pool-tier aggregate mortality and Wright-Fisher drift, then perceive to production. Gate: every GPU verdict is contingent on residency (Part 5.6) AND scale, routed per-deployment by a profile, with bit-identity (R-GPU-CANON-PIN) the price of a canonical offload; Archard wear and wide-i128 EM need a new wide-limb primitive first. The branchy cognition (converse, gossip, belief update, theory-of-mind) and the canonical merges (CommandBuffer, state-hash, naming game, scheduler) stay CPU by contract.
- **Intra-phase per-being parallelism (first phase parallelised).** The throughput lever for the cognition tick: not phase-level scheduling (the minds/belief hub serialises the expensive phases), but parallelising the per-being work WITHIN a phase, over the population N. The `converse` phase already proved the two-pass pattern (a pure read across `workers` threads, then a canonical-order apply through the `CommandKey` barrier); `World::perceive` now takes the same shape (`crates/sim/src/world.rs`, `gather_trace` across `std::thread::scope` workers), proven bit-identical to the serial gather at 2/3/8/16 workers. Remaining candidates: gossip, decide, drift, mortality (all draw-keyed gather-then-apply). The gather uses dynamic load balancing (workers pull work units from an atomic counter, re-canonicalised by a cheap work-unit sort), so it adapts to a hybrid CPU (Intel P and E cores, AMD X3D CCDs) with no topology query; determinism decouples correctness from scheduling, so this cannot change a result. Measured on the reference 265K, perceive scales about 1.8x and plateaus (memory-bound, capped by bandwidth); the compute-bound phases are where the core-heterogeneity win appears. For the memory-bound work the other lever is the GPU (an order of magnitude more bandwidth): the perceive notice roll is proven bit-identical on the GPU (`crates/gpu/src/perceive.rs`, `gpu_notice`, gated over 7200 pairs on the 5090), a canonical offload made possible by the draw-keyed RNG and the pinned fixed-point arithmetic; the full offload (SoA extraction, a resident cross-tick buffer per Part 5.6, hit compaction) is scoped, gated on a profile. Heterogeneous-scheduling design in `docs/deterministic_scheduler_design.md`. Gate: each phase's per-being rolls are already draw-keyed (R-RNG-COORD), so the parallel gather is a pure function of state; width-invariance is the proof.
- **Visual projection (scoped, first slice built).** How the deep world is shown: appearance derived from the canonical physics/material/anatomy data the sim already computes, never authored, with the renderer a non-canonical consumer (Principle 10). A data-driven `VisualProjection` registry (Principle 11) maps optical axes to a material palette, the anatomy part graph to a procgen silhouette, and state to overlays, with a two-tier glyph-then-procgen-sprite view and a content-hash sprite atlas. Scoped in `docs/working/VISUAL_PROJECTION_SCOPED_PROPOSAL.md`; the first slice is built (`physics_terrain_color` in `crates/viewer`, terrain colour from a tile's elevation/moisture/temperature). Awaits sign-off on the substrate shape; the reserved palette values are the owner's aesthetic call.
- **The generated map.** Topology and the 2.5D coordinate model (Part 56), fixed-point fractal worldgen with elevation, moisture, and temperature, biome classification by data-defined ranges, the level-of-detail quadtree (Part 6), and the camera-and-glyph view plus a windowed viewer (Part 14). This is `ROADMAP.md` M1 and Part 60 Stage 2 worldgen, proven by `crates/world/tests/zoom.rs`.
- **The reasoning-and-being core** (Part 60 Stage 3, the most mature area). The evidence engine (`R-EVIDENCE`, 62.7), recursive theory of mind (`R-TOM-UPDATE`, 62.11), the value-distance metric (`R-VALUE-METRIC`, 62.3), axiomatic belief (`R-AXIOM`, 62.4), the genome and genotype-to-phenotype map (`R-GENOME`, 62.5), being representation (`R-BEING-REP`), and the utility-AI decision layer, wired end to end and exercised by `dawn_seed.rs`, `dawn_lifecycle.rs`, and the false-belief-and-deception battery `tom_battery.rs`.
- **Language and dialogue.** The naming game over the roughly sixty-five semantic primes (`ROADMAP.md` M3, `sim/tests/primes.rs`), the emergent lexicon and articulation substrate (`R-LANG-DET` 62.12, `R-LANG-MODALITY` 62.13), the typological substrate (`R-LANG-TYPOLOGY`, built in `crates/sim/src/typology.rs`, item open pending consolidation), and modelled dialogue as a speech-act substrate (`R-CONVERSE` 62.14, `ROADMAP.md` M4, `dialogue_steering.rs`).
- **The physics substrate floors** (`R-PHYS-BIO`, `R-PHYS-MECH`, `R-PHYS-W2`, `R-PHYS-W3`; records 62.16 onward): five data floors and their closed-form fixed-point law kernels, built and tested, the reach-bounding authored layer.
- **The living-substrate and deep-time modules.** Stocks and flows (Part 15), biosphere generation, the pre-dawn radiation epoch, and the genesis sequence (`R-BIOSPHERE`), the species-lineage tree, and edibility as a measured relation.
- **The embodiment and behaviour stack.** Homeostatic physiology and affordances, structured anatomy, the per-part body with wounds and fluids (`R-BUILD-PHYS`, `R-WOUND`, `R-FLUID`, 62.20), emergent locomotion, and the evolved controller with homeostatic-survival selection (`R-BEHAVIOR-EVOLVE`, 62.19), including the eastward-scorer steering fix landed this session.
- **Tier consistency.** The two-tier individual-and-pool model and the conserved-projection registry (`R-TIER-CONSIST`, 62.9), and the resolved institution-function substrate (`R-INST`, 62.8).
- **The institution and ADICO-norm substrate** (`R-INST`, 62.8, Part 36), now built in code (`crates/sim/src/institution.rs`). An institution carries no authored kind: its identity is its structure (roles, ADICO-grammar norms, a blend over an open `FunctionRegistry` of function axes, legitimacy, lineage), and any type is recovered only as a derived, non-authoritative `EticDescriptor` (a fixed-point weighted-Tanimoto match against a `TemplateLibrary` that may be empty, in which case every institution reads generic and the engine runs). `Deontic` is a closed `{May, Must, MustNot}` (a logical primitive), the function axes are an open owner-set registry with a labelled `dev_seed`, and ADICO conditions key off `decision.rs`'s open `InputId` world-fact registry; the norm type (strategy/norm/rule) is derived from which optional fields are present, never a stored tag. `tier.decision_propensity` derives through the `DecisionPropensity` accumulator and `emit_undertaking` gate; the compact `AggregateInstitution` rides on `Pool` (`lod.rs`), its feature vector and legitimacy mass registered as conserved projections and proven conserved across promote/demote/merge/split (`crates/sim/tests/invariants.rs`), with promotion materializing an explicit institution whose signature reproduces the pool's compact vector. The mechanism is proven against a synthetic coordination-pattern stream, with the non-steering test (a race's exotic function axis, carried only as data, crystallizes an institution in a region other races cannot reach, distance-dominating), gloss-blindness (label/column permutation leaves metrics bit-identical), the empty-library fallback, norm-type emergence, order-independence, cross-thread determinism, and descriptor-out-of-hash (`Phase::CRYSTALLIZE = 0x1A`). Gate: mechanism built and tested; the LIVE crystallization detector wiring into the running agent loop (feeding it the decision layer's real coordinated undertakings and minting `InstId`s on the tick) is a NAMED FOLLOW-ON, and the reserved `inst.*` and `tier.decision_propensity` values (`calibration/reserved.toml`) are the owner's to set before a calibrated world crystallizes institutions.

## Tier B: the near-term frontier (what to do next), with gates

This is where the consensus order matters most, because the substrate shelf is deep but the running world is thin. Recommended order:

1. **Owner calibration of the reserved values.** The manifest carries 153 entries; 76 are set and 77 remain fail-loud sentinels (`calibration/reserved.toml`, RUNBOOK section 4). Under the Calibrated profile the engine refuses to start on any unset value, so the real (non-dev-fixture) world cannot run until these are set. This is the single largest unblock and gates everything that runs a world rather than a test. Gate: each value is reserved-with-basis at its mechanism site; you set it, the manifest graduates it to `set`. Progress (2026-07-03): Batches 1 through 11 graduated through the whole-batch fully-blind audit (worksheet §7), plus the three semantic design-changes (§8), the differentiated language-floor resolution (record 62.24), and the structured-value format (`require_map`) with the compound entries graduated (§10, the drift operator set, calcification rate and cap, the conformity and prestige strengths); the remaining reserved include the components the design leaves without a magnitude (calcification brittleness, the fission and deviation thresholds, the per-axis physiology drains, burn scale from the physics floor), the dawn-floor values, the environmental levers (thermal band and medium promotion), and the physics-floor batch.
2. **Wire the built core into the canonical runner.** `crates/sim/src/runner.rs` carries the physics field layer (Part 5.4, 5.5) with zero authored numbers. The being-and-cognition core is now composed onto that spine. Gate: integration, not research.
   - DONE (composition increment): the runner owns an optional cognition `World` and runs `World::tick` as a fixed sub-phase after the field phases, in a pinned within-tick order (field first). `Runner::with_world` (`crates/sim/src/runner.rs`), composite `state_hash` folds the field-side hash then the world's, and the determinism triad plus a clock-lockstep invariant is proven in `crates/sim/tests/determinism_harness.rs` (`composed_runner_tick_*`, worker widths [1,2,3,8]). No new authored number, RNG draw, or `Phase`. Honest limit: no field-to-cognition data flow yet, and the world hash does not yet fold the being lifecycle (genomes, ages, affect) or the dialogue log.
   - STEERING BOUNDARY (Principle 9, guiding-star audit): the canonical-emergent runner's behaviour source is the evolved controller (Part 8.4), never an authored policy. `World::decide`'s authored drive-and-action repertoire (the sentient deliberative tier, Part 8.1) is steering at the level of behaviour, so `Runner::with_world` fail-loud rejects a world that carries one (`World::has_behaviour`), quarantining the authored path off the canonical spine (proven by `the_canonical_runner_refuses_an_authored_behaviour_repertoire`). The composed cognition phases the runner does drive (belief, dialogue, gossip, language) are emergent and data-driven.
   - DONE (field-to-behaviour coupling, evolved-controller substrate, the guiding-star path chosen over the original sketch below): a runner built with `Runner::with_embodiment` owns an `Embodiment`, a located population of evolved-controller beings. Each tick, after the field step and the body-thermal exchange, a pure comfort-band map (`comfort_fraction`) turns each being's field-driven core temperature into a `TEMPERATURE` homeostatic reserve, per being from its reserved comfort band (Part 20), the being's evolved controller reads the reserve and moves-or-rests, and the beings' new coordinates re-sync `LocationIndex` for the next tick's exchange (`crates/sim/src/runner.rs`, `crates/sim/src/homeostasis.rs::dev_thermal`). The first increment is KINESIS: no directional thermal percept, so an uncomfortable being explores (`Phase::EXPLORE`, no new `Phase`) and directed thermotaxis emerges under survival rather than being authored. The composite `state_hash` folds each being's position, reserves, and controller state after the world fold; proven in `crates/sim/tests/thermal_coupling.rs` (the comfort map is even, a comfortable being rests and an uncomfortable one moves, the controller authors no heading, replay bit-identity and seed divergence, death a full half-band past the set point, and the R-EVOLVE-STEER anti-steering check that the warmth-west and warmth-east advantages match with bit-identical idle baselines). The behaviour source is the evolved controller only; no authored repertoire rides this path (Principle 9).
   - DONE (in-situ thermal selection, the guiding-star retirement of the hand-built fixture): `evolve_thermal` scores a controller by running it through the field-to-behaviour coupling (`Runner::with_embodiment`) in a frozen warm-border, cold-centre field and counting how long it keeps its temperature reserve off the floor. From random controllers, thermal homeostatic-survival selection produces a kinesis (move while cold, rest while warm) that keeps its body in the viable band, retiring the hand-built thermotaxis fixture the coupling increment used: selection produces it. `evolve` was generalized to `evolve_with(layout, params, seed, scorer)` so the scoring environment is data, not hardcoded (Principle 11), with `evolve` the water scorer and `evolve_thermal` the thermal one. Proven in `crates/sim/src/evolve.rs` tests (`thermotaxis_evolves_under_thermal_survival_selection` mean survival 129 to the 200 cap; the scoring field is invariant under a 90-degree rotation, the R-EVOLVE-STEER anti-steering check; a mover outlives an idle being that dies at the cold centre; the scorer is deterministic). No authored heading and no authored objective: survival is what is counted.
   - DONE (directional thermal percept, raw physics, sensed taxis): `Field::gradient_at` is a pure integer central-difference stencil, the raw temperature gradient (the GPU-portable counterpart of `Field::step` and `crates/gpu`'s field kernel); `Runner::step_embodiment` reads it per being and feeds it as the `TEMPERATURE` axis's directional percept through `locomotion::step_with_field_dirs`, an axis-generic per-being field-percept channel (a moisture or wind field plugs in the same way), merged alongside the known-source percept with no controller-layout change. The percept is raw physics (what a thermoreceptor senses), not comfort: no physiology is folded in, and the being's comfort reserve stays a separate input, so the evolved controller combines "am I uncomfortable" with "which way is warmer" and selection wires it. Proven in `crates/sim/src/evolve.rs` and `crates/sim/tests/thermal_coupling.rs`: a smooth rotation-invariant thermal bowl with a balanced set of four off-centre starts (`thermal_sensed_survival`, `evolve_thermal_sensed`); sensed taxis reaches the warm ring from every start (survives to the cap) while undirected kinesis random-walks and often dies (200 vs about 66 to 153); a fixed heading has a directional blind spot the percept-follower does not; the bowl is 90-degree rotation invariant (R-EVOLVE-STEER); directed thermotaxis evolves to near the cap; and `Field::gradient_at` points toward warmer and is flat on a uniform field. Honest limit: raw gradient plus the even comfort reserve lets a linear controller learn warmth-seeking in a cold world, but fleeing lethal heat needs a recurrent controller reading a signed thermoreceptive percept (a warm-versus-cold receptor, a new input channel) so selection can evolve the hot-versus-cold gating. GATE (owner-confirmed): this is deferred and rides in with the medium substrate, since lethal-hot environments (lava, desert) are what the medium work introduces; bidirectional thermotaxis lands under `R-MEDIUM`, not before there is heat to flee.
   - DONE (FieldCalib manifest loader): `FieldCalib::from_manifest` reads `field.diffusion`, `field.relaxation`, and `field.body_exchange` from the calibration manifest, fail-loud if any is still reserved (Principle 11), so a canonical run obtains its field calibrations from the owner's manifest rather than a fabricated default (the three entries ship reserved-with-basis in `calibration/reserved.toml`). Tests in `crates/sim/src/runner.rs`: it reads a set manifest exactly and refuses a reserved one.
   - REMAINING sub-increments, ordered: (a) map-backed terrain (real biomes and elevation) replacing the bounded open plane; (b) fold the being-lifecycle path (`seed_dawn_populations`, enculturate, birth, age, mortality) into the composed tick and the hash; (c) the cognition-`World` coupling (temperature as a percept to the deliberative tier, and a chosen action moving a `Coord3` against a unified `PlaceId`/`LocationIndex`) is DEFERRED behind rebuilding that deliberative tier (Part 8.1) on the evolved substrate, because its current `World::decide` path is the quarantined authored repertoire (Principle 9), not a clean coupling target.
   - OWNER-DIRECTED, the emergent-physiology direction (signed off; the organ abstraction was red-teamed and reframed, see below). First, DERIVE THE HOMEOSTATIC RESERVES FROM ANATOMY. Today reserve capacity scales with `body_mass` and only integrity derives from the per-part body. Mass-scaling is wrong for a huge, mostly-armored creature with few organs (it would be handed reserves it has no internal systems to justify): a being carries a reserve because it bears the organ that maintains it, and reserve size follows the organs, not total mass, so "no organs, no reserves" is expressible and armor and integrity decouple from metabolic reserves. RED-TEAM OUTCOME (owner-steered): the organ's function is NOT an authored tag. The first-cut design gave each organ kind an authored `OrganCategory` (fat-body to Metabolic, gills to Respiratory); red-teamed against Principle 8 that tag is a template, a closed function-per-kind authored one level down. The reframe: an organ is a tissue-composition structure (the exact pattern the body's fluids already use, a composition over the biology floor), and which reserve it backs is DERIVED from its composition (an energy-dense tissue is an energy store, a water-rich one a water store) against the physics-floor material axes (`bio.energy_density`, `bio.water_fraction`, `therm.specific_heat`). We author the floor physics and the tissue-composition vocabulary; the organ's role emerges. The first-cut authored-kind build is set aside for this composition-derived rework. Second, THE MEDIUM SUBSTRATE, generalized so aquatic life is one instance: a medium is a `Substance` in the physics substrate (`crates/physics`, content-addressed, not a label), defined by its physics-axis values (`mech.density`, `fluid.dynamic_viscosity`, `therm.temperature`, and the rest); a per-cell medium field of the GPU-portable stencil shape. The FLOOR TO AUTHOR here is a gas-exchange and respirable-medium physics law the floors do not yet carry (a medium's respirable content, dissolved-gas concentration or partial pressure, and Fick's-law diffusion across a membrane by area, permeability, and gradient), the one new authored piece, tracked as `R-MEDIUM`. Medium affinity is then EMERGENT: a high-surface-area membrane organ in contact with water respires water (a gill), one in contact with air respires air (a lung), from the organ's composition and geometry against that law plus selection, never a hardcoded "aquatic" flag, so a lava creature, a magical-fluid creature, a rooted autotroph drawing from its medium, and a sentient aquatic race all emerge. Full aquatic physiology is the chosen depth: medium, respiration, buoyancy (from body density), in-medium thermal exchange, and amphibious both-medium bands. The bidirectional-thermotaxis gate above rides in here. Both are substantial; the anatomy-derived reserves come first (composition-derived), then the medium substrate on top.
   - DONE (composition-derived anatomy-derived reserves, the first half of the owner-directed item, signed off as "Derived from tissue composition"): a homeostatic reserve's capacity now derives from the being's ORGANS, not its body mass. `anatomy.rs` gains a tissue-composition organ substrate: `TissueComposition` (a value on each biology-floor material axis, `bio.energy_density` and `bio.water_fraction`), `TissueComponent` (the floor-axis vocabulary a reserve reads), and `OrganKindDef` (an organ kind as data: id, name, fantasy gate, and composition, with NO function tag), plus an `organs: Vec<OrganKindDef>` registry, `organ_composition`, and a body-plan organ draw (`pick_organs`) keyed off `base + 100` with no coupling to body mass, covering, or trophic layer (the anti-steering invariant). `homeostasis.rs`: `HomeostaticAxisDef` gains `backing_component: Option<TissueComponent>`, and the canonical `Homeostasis::new(reg, plan, organs)` sets each backed axis's capacity to the development-weighted sum over the being's organs of their composition on that component (a derived, non-backed axis such as integrity or temperature keeps unit capacity). The mass-scaling path is retained only as the labelled `Homeostasis::from_mass` development fallback (fixtures and tests keep running); no production caller sources a reserve from mass. Which reserve an organ backs is DERIVED from its composition against the floor, never a tag (Principle 8): an energy-dense tissue backs energy, a water-rich one water. Proven in `crates/sim/src/homeostasis.rs` and `crates/sim/src/anatomy.rs`: capacity derives from composition; an energy-dense organ backs energy not water; a huge, mostly-armored giant with one tiny organ holds a SMALLER reserve than a small, organ-rich body (the owner's armored-giant case); no organs means no metabolic reserve and non-viability; capacity sums over organs and scales with development; a derived axis holds unit capacity regardless of organs; determinism; and the organ draw is registry-gated, fantasy-gated, and deterministic. The first-cut authored-`OrganCategory` build is retired by this rework. REMAINING on this item: the medium substrate (below), whose `R-MEDIUM` floor adds the respiratory-surface composition component the organ substrate is built to extend.
   - DONE (red-team hardening of the above, merged as #28): a red-team pass found the `TissueComponent` enum was a closed vocabulary sitting where the physics biology floor already models composition as string-keyed data (`Substance::vector`), a Principle 11 seam that capped what reserves could exist without a code change. Hardened: `TissueComposition` is now a `BTreeMap<String, Fixed>` over biology-floor axis ids, `HomeostaticAxisDef.backing_component` is an `Option<String>` floor axis id, and the enum is removed, so a reserve backed by protein or the R-MEDIUM respiratory-surface axis is a pure data edit (proven by a `bio.protein_fraction` test). The line 54 note's `TissueComponent`/`Option<TissueComponent>` is superseded by this floor-axis-keyed form.
   - DONE (the F3 birth-nonviability decision, owner-directed: lean on the existing closure cull, and prove it does not steer). The owner's call on a species whose organ roll gives it no metabolic reserve (born nonviable on energy) is to LEAN ON THE EXISTING CLOSURE CULL rather than add a seed-time viability filter, and to prove that leaning on it steers no outcome. Proven in `crates/sim/tests/biosphere_steering.rs` (Principle 9): the cull is physics-only (the seed-time least-fixed-point `grounded` walk reads only the food web, the runtime Part 15 `Stock` collapse reads only supply and demand, neither reads morphology, shown by a body-swap invariance test and a collapse test); birth-viability (`homeostasis::birth_viable`, a documented query, NOT a generator gate) is a pure function of the organ set, invariant to body mass, armor, and weapons; the armored giant with even one small energy organ survives while only the truly reserveless body is culled; and over 300 generated species the verdict is invariant to the drawn mass forced to each extreme, so the cull selects no mass class, and the culled are exactly those with an empty energy reserve. The birth-nonviability leans on the runtime half: a reserveless creature dies at once, its pool draws no sustaining return, and the existing over-harvest cull collapses it. The end-to-end wiring (reserve-viability feeding the pool persistence) lands with the being-spawn loop in the medium-substrate work; the invariants it must preserve are the ones proven here.
   - APPROVED, R-MEDIUM (owner: "as long as it is emergent on physics kernels, I approve"). The scoped proposal is `docs/working/MEDIUM_SUBSTRATE_SCOPED_PROPOSAL.md` (draft PR #33). The binding condition is emergence on physics kernels: the one new authored piece is a Fick's-law membrane gas-exchange kernel plus a respirable-content medium axis and an ambient-medium field, and medium affinity (a gill respires water, a lung air, a lava creature its lethal-hot medium) is emergent from organ composition against the medium through those kernels, never a flag. This moves the medium substrate (task #20) to the active build; the bidirectional-thermotaxis signed-percept gate rides in with it. Next build increment: the physics floor (the gas-exchange kernel and axes in `crates/physics`) under the emergence constraint, then the ambient-medium field and the respiration reserve (a data extension of the now floor-axis-keyed organ substrate).
   - DONE (R-MEDIUM increment 1, the physics floor, merged as #39): `law.membrane_gas_flux`, Fick's law in the mass-transfer form `J = k*A*(c_medium - c_internal)` (signed: uptake positive, off-gassing negative), plus the `fluid.respirable_content` and `fluid.gas_transfer_coefficient` axes, each reserved-with-basis. The kernel reads only the medium's respirable content, so a gill in water and a lung in air are the same kernel over different concentrations, equilibrium is zero flux, and no exchange happens without a surface (proven in `crates/physics/tests/fluids.rs`).
   - DONE (R-MEDIUM increment 2a, the respiration coupling, the organism side): `crates/sim/src/medium.rs` couples the gas-exchange kernel to a being's physiology. A `RESPIRATION` homeostatic reserve (a unit-capacity oxygen buffer, `dev_respiration`) drains by metabolism and is replenished each tick by `medium::respire`, which reads the being's exchange area (`exchange_area`, the development-weighted sum over its organs of the new `bio.respiratory_surface` biology-floor axis, the same composition-derived shape the metabolic reserves use) and the ambient medium's respirable content, and applies the signed Fick flux via a new `Homeostasis::adjust`. Proven: a gilled being breathes and survives in a rich medium; the same body suffocates in a poor one (outcome from the medium's content, not a label); a body with no respiratory organ suffocates even in the richest medium (the no-surface-no-breath consequence, the respiratory sibling of the F3 no-energy-organ case); a larger surface takes up more; determinism. REMAINING (increment 2b): the per-cell ambient-medium field that supplies each being's medium (the coupling takes it as input now, as the thermal coupling took a Field), buoyancy from body density against the medium (the existing `law.buoyant_force`), and the signed thermoreceptor for lethal-hot media.
   - DONE (R-MEDIUM increment 2b, the ambient-medium field, the world side): `crate::medium::MediumField`, a per-cell medium (respirable content and density) in the row-major layout the temperature field uses, and `medium::respire_at`, the located respiration that reads a being's cell and exchanges gas with it. Proven: a being in a rich cell breathes and survives while the same body in a poor cell suffocates (respiration is located, the medium is the cell's, not a label); off the field there is no medium and a being suffocates; the field reads its medium back and zero off the edge; determinism. The field carries the medium density for the buoyancy increment. STILL REMAINING (increment 2c): buoyancy, which needs a being's body density derived from its tissue composition against `mat.density` (no body density exists yet), against the field's medium density through `law.buoyant_force`; and the signed thermoreceptor for lethal-hot media.
   - DONE (R-MEDIUM increment 2c, buoyancy and amphibious emergence): `medium::body_density` derives a being's density as the development-weighted average over its organs of their `mat.density` composition (the water baseline when none declare one, the first-cut organ-composition proxy), and `medium::buoyancy`/`buoyancy_at` returns the signed net buoyant acceleration through the resolved `law.buoyant_force` and `law.weight` kernels, so the sign is the density difference. Proven: a light body floats and a dense one sinks in water; the same dense body floats on lava and falls in air (buoyancy is the cell's medium, not a label); body density is the composition average; determinism. And the amphibious case is proven emergent: a body whose respiratory organ exchanges in two respirable-rich media is viable in both cells, with no both-medium flag. STILL REMAINING to finish R-MEDIUM (increment 2d, lethal-hot media): in-medium thermal exchange (the medium field carrying a temperature the being's thermal coupling reads) and the signed thermoreceptor (a warm-versus-cold controller input so selection can evolve hot-fleeing), the deferred bidirectional-thermotaxis gate.
   - DONE (R-MEDIUM increment 2d part A, in-medium thermal exchange): `MediumField` now carries a per-cell temperature (the same row-major layout as its respirable content and density), and `medium::in_medium_temperature`/`in_medium_temperature_at` relaxes a being's core temperature toward the medium of its cell, `new = prev + rate * (medium_temp - prev)`, the discrete form of Newton's law of cooling over `Fixed` (checked, cap-on-overflow). Physics in, death out: a body held in a lava-hot medium heats past its comfort band (`runner::comfort_fraction` falls to zero) and a body in a lethal-cold medium cools past it, both lethal, while a temperate medium holds the body in band, with no authored rule that lava is lethal. The anti-steer is proven: the exchange is a scalar relaxation toward the medium temperature carrying no spatial heading, and an equal gap above and below the body drives an equal and opposite step (`a_hot_and_a_cold_medium_are_mirror_image_treatments`: `up == -down`), so the mechanism bakes in no direction (Principle 9). Proven in `crates/sim/src/medium.rs` (19 medium tests): heats toward hot and cools toward cold, equilibrium at the medium temperature, lethal-hot and lethal-cold both kill while temperate holds, the located form reads the cell and holds off the field, determinism. STILL REMAINING to finish R-MEDIUM (increment 2d part B, the deferred bidirectional-thermotaxis gate): the signed thermoreceptor, a raw warm-versus-cold percept delivered as its own controller input (not folded into a "which way to safety" heading, which would be steering), so selection can evolve hot-fleeing under the lethal-hot media this increment makes real.
   - DONE (R-MEDIUM increment 2d part B, the signed thermoreceptor and bidirectional thermotaxis: R-MEDIUM is now COMPLETE): the controller gains a fifth per-axis input, the signed setpoint-deviation percept (`controller.rs` `INPUTS_PER_AXIS` 4 to 5, the general substrate: every homeostatic axis exposes both its even comfort level and its signed deviation, so the mechanism authors no "temperature is special"). The runner supplies it for the TEMPERATURE axis from the new odd `runner::signed_deviation` (too hot positive, too cold negative, saturating at the band edges), threaded through `locomotion::step_with_field_dirs` alongside the gradient percept. It is a raw percept, not a heading: it says the body is too hot, not which way to flee, so the controller must combine it with the gradient itself (Principle 9). The proof (`crates/sim/src/evolve.rs`): a bidirectional scorer scores survival in BOTH a lethal-cold bowl and a lethal-hot bowl (mirror images across the set point, proven cell-for-cell); NECESSITY, seed-robust: no single gradient polarity survives both (the warmth-seeker climbs to the warm rim in the cold bowl but walks into the lethal-hot centre, 200 vs 14 ticks; the heat-fleer the mirror), because telling hot from cold is the bit the even comfort reserve cannot carry; EMERGENCE: from random controllers, homeostatic-survival selection with the signed percept and a recurrent controller produces a being that seeks warmth when cold and flees heat when hot, surviving both bowls to the cap (bi 200), without any heading or hot-versus-cold rule authored; and the percept is LOAD-BEARING by ablation (zeroing only the signed input drops the same evolved controller from 200 to 131). Anti-steer proven throughout: `signed_deviation` is exactly odd about the set point (the signed counterpart of the even `comfort_fraction`), the two bowls are mirror images, and the start sets are balanced, so the mechanism favours neither hot nor cold and no compass direction. Honest limit: the bidirectional gating is a product of two percepts, so it needs the recurrent controller (a reaction norm cannot form it); the reaction norm still cannot solve a both-dangers world. This retires the bidirectional-thermotaxis gate the directed-thermal-percept increment deferred, so full aquatic-and-thermal physiology (medium, respiration, buoyancy, in-medium thermal exchange, amphibious bands, and now heat-fleeing) is emergent on physics kernels with no authored steering. R-MEDIUM is COMPLETE.

Gate for the whole cluster: `ROADMAP.md`'s "stay serial" risk, the moment a phase is parallelised these become live blockers at once.
   - DONE (determinism-cluster on-ramp: `R-HARNESS-COVER` Phase-0, and `R-REDUCE-ORDER` for the two live combines). The sim determinism harness worker sweep was vacuous: it ticked the promoted beings on empty input, so the converse phase emitted no dialogue moves and the `CommandKey` barrier re-ordered an empty set, proving nothing. It now drives the beings with an observation schedule (`crates/sim/tests/determinism_harness.rs`: `seed_observations`, wired through a new additive `Runner::step_with_world_inputs` for the composed sibling), so the converse phase produces a non-empty, thread-scrambled move set (1650 moves in the direct sweep, 1476 in the composed), and a move-count guard (`MIN_EXPECTED_MOVES`) asserts the run can never silently go vacuous again; the widths 1/2/3/8 bit-identity and the move-count width-invariance both hold. Separately, the two live `R-REDUCE-ORDER` combines were analysed rather than rewritten (`crates/sim/tests/reduce_order.rs`) and an adversarial determinism audit corrected one claim. The typology weighted pick is order-independent by construction, pinned by the value-id-sorted walk `TypologyPrior::set` guarantees (value id is the total key that recovers the canonical weight vector from any permutation). The gossip conflict apply is now order-independent: an adversarial audit found the earlier first-writer-wins candidate set made it order-dependent when competing assertions carried different candidate sets (`add_evidence` silently dropped evidence toward a value absent from the frozen `hyps`), so on the owner's north-star call the candidate set is now the sorted UNION of every asserted hypothesis (`InferenceFrame::merge_hyps`, `evidence.rs`), applied in both the first-order belief (`consider`) and the theory-of-mind (`model`) paths. A belief's hypothesis space emerges from what the world asserts rather than from who spoke first, no evidence is dropped by arrival order, and the apply is safe to parallelise. Both R-REDUCE-ORDER sites are order-independent, proven across an arrival-order shuffle (`crates/sim/tests/reduce_order.rs`). Gate unchanged: the full coarse-versus-fine harness proof and the full `R-REDUCE-ORDER` form stay open, and the cluster stays serial until parallelism.
## Tier C: engine fidelity in time and breadth (gated on Tier B)

- **`R-TEMPORAL-LOD`** (site Part 32), the adaptive per-region clock, scoped in `docs/temporal_lod_research.md`. Hard prerequisites, cited: `R-PROJ-REGISTER` (load-bearing), `R-HARNESS-COVER`, `R-GPU-CANON-PIN` (resolved; the fixed-point-sampler primitives are built in `crates/gpu`), and the inter-region order items `R-CMD-ORDER`, `R-REDUCE-ORDER`, `R-SAVE-SCHEMA`.
- **`R-AGENT-EXEC`** (site Part 57), event-driven agent execution, scoped in `docs/event_driven_execution_research.md`. Prerequisites: `R-CMD-ORDER` (built) and the deterministic scheduler (signed off, core built in `crates/core/src/schedule.rs`, and its first real tick integration landed: the runner's tick phases are declared as scheduler systems and run through the serial executor bit-identically to the hand-pinned order (`Runner::step_scheduled`, `Runner::tick_systems`, proven in `crates/sim/tests/determinism_harness.rs`), with the scheduler auto-discovering that the cognition world parallelises with the field phases; the hotter `World::tick` cognition phases are the next surface, then the Rayon executor when profiled). It shares one event-queue substrate with `R-TEMPORAL-LOD`, so the two must be built to a single design.
- **`R-VIEW-ELAB`** (site Part 54), the non-authoritative view elaboration; sits with the level-of-detail foundations and is partly present as the pure-read superfine render.

## Tier D: the made world (Part 60 Stages 6 through 13), the largest new work

Gated on the focus-scale local settlement layer (Part 60 Stage 11), which Part 60 names the keystone and the heaviest single capability, on the scale of Dwarf Fortress's own core loop. The order within this tier follows Part 60: the living world (Stage 6, ecology, climate, economy, geology, with the stocks and biosphere substrate already built), peoples and conflict and deep history (Stage 7), the observation and dramaturg layer (Stage 8), emergent society (Stage 9, institutions and governance and economy already resolved as substrate, plus language drift, magic, combat, and divinity), presentation and modding and adaptive time (Stage 10, which folds in `R-TEMPORAL-LOD`), the local settlement layer (Stage 11), the civilizational physical layer (Stage 12, mechanical power, infrastructure, transport, agriculture), and knowledge and material culture and the social atom (Stage 13).

Content-registry gates that must open for world content to emerge, each a data registry rather than a closed enum (Principle 11), cited to site: `R-EVENT` (Part 7), `R-RELATION` (Part 10), `R-WEATHER` (Part 18), `R-CONTACT` (Part 21), `R-CATASTROPHE` (Part 26), `R-DOMAIN` (Part 38), `R-INFRA` (Part 46), and `R-COMMS` (Part 41).

The gaps-and-holes items ride this tier, several with a buildable half already in code: `R-EMOTION` (transient affect, buildable half in `affect.rs`), `R-SENSORIUM` (channel-gated perception, buildable half in `sensorium.rs`), `R-AGING` (the individual-tier life-process loop built in `world.rs` and now WIRED into `World::tick` as a pinned `life_cadence` sub-phase that ages and rolls mortality on the life-cadence period, per-world overridable, mortality gated on an installed owner hazard, proven to replay bit-for-bit; the canonical period now DERIVES from the world's orbit (`World::from_manifest_with_orbital` over `clock::ticks_from_seconds`, R-CELESTIAL) rather than the hardcoded `LIFE_CADENCE_TICKS`, which is demoted to a labelled dev/test fallback; the pool-tier age distribution and mortality built in `crates/sim/src/demography.rs` (`AgeHistogram`) and adopted into the two-tier world (`lod.rs`: `Pool.ages`, `age_pools`, age-carrying promote/demote, the `age_population` conserved projection), item open pending the age-tracked split rule and wiring the pool-tier demography into the tick), `R-REST`, `R-REPRO` (mate-choice direction researched and recommended emergent, cited in `docs/working/REPRO_MATE_CHOICE_SCOPED_PROPOSAL.md`; the load-bearing claim that direction follows the offspring fitness landscape and the mechanism authors none is proven prototype-in-isolation in `crates/sim/src/mate_choice.rs`, with the genome-derived fitness, the selection loop, the feature-weighted version over both axes (`evolve_featured_preference`), and the `World::birth` choose site (`World::choose_mate`, a per-being heritable preference seeded with unbiased variation and inherited at birth) all built; the shared-`evolve_with` folding and a Dobzhansky-Muller table on the World choose path are the remaining follow-ons; the SEX / BREEDING-SYSTEM substrate and the reproductive census now BUILT (gate: `crates/sim/src/breeding.rs` `SexClass`/`BreedingSystem`/`BreedingSystemRegistry`, a data-driven mating-type registry with dev fixtures for binary anisogamy, N mating types, and hermaphroditism, and the Fisherian `fisher_select_step`; `crates/sim/src/genome.rs` new `Channel::SexDetermination`, so sex is a gene-fed phenotype read through `express()` off a data-chosen locus with no `Phase::SEX_DETERMINE` and no drawn ratio; `crates/sim/src/race.rs` `Race.breeding`; `crates/sim/src/census.rs` `ReproductiveCensus` plus `ReproductiveMoments` and the Ne kernel: Wright 1931 `effective_size_sex` with its k-class harmonic generalization `effective_size_classes`, Crow-Kimura 1970 `effective_size_var`, composed by one race-blind `ReproductiveMoments::effective_size` feeding `GenePool::effective_size`; `crates/sim/src/world.rs` credits the census in `World::birth` and stamps founder sex at the dawn, window-stamped and RNG-free; pool tier via `AgeHistogram::add_births` and `Pool.repro`/`Pool::effective_size`, tier-consistent with the individual census in expectation (record 62.9); tests in `census.rs`, `breeding.rs`, `demography.rs`, and `tests/breeding_census.rs`. Non-steering (Principle 9): two races diverge in Ne only through their census data through the one kernel, swapping the census inputs swaps the Ne, a symmetric census yields N, and a 1:1 sex ratio EMERGES from the sex-determination locus under equal-investment selection rather than being hardcoded, shifting off 1:1 under unequal investment. Manifest: `genome.effective_population_size` RE-SCOPED to the pre-dawn founder seed (the canonical Ne now derives from the census), the value kept as the world-dialing lever. Remaining: reset the census window onto the generation cadence and route mate compatibility through `World::choose_mate`), `R-CHILDHOOD`, `R-JUSTICE`, `R-LIVELINESS`, `R-TECTONICS`.

## Tier E: the north star (Part 60 Stage 14; Parts 41, 61), the far horizon

The emergent technology design space, gated on the made world (Stages 11 through 13) and the physics substrate being in place. Its first gate is the one still-unimplemented test in the whole workspace: `convergence_without_a_target_is_forced_by_physics` (`crates/sim/tests/steering.rs`, an ignored placeholder whose own guard says the subject "does not exist yet"). Stage 14 must first prove convergence without a target, two isolated cultures reaching the same physical attractor from different seeds, with the convergence explained by physics and not authored bias, checked by the steering audit.

The `R-DEEPTECH` cluster: composition is resolved (`R-DEEPTECH-COMPOSE`, 62.10); the four deeper questions remain open and are, by the owner's standing instruction, to be taken super-deep when reached rather than scoped down now: `R-DEEPTECH-SCIENCE`, `R-DEEPTECH-PHYSICS`, `R-DEEPTECH-DEPTH`, and `R-DEEPTECH-SCALE` (sites Parts 41 and 61). The new steering item `R-EVOLVE-STEER` (site Part 8.4, flagged this session) rides here as well, since the pool-tier controller-evolution wiring it constrains is itself gated on the quantitative genome tier (25.10) and temporal level of detail (Part 32).

## Cross-cutting gates (true at every tier)

- **Owner calibration.** Eighty-two reserved values remain fail-loud. Nothing that runs a real world, as opposed to a dev-fixture test, is unblocked until the values on its path are set. This is the most pervasive gate in the project.
- **Stay serial.** Every determinism item in Tier B is dormant only while the tick is a single stream. The first parallelised phase makes the whole cluster a live blocker at once.
- **Tier consistency.** Any kernel that runs on both a promoted individual and a pool representative (the axiom kernel, the controller expression) must run identically on both, the invariant `R-TIER-CONSIST` guarantees and `R-PROJ-REGISTER` extends.

## What I recommend you sign off on

The order above is my synthesis of the consensus. The one genuine fork worth your explicit call is the head of Tier B: whether the immediate next work is (a) owner calibration so a real world can run, (b) wiring the cognition tick into the canonical runner so the built core drives a world at all, or (c) the determinism cluster so the world can later parallelise and persist. My recommendation is (b) then (a) then (c): make the built core run under the canonical runner first, calibrate against it, and hold the determinism cluster until just before parallelism, since the serial tick already replays bit for bit. The three consolidation debts (`R-CMD-ORDER`, `R-LANG-TYPOLOGY`, and the canonical-walk and reduce helpers) and the stale `ROADMAP.md` "Where we are" section are bookkeeping to reconcile whenever convenient, not blockers.

## Reserved-value derive-from-fundamentals audit (2026-07-03, applied)

Gate: the derive-vs-fundamentals audit of the full calibration manifest (`docs/working/RESERVED_VALUES_WORKSHEET.md` §13 through §17), applied to `calibration/reserved.toml` on `claude/reserved-values-consolidation`. Seventeen HIGH human/terran steers were found among graduated values; eight reverted set to reserved (fail-loud derive sentinels), five kept set with a flagged basis (hard readers or dial bases), twelve still-reserved steers de-anchored in basis. The manifest moved 76 set to 68 set of 153. The derivations themselves (h² readout, field diffusivity from thermal axes, damage caps from floor maxima, the behaviour-controller scalings, the ToM single-source-of-truth aliases, per-pair projection loss, enculturation from belief plasticity, the genome law constants) are the buildable-today implementation batch now in design; the blocked ones await their prerequisite build (the metabolic-rate kernel and body-surface-area axis, the edibility `ResourceField` composition, the parse-cost and attenuation laws, tier-consistency, the per-race maturation and memory datum).

R-CELESTIAL orbital elements: BUILT (gate: `crates/world/src/celestial.rs` `OrbitalElements` plus `crates/sim/src/clock.rs` `ticks_from_seconds`, `orbital_from_manifest`, `base_tick_seconds_fixed`; tests in `clock.rs`, `genesis.rs`, `world.rs`). A world's year and day are now fixed-point world-seconds carried through `GenesisParams`/`LivingWorld` (folded into `LivingWorld::state_hash` at a pinned position) and read from two new reserved scalars `world.orbital_period_seconds` and `world.rotation_period_seconds` (owner-set per world, fail-loud; Earth is the labelled `OrbitalElements::dev_earth` fixture, one option among many). The canonical life-cadence now derives as `ticks_from_seconds(orbital_period_seconds, time.base_tick_seconds)` in `World::from_manifest_with_orbital` rather than the hardcoded 31,536,000, with `LIFE_CADENCE_TICKS` demoted to a labelled dev/test fallback. The maturation half of `language.generation_ticks` (`Race::maturity_years` times the orbital year in ticks) is now BUILT (Wave-2 derive build-out below): `Language` carries its race, `World::drift_languages` derives each lineage's drift cadence as `race.maturity_years * World::life_cadence_ticks()`, and the `language.generation_ticks` scalar is RETIRED.

R-AXIOM evidence-ring capacity: BUILT (gate: `crates/sim/src/axiom.rs` `RingCapacityLaw::capacity_for` and `::from_manifest`, `crates/sim/src/calibration.rs` `require_curve`, wired at the dawn and at birth in `crates/sim/src/world.rs`; tests in `axiom.rs`, `calibration.rs`, `dawn_seed.rs`, `birth.rs`, `inheritance.rs`). The evidence-ring capacity now DERIVES per being from its own expressed `Mind.memory` through a reserved memory-to-slots curve (curve read, round half-up, clamp to a reserved hard ceiling), read by the same `Curve` mechanism the entrenchment gate uses. This supersedes the interim `ring_capacity_from_memory` (a `to_int`-clamped linear form, worksheet §13b), whose two-point case the curve reproduces. The single reserved `axiom.evidence_ring_capacity` is retired and split into `axiom.evidence_ring_curve` (the memory-phenotype-to-slots map, Miller's 7 plus or minus 2 kept only as a candidate point on the curve) and `axiom.evidence_ring_hard_cap` (the per-tick and per-save state-hash and replay budget), both reserved-with-basis (the manifest moved to 154 entries). The birth path is reordered so the child's genome and mind are expressed before its beliefs are inherited, fixing a bug that copied the first parent's ring cap onto the child regardless of the child's own recombined memory; the non-steering test (`dawn_seed.rs`) proves two races diverge in ring capacity purely from their memory-gene data through the one law, with no `RaceId` branch (Principle 9).

Maturation-datum: BUILT (gate: `crates/sim/src/race.rs` `lifespan_years`/`maturity_years` + `maturation_fraction`/`life_fraction`/`is_mature`; `crates/sim/src/world.rs` `race_of` map + `apply_mortality_by_race`; tests in `race.rs`/`life_stage.rs`). Adds the per-race maturation data the blocked steer-derivations (`plasticity_by_age`, `maturity_targets`, `l2_acquisition`) read, restores the missing per-being `StableId`-to-`RaceId` map so it is reachable, and makes mortality read a race-normalized `life_fraction` so one shared hazard curve means the same for an 80-year and a 700-year race. Non-steering: two races diverge in maturity and mortality purely from their data through the identical code path.

Edibility-composition: BUILT (gate: `crates/sim/src/edibility.rs` axis-id-keyed `Composition`/`Physiology` + the `net_nutrition` argument-order fix; `crates/sim/src/locomotion.rs` `ResourceField` per-tile `matter` + ingest derived from `laws::satisfaction`). Ingest now derives from the tile's measured composition against each walker's own physiology, retiring the flat `physiology.intake_yield` (tombstoned). Fixes a live bug (net_nutrition was always 1.0) and a Principle-11 fabricated-index defect (positional vectors re-keyed to biology-floor axis ids). Non-steering: two physiologies diverge on one identical tile, no race branch.

Env-variance: BUILT (gate: `crates/core/src/keys.rs` `Phase::DEVELOPMENT` 0x16; `crates/sim/src/race.rs` `environment_variance`; `crates/sim/src/world.rs` `env_offset`; tests in `development_env.rs`). A mean-zero symmetric per-being developmental offset makes `express()` vary per individual, so V_E is positive across a cohort and the phenotype variance exceeds the genotypic variance (V_P > V_A, h² < 1), the environmental half of narrow-sense heritability. The new reserved `genome.environment_variance` is fail-loud, and `Fixed::ZERO` reproduces today's homogeneous world bit-for-bit. Non-steering: V_E widens each race's spread without eroding the between-race difference; mean-preserving. Pairs with the still-walled breeding-value tier (V_A half) to fully derive `narrow_sense_heritability`.

Breeding-value tier: BUILT (gate: `crates/core/src/gauss.rs` `GaussApprox`/`gaussian_unit`/`gaussian`, exported in `crates/core/src/lib.rs`, tests in `crates/core/tests/gauss.rs`; `crates/sim/src/genome.rs` `GenePool` per-locus `effects` plus stamped `gauss`, `additive_variance`, `narrow_sense_heritability`, `hash_into`, the rewritten `promote`/`demote`/`found`, and `GeneticScheme.additive_mutation_step`/`gauss` with the `gamete` continuous step at `SLOT_MUTATE_STEP`; tests in `crates/sim/tests/breeding_value.rs`). On the owner's three stamped decisions: the integer-Gaussian is sum-of-uniforms at k=12 (the unit-variance scale `sqrt(12/k)` is exactly one, tails bounded to +/- 6, an honest limit), the `GenePool` representation carries per-locus additive effects alpha_i, and `narrow_sense_heritability` GRADUATES from an authored constant to the derived read `V_A/(V_A+V_E)` with V_A = `additive_variance()` = sum `2*p*(1-p)*alpha^2` and V_E = `genome.environment_variance`. A promoted individual now carries a continuous additive spine: per locus the pool's additive mean plus a mean-zero within-locus deviation scaled to the locus additive std `sqrt(2p(1-p))|alpha|` (one `Fixed::sqrt` per locus, never in a sub-draw loop), drawn on a slot distinct from the state draw; across a cohort its variance reconstructs `additive_variance()` (tier consistency, `R-TIER-CONSIST`), while its mean matches the pool so promote-then-demote is unbiased (the `2Ne`-weighted additive-mean fold in `demote`). The continuous mutation step (`GeneticScheme.additive_mutation_step`, reserved `genome.additive_mutation_step`, fail-loud) is the sole lever that grows the additive variance; a zero step freezes the spine. Locked representation: `effects` and the stamped `gauss` are folded into `GenePool::hash_into`, so the change is visible in identity. Manifest: `genome.gauss_approx` SET to `SumOfUniforms{k=12}` (a world-identity measure re-rolling every quantitative lineage if changed); `genome.additive_mutation_step` added reserved fail-loud; `genome.narrow_sense_heritability` and `being.heritable_fraction` retired to tombstones (they now derive; the effect vector alpha_i is per-race genome data, dev fixtures, never a manifest scalar). Non-steering (Principle 9, `breeding_value.rs`): two pools with identical frequencies and Ne but different alpha vectors (A dense small, B few large) diverge in V_A, heritability, and promoted spread; a relabelling swaps the outputs identically; a same-alpha, different-id case gives identical V_A; the kernels are race-blind and key off the effect data alone. The V_A==V_E case gives exactly one half (the human twin-study midpoint) as an emergent consequence, not an input. Consistency: `evolve::mutate` (behaviour-controller step) and `axiom::inherit_seed` (axiom-seed mutation, via the `world.rs` caller) now draw the same `core::gaussian_unit` k=12 primitive in place of their former bounded-uniform steps, keeping their existing keys; two seed-tuned property tests were re-tuned to the new deterministic trajectory (the thermotaxis dev-fixture seed `0x1234` to `0x1007`, the axiom mutation-bound assertion to the Gaussian +/- 6-std tail). Deferred as before: the infinitesimal segregation noise on gamete formation, multi-allele loci, the large-Ne Wright-Fisher approximation, and the distance-measure and speciation calibrations.

Technique-transmission: BUILT (gate: `crates/sim/src/transmission.rs` `Knowledge`/`TransmissionParams`, the transmit/erode/`is_stabilised` laws; `crates/core/src/keys.rs` `Phase::TRANSMIT` 0x17 and `Phase::KNOW_LOSS` 0x18; tests in `transmission.rs`). A knowledge-transmission substrate over an OPAQUE content-addressed `DesignId = u64` (never an authored Technique enum, the generalization catch that dissolves half of the Part 23/41 inconsistency structurally), with a copy-drift transmit law whose fidelity is a FUNCTION of the copier's per-race memory and perception (never an authored per-race table) and a below-floor erosion-and-cull loss law with free rediscovery. Exposes the reserved `transmission.drift_rate`, `transmission.loss_rate`, and `transmission.loss_practitioner_floor`, from which `compose.transmission_stability` now derives set-equal (`stability_span := ceil(ONE/loss_rate)`, `drift_similarity_radius := 2*drift_rate`, a local proficiency-convergence metric until the Part 41 evaluator's morphospace metric lands). Non-steering: a fidelity-swap dual invariant proves the outcome keys off derived per-race data, not race identity. The holder-count conserved projection is deferred (Knowledge is not attached to the tier boundary yet).

Trace-kind + race-base-rate substrate: BUILT (gate: `crates/sim/src/trace.rs` `TraceKindRegistry`/`TraceKindDef`/`DecayLaw` and the derivations `mortality_implication_weight`, `organic_salience`, `corroding_salience`; `crates/sim/src/base_rates.rs` `RaceBaseRateRegistry`/`RaceBaseRates`; `crates/sim/src/absence.rs` `absence_window`/`characteristic_lifespan`; `crates/sim/src/evidence.rs` `good_weight`; tests in each of those modules). Three authored evidence numbers now DERIVE through cited primitives. `evidence.implication_weights` retires: a trace's belief weight is I.J. Good's weight of evidence `good_weight` (ln P(E|H) - ln P(E|not H)) over the trace kind's own reliability and the race's own natural-mortality base rate, so a high-background-mortality race finds a corpse less diagnostic. `evidence.trace_decay_curves` retires: a trace's salience decays through the physics reaction kernel (thermal-activation gate) and `Fixed::exp` for organic remains scaled by the race's `decay_multiplier`, and through the physics corrosion kernel integrated over elapsed time for corroding traces. `evidence.absence_windows` retires: the presumed-dead window derives from the race's visibility, capped at `characteristic_lifespan` of the race's own hazard (a `LIFESPAN_HAZARD_THRESHOLD` percentile convention, not an authored biology value). The reserved inputs (per-kind reliability and `DecayLaw` parameters, per-race visibility and `decay_multiplier`, universal absence-stage multipliers) live as typed data on the registries (labelled dev fixtures), not manifest entries; the manifest drops three sentinels. Non-steering (Principle 9, swap-tested): the higher-background-mortality race gets the strictly lower implication weight, the lower-visibility race the strictly longer absence window, and the more corrosion-prone kind the strictly faster decay, each swapping when the data swaps, with a static check that no derivation branches on a `RaceId`/`TraceKindId` literal. `DecayLaw` is a CLOSED enum over the fixed physics kernels (an owner call, leaning enum since `physics::laws` is itself a fixed hand-authored kernel set); it is flagged in the type doc. Two integrations are deferred as named follow-ons and NOT done here: the global `World::mortality_hazard`/`apply_mortality` path is untouched (the two mortality sources are not yet unified), and the public `Trace` struct is untouched (no time-varying salience field, no `created_tick` sweep, no `PlaceId`-to-temperature wiring); the derivations are pure and standalone so the build stays additive.

R-METABOLIZE (derived resting metabolism and body-to-medium exchange): BUILT (gate: `crates/physics/src/laws.rs` `basal_metabolic_rate`/`resting_heat_loss`/`metabolic_drain_fraction`; `crates/physics/data/biology_floor.toml` new `bio.convective_surface` axis; `crates/sim/src/physiology.rs` (new) `whole_body_surface`/`whole_body_specific_heat`/`whole_body_energy_density`/`derive_base_drain`/`derive_exertion_coupling`/`derive_body_exchange_rate`/`MetabolicAnchors`; `crates/sim/src/homeostasis.rs` `DerivedDrain`/`metabolize_derived`; `crates/sim/src/runner.rs` per-being `body_exchange_rate` map + `set_body_exchange_rate`, `phase_body_exchange` rewired; tests in `laws.rs`, `physiology.rs`, `homeostasis.rs`, `runner.rs`, and `crates/sim/tests/metabolism_steering.rs`; closes the worksheet §102 blocked-on-the-metabolic-kernel derivation). Three authored scalars now DERIVE from a body's mass and tissue against the physics. `physiology.base_metabolic_drain` retires to a DERIVE sentinel: the resting drain is Kleiber's law `P = a*m^(3/4)` (`basal_metabolic_rate`, the exponent an authored universal physics affordance per West/Brown/Enquist, evaluated by the EXACT two-square-root fixed-point identity `m^(3/4) = sqrt(m*sqrt(m))` so no exp/ln is touched) plus the resolved convective and radiant thermoregulatory heat loss over the whole-body `bio.convective_surface` (`resting_heat_loss` reusing `convective_flux` + `radiant_emission`), bridged to a fraction of the reserve's stored energy (`metabolic_drain_fraction`). `physiology.exertion_drain_coupling` retires: the exertion drain derives from the mechanical work power `laws::power(force*velocity)`, scaled per tick by the being's exertion in the new `Homeostasis::metabolize_derived` (the scalar-field `metabolize` kept as the fixture path). `field.body_exchange` becomes a per-being derived rate `h*A/(m*c)` (`derive_body_exchange_rate`: `h` the medium coefficient, `A` the whole-body convective surface, `m*c` the body's thermal mass over `therm.specific_heat`), the runner using the derived per-being rate when supplied and the `FieldCalib.exchange` scalar only as a labelled fixture-fallback for a being placed without a body. New owner anchors, all reserved fail-loud with basis: `metabolism.kleiber_coefficient` (the coefficient a), `metabolism.body_mass_kg_scale` (the normalized-body-mass-to-kilograms R-UNITS-PIN bridge, NOT derivable), `metabolism.medium_convective_coefficient` (h), plus `metabolism.surface_emissivity` and `metabolism.stefan_boltzmann` for the radiant term. Determinism: the two-sqrt path is exact, the whole-body reads sum organs order-independently (`saturating_add`), `metabolize_derived` walks `reg.axes` canonically and `phase_body_exchange` walks `body_temp` in `StableId` order. Non-steering (Principle 9, `metabolism_steering.rs`): a large low-surface energy-dense body and a small high-surface water-rich body diverge in derived base drain and body-exchange rate from composition and mass alone; a hot-set-point body in a cold medium and its mirror diverge in derived drain from temperature alone; identical physics derive identical results and replay bit-for-bit; and a static source scan proves the kernels read no `RaceId`. Larger-body-drains-a-smaller-fraction is proven (basal grows as `m^(3/4)` while the reserve grows with size, the Kleiber signature). Honest limits: the exact kJ/g-to-joule reconciliation of the reserve's stored energy is the R-UNITS-PIN owner units bridge (the mechanism derives, the absolute scale is the owner anchors); the base drain (watts) and exertion drain (`laws::power` kilowatts) live on different power scales pending the same bridge; and, TIER-CONSISTENCY, the base drain is NONLINEAR in mass (`m^(3/4)`) and temperature (`T^4`), so a pool-tier drain over a size distribution is NOT the drain of the mean size (a Jensen gap), the honest cross-tier difference `docs/design.md:2803` already declares for a nonlinear law output over additive quantities, with an R-TIER-CONSIST reconciliation (a size-distribution moment or an accepted honest gap) named as the follow-on.

R-LANGMOD-PERCEPTUAL-GEOMETRY (perceptual geometry derives from channel physics): BUILT (gate: `crates/physics/src/laws.rs` `acoustic_absorption`/`tube_resonance` and the `F_ABS_MAX` overflow ceiling; `crates/physics/src/graph.rs` two `KernelContract` arms; `crates/physics/data/fluids_floor.toml` new `acoustic.absorption_reference`/`acoustic.resonator_length`/`acoustic.formant_frequency` axes and `law.acoustic_absorption`/`law.tube_resonance`; `crates/sim/src/langmod.rs` (new) `perceptual_geometry`/`PerceptualGeometry`/`PerceptualParams`; tests in `crates/physics/tests/fluids.rs` and `crates/sim/src/langmod.rs`; re-bases `calibration/reserved.toml` `langmod.perceptual_geometry`). Two authored universal physics affordances land on the fluids floor (Principle 9 permits authored physics): thermoviscous frequency-squared absorption `alpha = reference*f^2` (Stokes), overflow-staged as `reference*f` then `*f` (the poiseuille grow/shrink discipline) with a frequency past the `sqrt(2^31)` ceiling routed to the cap; and quarter-wave closed-open tube resonance `f_n = (2n-1)*c/(4L)` (the source-filter formant model), staged `c/L` first so the large intermediate never forms, a near-zero length routed to the cap and a zero sound speed to zero. Both report the linear indicator (alpha, alpha*path through the EXISTING `optical_depth`), deferring the exp transform, and both are pure closed-form `Fixed`, caller-cap-passed, and total on adversarial inputs. DEVIATION from the task sketch, on a codebase-grounded audit: the task proposed Asserted `KernelContract` arms, but both monomials CLOSE over integer exponents (`reference^1 * frequency^2` reduces to the absorption coefficient `1/m` once the reference carries its true residual dimension `1/(m*Hz^2)`; `c^1 * L^-1` reduces to a frequency), so under the closed-monomial discipline `graph.rs` states (Asserted is "never a lazy skip of a checkable monomial", and the explicit-rate pass made poiseuille a verified Monomial for exactly this reason) both are Monomial, dimensionally VERIFIED at load rather than waived (speed_of_sound stays Asserted because its square root halves the exponents to non-integers, the honest Asserted case). The three new floor axes are surfaced RESERVED-with-basis (cited acoustics envelopes: Kinsler, Fant, Stevens), the owner's to set, never fabricated; the absorption reference's sub-epsilon SI envelope reserves a per-quantity windowed scale (R-UNITS-PIN). The sim-side `langmod::perceptual_geometry` DERIVES the per-modality confusability table: per feature value a resonator length maps to a formant vector via `tube_resonance`, pairwise formant distances are weighted by `acoustic_absorption` over a typical path (through `optical_depth`) and by the being's sensorium per-channel just-noticeable difference (the channel gate: a being blind to the channel derives nothing), and the medium-blind contrast budget is the usable-span-over-just-noticeable-difference. `langmod.perceptual_geometry` is re-based off the human auditory dispersion target to derive through this. NON-STEERING RESULT (Principle 9, proven both floors): the SAME resonator lengths in two real media (air c ~340, water c ~1480, each c from `speed_of_sound` over its floor bulk modulus and density) give two DIFFERENT formant vectors and two different confusability tables, with no authored per-race table and no `RaceId` (the function takes none); the equal-capacity invariant holds (medium B at twice the sound speed and twice the just-noticeable difference shares A's contrast budget though its confusable pairs differ, because frequency-squared absorption blurs high formants more, so a physics difference does not force a richness difference). Honest limit: the raw-`Fixed` kernel path works in a representable scale, so the true sub-epsilon SI absorption reference is exercised through a scale-bridged value in tests and its exact bridge is the reserved R-UNITS-PIN anchor; the read-out models the acoustic modality (the manual and chromatic modalities plug in the same shape once their channel-physics laws land).

R-LANG-TYPOLOGY word-order harmony tilt (derived from parse cost): BUILT (gate: `crates/physics/src/laws.rs` `parse_cost`/`harmony_tilt` plus their unit tests; `crates/sim/src/typology.rs` `linearization_domain`/`derived_tilt`/`grammar_parse_cost`/`TiltParams`, the `HarmonyBias.structural_weight` field replacing `weight`, the rewired `tilted_weights`/`sample_profile`, and the `TypologyParams` temperature read; `crates/sim/src/language.rs` new `Linearization` enum and `ProductionModalityDef.linearization` field; tests in `laws.rs`, `typology.rs`, and `crates/sim/tests/reduce_order.rs`; retires `calibration/reserved.toml` `lang.typology_harmony_strong`/`lang.typology_harmony_weak` to tombstones and adds `lang.typology_temperature`). The authored WALS/Dryer harmony tilts stop being numbers and become DATA plus one derivation. On the owner's SPLIT: a direction-NEUTRAL processing-cost floor lands in `laws.rs` (`parse_cost(domain_extent, memory_capacity, cost_max)`, the Hawkins 1983/2004 dependency-integration cost as the integer-Hill saturating form `extent/(extent+memory)` scaled by the cap, softened by working memory; `harmony_tilt(cost_reduction, temperature, tilt_max)`, the softmax weight `exp(cost_reduction/temperature)` floored at one and saturating at the cap through the canon-pinned deterministic `Fixed::exp`), and the branching-consistency mapping lives in `typology.rs`. Both kernels are LABEL-BLIND and DIRECTION-BLIND: they read only a scalar extent and a scalar reduction, never a word-order value, so they author no attractor (Principle 9). The `HarmonyBias` row now carries a data-defined `structural_weight` (how many linearization decisions the pairing constrains: the two-sided fully-phrasal adposition and relative-clause pairs get 2, the one-sided partly-non-phrasal genitive pair gets 1, grounded in Dryer's Branching Direction Theory), so strong-vs-weak is DATA and the tilt DERIVES: `derived_tilt` folds the firing rows' structural weights by the order-independent `Fixed::saturating_sum`, runs the folded extent through `parse_cost` then `harmony_tilt`, and `tilted_weights` multiplies the prior count by that derived tilt in place of the retired constant. The single reserved manifest entry is now the softmax `lang.typology_temperature` (the two tier tilts tombstoned; the disharmony gate kept). NON-STEERING RESULT (Principle 9, proven): two races identical but for a permutation swapping which adposition value id is head-initial produce an IDENTICAL derived tilt, an IDENTICAL grammar parse cost, and an IDENTICAL (exact, weight-over-total) sampled harmonic proportion, with the non-permuted parameters drawing bit-identically and the empirical proportions matching within tolerance; the DIVERGENT-MODALITY test shows a `Simultaneous` modality suppresses the tilt to the untilted marginal (about 0.49 postpositions given OV) while the `Sequential` one shows a strong tilt (about 0.96), the two grammars diverging; a per-race test shows a larger working memory softens the parse cost and weakens (never removes) the harmony pressure; and the sampler replays bit-for-bit across repeats and call order (observer independence, identical at every LOD tier). HUMAN-DATA-ROW gate (validation): with the single dev-fixture temperature at the human calibration (and the human race's working memory), the sampled harmonic proportion reconstructs WALS 95A on the adposition axis (about 0.96, in the 94 to 97 percent band) and Dryer 1992 on the OV genitive side (about 0.89), proving the one free scale is validated AGAINST the human row rather than authored as the tiers. DEVIATIONS, surfaced: (1) `cost_max` is passed as `ONE` so `parse_cost` reports a normalized cost FRACTION and the temperature is the single free scale (no second magnitude hides in the cap); (2) the genitive VO side sits at the WALS-language-count marginal (about 0.55), not Dryer's genera-based 0.45, since the one-sided bias does not tilt that side, the model's honest one-sided prediction stated in the test and the temperature basis; (3) `sample_profile` takes `#[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]` at nine args (substrate, calibration, modality flag, draw coordinate), the same `#[allow]` the `laws.rs` kernels take; (4) `grammar_parse_cost` was added as a companion pub fn so the grammar-scope monotonicity test (a harmonic grammar costs strictly less than a mixed one) runs the real code path; (5) the direction-neutrality is exact at the proportion and weight level, while individual per-draw picks differ because the cumulative walk is value-id-ordered, so the test asserts the exact tilted proportion and derived tilt and grammar-cost identity plus a Monte-Carlo cross-check. Determinism: pure `Fixed` kernels, canon-pinned `exp`, checked-and-capped arithmetic, order-independent folds, no new `DrawKey` (only the weights fed to the existing keyed walk change), and the modality gate a deterministic conditional on the data flag.
