Belief facet-strength + prevailing-belief substrate (the Part 54 belief lift/restrict operator): BUILT (gate: `crates/sim/src/belief.rs` `FacetStrength`/`BeliefKey`/`PrevailingBelief`/`BeliefPool`/`BeliefParams` and the `instantiate_strength` lift, the `advance_diffusion`/`lift_one`/`lift_cohort`/`fold_one`/`fold_back` operators; `crates/core/src/keys.rs` `Phase::BELIEF_LIFT` 0x19; `crates/sim/src/evidence.rs` `aggregate_diffusion_rate`; `crates/sim/src/lod.rs` the `BeliefPool` on `Pool`, the `Vec<(BeliefKey, FacetStrength)>` on `Individual`, `promote_lifting`, the belief restriction folded into `demote`, `belief_mass`, and the belief folding in `state_hash`; `crates/sim/tests/invariants.rs` the `aggregate_belief_mass` projection with the round-trip and leak tests; tests in `belief.rs`, `keys.rs`, `invariants.rs`). The belief keystone deferred from the evidence work (design.md Part 54) lands on the owner's decision: a prevailing belief carries an INTENSIVE `knowledge_level` (a `Fixed` in `[0,1]`, the derived mean conviction) and an EXTENSIVE belief `mass` (the raw Q32.32 bit-sum of member facet strengths, an exact-associative `i128` like `total_wealth` at `lod.rs`), reconciling the Part 9.14 integer diffusion with the Part 54 monotone fixed-point curve and plugging into the conserved-projection registry. Lifting (`promote_lifting`) mints each promoting mind's facet strength from the pool level through the reserved monotone curve plus a counter-keyed per-mind dispersion (keyed on being, belief-content hash, tick, and `Phase::BELIEF_LIFT`), subtracting exactly the minted bits; restriction (`demote`) folds the id-ordered strengths back by adding exactly their bits, so total belief mass is conserved BOTH directions by construction and registers alongside population and wealth. CONTENT-BLIND (Principle 9, proven): the diffusion and the lift key on no belief's identity, so two beliefs differing only in their `BeliefKey` diffuse and lift identically and a permutation of belief ids leaves belief-mass conservation and the canonical state hash invariant; two races diverge only through their per-race curve DATA, a pure function of the curve, with no belief-kind branch. HONEST LIMIT, documented: because the curve may be nonlinear and the dispersion is a finite sample, the intensive level drifts slightly on a lift while the extensive mass stays exact; that the population mean reconstructs the pool level within a fixed-point tolerance is a CALIBRATION TARGET on the curve and dispersion (proven within 0.01 on the identity-curve fixture), not a mechanism-enforced identity, the deliberately-lossy lift direction of Part 54 corrected on the next re-summarize. Determinism: mass is a raw i128 bit-sum (exact, associative), the dispersion draw is bit-identical and independent of cohort iteration order, and the fold-back mean is order-independent; any level-to-mass remainder rides the existing lowest-id rule (`tier.partition_remainder_rule`). R-DEEPTECH-COMPOSE (the Part 41 technology-composition evaluator): BUILT (gate: a NEW crate `crates/compose` (`civsim-compose`), depending only on `civsim-core` and `civsim-physics` and added to the workspace members and default-members; `crates/sim` now depends on it. Modules `interval.rs` (the fixed-point `Interval` with saturating, bound-propagating `Add`/`Sub`/`Mul` and `min_with`), `form.rs` (the FORM/JOIN floor: `FormRegistry`/`FormId` over the wave-1 geometric axes `mech.contact_area`/`section_modulus`/`arm_length`/`edge_radius` and `JoinRegistry`/`JoinId`, labelled dev seeds), `node.rs` (`CompositionNode`/`NodeBody::Leaf`/`::Composite`/`ComponentRef`/`IntentRef` with a PURE-CONTENT `content_id`), `interface.rs` (the open `InterfaceRegistry` of `InterfaceAxisDef` bound to physics axes with `Direction` and role, the fixed-width `PortVector`), `combinator.rs` (the `CombinatorRegistry` keyed by topology, dev-seeded with the four kernels `LimitingMin`/`SaturatingSum`/`ConservedBudget`/`EfficiencyProduct`), `proxy.rs` (the open `ProxyRegistry` of closed-form whole-system proxies plus `ProxyWeights`), `eval.rs` (`evaluate_node`/`evaluate_uncached`/`Memo`/`NodeEval`/`PenaltyCurve`/`EvalParams`), `promote.rs` (the three-gate `promote`/`promoted_library`); tests in `crates/compose/tests/evaluator.rs` (15) plus the fmt/clippy gates; re-bases `calibration/reserved.toml` `compose.viability_threshold`, `compose.interface_penalty_curve`, `compose.emergent_proxy_weights`). The Part 41 evaluator is the EMERGENT side of the technology substrate, kept in its own crate OUTSIDE `crates/physics` on purpose (Principle 9, the authored-physics boundary made a crate boundary): nothing in physics depends on compose, and the kernel path takes only `Fixed`, never a material or race id. A leaf runs the physics law kernels (`bend_stress`, `fracture_onset`) over form geometry and a material `Substance` vector through an axis-presence dispatch; a composite recurses (children resolved by content id from the `Memo` store, cache-keyed by that id), folds child vectors by each interface axis's combinator, applies the proxies, and charges a graded interface-mismatch penalty through a `decision::Curve`-shaped `PenaltyCurve` (graded inside the adaptable range, FLOORED beyond, so a mismatch is softened by an emergent adapter rather than hard-rejected). Three of the six `compose.*` values now route through the evaluator: `compose.viability_threshold` DERIVES to the physics collapse boundary (viability is a DIMENSIONLESS safety fraction `1 - utilization`, so the boundary is a safety of ZERO, defined by the material's own yield and fracture data; only an owner safety factor above zero stays reserved-with-basis); `compose.interface_penalty_curve` is reserved-with-basis THROUGH the evaluator (the adaptable range derives from the interface axis's physics range width, the penalty depths reserved); `compose.emergent_proxy_weights` is reserved-with-basis THROUGH the evaluator (the proxy membership is data, each proxy's criticality weight reserved and FAIL-LOUD at `Memo::new`); `compose.transmission_stability` already derives set-equal to the transmission substrate rates (unchanged). NON-STEERING RESULT (Principle 9, proven): the SAME structural design (identical form, join, and PortVector contract) over two materials with divergent physics (a hard-brittle stone, high strength and low toughness, versus a tough-ductile bronze) DIVERGES in viability and aggregated vector purely from the material vectors, with the stone winning the stress margin and the bronze the toughness margin (neither dominates), and the kernel path taking no id (a relabelled substance with identical physics evaluates identically). NON-TEMPLATEDNESS (Principle 8): two peoples with different interface substrates (one exposing an exotic stiffness-resonance axis) get DIFFERENT promoted-library shapes under ONE physics (the exotic people's resonance proxy rejects a heavy design the base people promote). MEMOISATION: evaluate-with-cache equals evaluate-without-cache bit-for-bit. CONTENT-ID: same node maps to the same u128 across builds, permuted children canonicalize equal, and the intent is not folded. TIER-CONSISTENCY: the additive envelope-mass slot (ConservedBudget) satisfies parent equals the sum of children EXACTLY (an `i128` bit-sum), while a nonlinear proxy over that additive mass (a square-root resonance) is tier-resolution-dependent BY CONSTRUCTION and is NOT asserted invariant (the honest coarser-physics gap). DEVIATIONS, surfaced: (1) the node `content_id` uses PURE-CONTENT addressing (a `StateHasher` digest over the canonical body, master seed and intent OMITTED), matching the physics `Substance::content_id` pattern for cross-world dedup, flagged for owner ratification; (2) the interface-mismatch `PenaltyCurve` is a compose-local mirror of `civsim-sim`'s `decision::Curve` (compose sits below sim in the crate graph, so it cannot depend on it), same piecewise-linear clamp-at-ends shape; (3) the leaf structural dispatch consumes contact_area, section_modulus, and arm_length; edge_radius is carried by the form floor for the cutting dispatch, not the structural one; (4) the physics caps the leaf routes out-of-range results to derive from the substrate's axis-range upper bounds by dimension, with `Fixed::MAX` (the representable ceiling, not an owner value) the fallback when a dimension has no set axis. Eight `value_metric.*`/`lang.*`/`langdet.*`/`langmod.*`/`genome.*`/`tom.*` values move from authored numbers to fundamentals. (1) A body function's produce capacity is the mean structural integrity of its intact bearers, kneed at the wound function-loss threshold, so redundant limbs degrade a manual channel gracefully and a bearer worn past the threshold loses the function; (2) the language capability gate is the Liebig minimum of that produce half and the sensorium's perceive acuity, two races diverging only through body and sensorium data run through one kernel; (3) the cross-race value incommensurability is measured per race-pair as the etic projection loss (one untranslatable axis of stance s raises the distance by exactly the magnitude of s) rather than a flat floor, which is removed from `cross_race_distance` entirely; (4) enculturation pull is the Friedkin-Johnsen complement `1 - effective_stubbornness`; (5) concept-salience decay reads a decreasing memory-to-rate curve at the founding band's mean memory (`band_mean_memory`, an i128 sorted fold) floored by an underflow bound, so a sharp-memoried culture leaks its lexicon slower; (6) the shared etic substrate grows bottom-up, one axis per emic value axis that recurs across at least `etic_recurrence_min` races, an idiosyncratic axis staying private; (7) typology distance weights are the order-2 diversity `N^2 / sum(c_i^2)` of each parameter's prior counts; (8) the Dobzhansky-Muller cross counts by the joint Hardy-Weinberg product of the two pools' allele frequencies gated by the same presence, retiring the marginal-AND. The ToM meta params derive as the first-order `evidence.*` params themselves and the witnessed/told/said ladder derives from them by the offsets `commit + margin`, `commit`, `commit - margin`, so a witnessed access out-ranks a contrary telling by exactly the runner-up margin the commit test uses and a lie is seen through by construction; `reachable`, `absence`, and `denied` stay independent reserved levers. Wave-2 derive build-out (five related language-substrate derivations applied): BUILT (gate: `crates/sim/src/langmod.rs` `acquisition_split` + `phoneme_priors`; `crates/sim/src/language.rs` a `resonator_length` field on `FeatureValueDef`, `Language::race` (set at `Language::new`, carried through `fork`), the retired `DriftParams.generation_ticks`, and the `L2AcquisitionLaw` + `LangKnowledge` L2 kernel; `crates/sim/src/agent.rs` `RetentionLaw`; `crates/sim/src/world.rs` a `races` registry field (populated at `seed_dawn_populations`, settable with `set_races`), `set_form_system_for`, and `drift_languages` taking a `races` param with a per-lineage derived cadence (the `drift_step` move-out-and-back wrapper on the tick, `lang.race` folded into `state_hash`); `crates/sim/src/lib.rs` additive re-exports; tests in `langmod.rs`, `language.rs`, `agent.rs`, the reworked `crates/sim/tests/drift.rs`, and the new `crates/sim/tests/l2_acquisition.rs`; re-bases in `calibration/reserved.toml` of `langmod.acquisition_split`, `lang.phoneme_priors`, `lang.l2_acquisition` (to a maturation curve), and `langdet.usage_recency_window` (+ new `langdet.retention_memory_scale`), the RETIREMENT of `language.generation_ticks` in both `reserved.toml` and `calibration/profiles/dev-fixtures.toml`). Five values move from authored numbers to fundamentals, all on the substrate the Wave-1 gate and the celestial/maturation data already built. (1) `langmod::acquisition_split` is the being's perceive minus produce capability, read straight from the two `capability_halves`, so the receptive-bilingual asymmetry falls out of the capability gap: a race strong in perception weak in production splits positive, the swap mirrors it exactly, equal halves split zero, no `RaceId`. (2) `langmod::phoneme_priors` is a spread-maximising dispersion prior over the race's own `perceptual_geometry` confusability (each value's prior the sum over the others of `ONE / (ONE + confusability)`, higher where a value is more distinguishable), masked by the per-value capability gate so a value the race cannot produce or perceive gets zero prior; UPSID/PHOIBLE become the human race's DATA ROW (its resonator lengths, now carried per feature value on `FeatureValueDef.resonator_length`, and its sensorium acuity) rather than the global prior. Two media give two priors from the channel physics alone, no authored inventory, no `RaceId`. (3) the L2 kernel (`L2AcquisitionLaw::increment_for` + the per-being-per-language `LangKnowledge`) derives the age-of-acquisition breakpoint from each race's own maturation (`Race::maturation_fraction`, off `maturity_years`), the increment a decreasing data curve read at the maturation fraction, so two races with different `maturity_years` cross the critical period at different raw ages from one kernel and the increment slows past each race's own breakpoint, never the human late teens, no `RaceId`. (4) the drift cadence derives PER LINEAGE: `Language` carries its race, and `World::drift_languages` reads each lineage's race maturity against the world's `life_cadence_ticks` (the orbital year in ticks) so the generation length is `race.maturity_years * life_cadence_ticks`, two lineages of races with different maturities drifting on different cadences (proven by change-log count over a fixed span) with the one global `generation_ticks` scalar retired; a lineage whose race is absent does not drift on a fabricated cadence. (5) `RetentionLaw::window_ticks_for` scales a base recency window (the kept `langdet.usage_recency_window`) by a data curve read at a mind's memory, so a sharper memory holds a longer window and a flat curve reproduces one window, keying on the memory scalar, no `RaceId`. Every kernel is fixed-point, deterministic, race-blind (Principle 9), and carries a non-steering test. NEW RESERVED INPUT surfaced fail-loud with basis (never fabricated): `langdet.retention_memory_scale` (the increasing memory-to-window-multiplier curve the retention law reads). RE-BASED to DERIVE (kept reserved, fail-loud, value cleared): `langmod.acquisition_split` (no input remains, a pure capability subtraction), `lang.phoneme_priors` (the physics-and-sensorium data plus the new `resonator_length`), `lang.l2_acquisition` (re-scoped from a scalar rate to a maturation-fraction increment curve), and `langdet.usage_recency_window` (re-scoped to the BASE window the retention curve scales). RETIRED (comment tombstone, engine no longer reads it): `language.generation_ticks`, the same treatment as `genome.mutation_step`. DEVIATIONS, surfaced: (a) `drift_languages` needs the `races` registry, but threading it through `World::tick` would touch about eighty call sites, so the world now stores a `races` field (populated at `seed_dawn_populations`, settable with `set_races`, moved out and back on the tick's `drift_step` to satisfy the borrow checker), consistent with how `life_cadence` reads stored fields rather than per-call race maps; the field is owner config, not folded into `state_hash` (the lineage's `race` id is, mirroring how `race_of` is unfolded), so the observable divergence is the drift the derived cadence produces over time. (b) The retention law is placed in `agent.rs` (co-located with `Mind.memory`, the belief-deterioration consumer it names), not `language.rs`; the task allowed either. (c) `phoneme_priors` returns priors in feature-value order paired with the index as the id (the geometry is built index-ordered from the values), so a caller with arbitrary value ids zips the returned priors with its own ordered value list; documented at the function. Gates: `cargo build`, `cargo test -p civsim-sim` (515 lib + integration green), `cargo test -p civsim-core`, `cargo fmt --all -- --check`, `cargo clippy --workspace --exclude civsim-gpu --lib --tests` (zero warnings), `scripts/verify.sh`, and the real-manifest parse all green. Not done here (follow-ons): the Part 62 consolidation and audit-log Section 1 blocks stay owner-sign-off follow-ons; the five kernels are standalone (like the Wave-1 salience law and capability gate), not yet wired into the canonical `World::tick`.

Wave-3 derive build-out (three semantics-and-distance derivations applied): BUILT (gate: `crates/sim/src/value.rs` `GroundMetric::resolution` (the grid separability floor) and `incommensurability_ceiling` (a pure alias of the per-race-pair etic projection loss `project_to_etic_with_loss` sums); new `crates/sim/src/semantics.rs` (`Concept`, `SemanticSubstrate`, `ConceptThresholds`, `concept_thresholds`, `substrate_quantization`, `QUANTIZATION_DIVISOR`); new `crates/sim/src/langdist.rs` (`lexical_distance`, `phonological_distance`, `language_distance`, `ComponentWeights`, `distance_component_weights`); a `FormSystem::inventory` accessor on `crates/sim/src/language.rs`; `crates/sim/src/lib.rs` module registration and additive re-exports; per-module non-steering tests; re-bases in `calibration/reserved.toml` of `lang.concept_thresholds`, `langdet.substrate_quantization`, `langdet.incommensurability_ceiling`, and `lang.distance_component_weights` to DERIVE). Three reserved values move from authored numbers to fundamentals on the substrate Wave-1 (the etic projection loss and `information_weights`) and Wave-2 (`perceptual_geometry`) already built. (1) `value::incommensurability_ceiling` is a pure ALIAS of the summed measured etic projection loss of a race pair (the same two loss terms `cross_race_distance` folds in), surfaced on its own so the language-distance no-shared-form ceiling and per-cell one-sided-coverage contribution read the measured loss rather than a separate constant; symmetric, no `RaceId`. In `langdist` those two cases are the normalised language image: a concept one side lacks counts as fully non-cognate and a form-disjoint or cross-modality pair reaches the ceiling of one, both emerging from the non-cognate share, no separate authored constant (`langdet.incommensurability_ceiling` re-based to DERIVE). (2) the Part 33.1 semantic substrate: `Concept` is a `prototype: Vec<Fixed>` point over a meaning `GroundMetric`, `SemanticSubstrate` a `ConceptId`-to-`Concept` map, and `GroundMetric::resolution` the grid separability floor (the lightest positive finite structural distance, defaulting to `ONE` for independent axes). The discrimination threshold DERIVES as the minimum positive inter-meaning distance (Euclidean over prototypes, the pinned independent form, structured meaning metrics left as the same flagged seam `value_distance` returns `None` for) floored by the perceptual just-noticeable difference; the lexicalisation threshold as the occupied meaning span spread over the contrast budget, floored by discrimination. `substrate_quantization` is a fixed integer fraction (`QUANTIZATION_DIVISOR = 2`, the Nyquist separability bound) of the discrimination threshold, the one knob reused for the walk, the walk key, and the correspondence tie window, consistent with `GroundMetric::resolution`. Two races with different meaning prototypes get different thresholds from the one kernel, no authored human concept set, no `RaceId` (`lang.concept_thresholds` re-based to DERIVE, its concept-drift-rate the one remaining reserved input; `langdet.substrate_quantization` re-based to DERIVE, no input remaining). (3) `langdist::distance_component_weights` derives the three component weights as each layer's own order-2 diversity (the Hill number `N^2 / sum(c_i^2)`, the same measure `information_weights` uses) across a corpus, the lexical layer over pooled word-forms, the phonological over pooled producible primitives, the grammatical over pooled `(parameter, value)` settings, each over the total and normalised to sum to exactly one by deterministic residual absorption into the lexical component (R-LANG-DET); lexical dominance EMERGES from the entropy of real lexicons rather than the authored 0.6/0.25/0.15, the weights invariant to permuting which language is which and reading no `RaceId` (`lang.distance_component_weights` re-based to DERIVE, no input remaining). Every kernel is fixed-point, deterministic, race-blind (Principle 9), and carries a non-steering test. DEVIATIONS, surfaced: (a) the task names the ceiling `value_metric.incommensurability_ceiling`, and the alias lives in `value.rs`, but the manifest entry whose basis is verbatim the no-shared-form-and-one-sided-coverage ceiling is `langdet.incommensurability_ceiling`, so that is the entry re-based (no redundant `value_metric.incommensurability_ceiling` entry added, since the alias introduces no new reserved input beyond the already-derived projection loss). (b) the language-distance ceiling and one-sided contribution are the top of the normalised `[0, ONE]` share (`ONE`), the language image of the value-space projection-loss ceiling, rather than a literal cross-crate call into `value.rs` (which would need value profiles the language layer does not hold); the two are the same untranslatable-magnitude concept at two scales, documented at both sites. (c) the `jnd` and contrast budget flow into `concept_thresholds` as `Fixed` parameters (from `perceptual_geometry` / `PerceptualGeometry::contrast_budget`) rather than recomputing the perceptual geometry inside `semantics.rs`, keeping the module a pure geometry-and-threshold kernel. (d) semantics-and-langdist are non-trivial builds (each a new module with its own test submodule), larger than Task 1's small value.rs alias, as the task anticipated. Wave-4 derive build-out (the FINAL four derivations, closing the derive column): BUILT (gate: NEW `crates/sim/src/personality.rs` (`TraitAxisId`/`TraitDef`/`PersonalityProfile`/`PersonalityRegistry`/`TraitInstance`/`plasticity_at`/`age_personality`), registered in `crates/sim/src/lib.rs` and wired into `crates/sim/src/world.rs` (a `personality` registry field and per-being `traits` map, `set_personality_registry`/`install_personality`/`trait_value`, birth-neutral seeding at the dawn and at birth, pruning in `remove_being`, and a `drift_personalities` beat inside `life_cadence` after aging); `crates/physics/src/laws.rs` `thermal_diffusivity`; `crates/sim/src/runner.rs` `derive_field_diffusion`/`FieldCalib::from_manifest_with_medium` and the `STENCIL_STABILITY_BOUND`/`DIFFUSIVITY_MAX` constants; `crates/sim/src/evolve.rs` `EvolveParams::from_layout`/`from_manifest_and_layout` and the `ACTIVATION_CLAMP_WIDTH` constant; `crates/sim/src/evidence.rs` `derive_aggregate_diffusion_rate` and the rewritten `aggregate_diffusion_rate`; tests in each module plus the new `crates/sim/tests/personality.rs`; re-bases/retires in `calibration/reserved.toml` of `being.plasticity_by_age`, `being.maturity_targets`, `field.diffusion` (+ new `field.cell_size`), the three `behavior.controller_*` scalars (+ new `behavior.controller_target_mutations`/`behavior.controller_mutation_step_fraction`), the three `medium.*` profiles (thermal axes added), and `evidence.aggregate_diffusion_rate`). Four derivations close the derive column the audit-fix tail named. (1) AGE-PERSONALITY: `being.plasticity_by_age` and `being.maturity_targets` stay per-race `TraitDef` data on a new `PersonalityRegistry`, and one `age_personality` kernel, read at `World::life_cadence`, drifts each being's trait toward its race's maturity target at `plasticity_curve.eval(Race::maturation_fraction(age))`, high in youth and low at the maturity plateau; two races diverge (one trait rising, one falling) purely from their curve and target data, no `RaceId` branch, and the trait state rides the aging cadence deterministically (not folded into `state_hash`, matching how `ages` is treated). The human maturity principle (rising rank-order stability, rising conscientiousness, falling novelty-seeking) is one race's data row. (2) FIELD.DIFFUSION derives from the SELECTED medium: `laws::thermal_diffusivity` is the medium's `alpha = k/(rho*c)`, and `runner::derive_field_diffusion` scales it by the base tick over the squared cell size and clamps to the four-neighbour stencil's 1/4 von Neumann stability bound, so air and water get different coefficients from `k/(rho*c)` alone; the medium is the lever and the diffusivity is physics. The three medium profiles gain reserved-with-basis `conductivity` and `specific_heat` axes (real air/water/CO2 values from Incropera and DeWitt), and a new reserved `field.cell_size` is the scale bound. (3) BEHAVIOR.CONTROLLER trio: `EvolveParams::from_layout` derives `init_spread = 1/sqrt(n_in)` (Xavier/He fan-in scaling, no new scalar), `mutation_rate = target_mutations/weight_count` (so the per-locus rate falls as the controller grows at fixed expected mutations), and `mutation_step = mutation_step_fraction * clamp_width` (a fraction of the activation's [-1, 1] range); the two new reserved fractions `behavior.controller_target_mutations` and `behavior.controller_mutation_step_fraction` are fail-loud with basis, and the three old `behavior.controller_init_spread`/`_mutation_rate`/`_mutation_step` scalars retire to a tombstone. (4) EVIDENCE.AGGREGATE_DIFFUSION_RATE derives as the mean field of the individual-tier gossip loop `told_weight * trust_baseline * contact_density` (`evidence::derive_aggregate_diffusion_rate`); `aggregate_diffusion_rate` reads the two gossip parameters at unit contact density, with the per-belief contact density entering downstream as the `PrevailingBelief::advance_diffusion` distance coupling, so no independent Earth-village rate is authored, and a tier-consistency test validates the aggregate logistic run at the derived rate against the mean of a stochastic individual-tier gossip ensemble within a sampling tolerance. Every kernel is fixed-point, deterministic, race-blind (Principle 9), and carries a non-steering test; each new reserved input is fail-loud with basis (never fabricated). DEVIATIONS, surfaced: (a) the age-personality substrate is a full new module with world wiring (a birth-neutral trait seed at the dawn and at birth, and a `drift_personalities` life-cadence beat), larger than a small alias, as the task anticipated; the birth value is a neutral zero the drift moves away from (a being's inherited starting personality is a named follow-on), so a maturity target above zero reads as a rising trait and one below as a falling one. (b) field.diffusion carried more than a reserved add: it needed the physics `thermal_diffusivity` law, the `conductivity` and `specific_heat` medium axes, and a new `field.cell_size` scale constant, and its HONEST LIMIT stands: at a one-second base tick and a map-scale cell the physical coefficient is far below the stencil bound and even below Q32.32 resolution, so the derivation reproduces heat that barely conducts per tick (physically correct), and a scale-appropriate cell size or a coarser field sub-step is where a visible diffusion rate comes from (recorded in the `field.diffusion` and `field.cell_size` bases). (c) the aggregate rate keeps `evidence.aggregate_diffusion_rate` as a reserved pointer (a DERIVES basis, no scalar) rather than a tombstone, because `advance_diffusion` still takes the per-belief contact density as its `distance` argument, so `rate * distance` is the full mean-field product. World-wiring increment 2 (the production scenario-to-`Runner` assembly, handoff section 4): BUILT (gate: `crates/sim/src/worldbuild.rs`, a new module carrying `DawnPeoples` (a world's declared races, founding bands, breeding registry, personality registry, and optional mortality hazard) and `build_dawn_runner`, the top-level world-build function that assembles a whole `Runner` from a resolved scenario: it builds the `World` from the manifest with the life cadence derived from the orbit, installs the breeding and personality registries before seeding, seeds the dawn population through `seed_dawn_populations` (sizing each founder's evidence ring from expressed memory through `RingCapacityLaw::from_manifest`), arms the language and drift calibrations (concepts from the NSM primes, `LanguageParams`/`DriftParams` fail-loud from the manifest), optionally arms a mortality hazard, derives the field from the resolved medium through `FieldCalib::from_resolution` (the increment-1 seam, now with a top-level caller), and composes the armed world onto the field runner through `Runner::with_world`; `calibration/profiles/dev-fixtures.toml` extended with the world-build path's fixtures (`medium.air`, `medium.water`, `field.cell_size`, `field.relaxation`, `field.body_exchange`, `axiom.evidence_ring_curve`, `axiom.evidence_ring_hard_cap`), each a labelled placeholder with its basis while the reserved fail-loud entries stay in `reserved.toml`; a new integration test `crates/sim/tests/world_build.rs` (4 tests) proving the assembly seeds a genome-real dawn, replays bit for bit and is seed-sensitive, advances its composed cognition world every step (closing the open question: a `Runner` wrapping a dawn world DOES tick the inner cognition beats), derives the field from the medium end to end (an air world and a water world build a bit-identical dawn but diverging fields), and keeps the scheduled order bit-identical to the pinned order). Fail-loud (Principle 11), determinism-clean (Principle 3, the seed keys before any minting and the field runner adds no RNG phase), and steering-clean (Principle 9, the assembly installs no authored decision repertoire, so `with_world`'s refusal boundary holds by construction). DEVIATION, surfaced: the assembly runs under `Profile::Development` on the dev-fixtures profile (the `Profile::Calibrated` world still awaits the owner's reserved-value calibration, Tier B item 1, so nothing here graduates a reserved value); the races and founding bands are a caller-supplied input, not a product of the path, since the race-genesis that would grow sentient races from the pre-dawn biosphere (design Part 28) is a later arc; and the per-race articulation substrate that would make the naming game and drift LIVE is the language-substrate increment below, so the language calibrations are armed but inert until a lineage carries a form system. Gates: `cargo build`, `cargo test -p civsim-sim -p civsim-physics -p civsim-core` (all green), `cargo fmt --all -- --check`, `cargo clippy --workspace --exclude civsim-gpu --lib --tests` (zero warnings), `scripts/verify.sh` clean. Not done here (follow-ons): the derived language substrate (2a-2e below), reproduction (increment 5), enculturation (increment 6).

The language-substrate increment (handoff increment 2, "arm language from `phoneme_priors`, no authored lexicon"), decomposed and audit-confirmed to be an L not an S-M: `phoneme_priors` returns dispersion WEIGHTS with no consumer that builds a `FormSystem` (the bridge from weights to producible feature-values to `FormSegment`s to `FormSystem::new` does not exist), `Race` carries NO acoustic/articulation/sensorium data (so a per-race derived form system has no owner-data home), and the WP5 `Sensorium` conflation is load-bearing (`langmod::capability_halves` reads `sensorium.reads(channel)` as a `[0, ONE]` acuity while `langmod::perceptual_geometry` reads the SAME field as a Hz-scale just-noticeable difference). Ordered sub-increments, each independently testable and gated: 2a, land WP5 first (split `Sensorium` into a per-channel acuity read by `capability_halves` and a per-channel resolution/JND in Hz read by `perceptual_geometry`, distinct fields or accessors, fixing the latent bug regardless of the rest); 2b (the L core), give per-race articulation and resolution a data home (fill `FeatureValueDef.resonator_length` with real base per-feature-value geometry reserved-with-basis, replacing the degenerate ZERO, add a per-race vocal-tract scale to `Race` that scales those base lengths in `perceptual_geometry` plus a per-race sensorium resolution seed, following the per-race registry pattern with no `RaceId` branch, and flag the vocal-tract scale as authored-now-derivable-later from the body plan / R-ORGAN-FLUX); 2c, add the reserved producibility threshold (the prior-and-gate level below which a feature value does not enter the inventory, the selection folding in canonical `FeatureValueId` order); 2d, bridge the thresholded inventory to a `FormSystem` (`FormSystem::new(modality, inventory, min_len, max_len)` per race, `min_len`/`max_len` reserved-with-basis or derived via a contrast-budget argument, fail-loud on an empty inventory); 2e, arm the per-race `FormSystem` at the founder step built above via `set_form_system_for`, so the already-live naming game and drift run (milestone: bands coin and converge one word per concept, separated lineages drift into sister languages on their race cadences). WP5 in the WIRE-PENDING list above is subsumed by 2a.

The language substrate (2a-2e): BUILT (2026-07-04). 2a (`crates/sim/src/sensorium.rs`, `crates/sim/src/langmod.rs`): `Sensorium` split into a per-channel acuity map (read by the perceive gate and `capability_halves`) and a sibling resolution/JND map (read by `perceptual_geometry`), fixing the WP5 conflation where a valid acuity of one read as an implausible one-hertz JND; `reads()`/acuity unchanged so the perception gate is untouched, no golden-hash refresh. 2b (`crates/sim/src/race.rs`, `crates/sim/src/langmod.rs`, `crates/sim/src/language.rs`): `Articulation { vocal_tract_scale, hearing_resolution }` as an `Option` on `Race` with a `with_articulation` builder, `articulated_geometry` scaling the shared base lengths by the race's vocal tract and reading its hearing resolution as the sensorium JND, and `ArticulationSubstrate::phonetic` carrying real base resonator lengths (replacing the syllabic zero) with a `resonator_lengths` accessor; the vocal-tract scale flagged authored-now-derivable-later (body plan / R-ORGAN-FLUX). 2c (`crates/sim/src/langmod.rs`): `producible_values` selecting the values whose dispersion-and-capability prior clears the reserved threshold in canonical `FeatureValueId` order, a gate-masked (zero-prior) value never entering. 2d (`crates/sim/src/langmod.rs`): `form_system_from_values`, the previously-missing bridge from thresholded producible values to `FormSegment`s to a coinable `FormSystem`, fail-loud (`FormSystemError::EmptyInventory`) rather than coining empty words. 2e (`crates/sim/src/worldbuild.rs`, `crates/sim/src/world.rs`): `LanguageGenesis` and `arm_dawn_languages` deriving each articulating race's form system through the 2b-2d pipeline (cached per race) and installing a per-band lineage, wired into `build_dawn_runner` via the optional `DawnPeoples.language`, plus a `World::being_ids()` accessor. Reserved-with-basis, surfaced never fabricated (`calibration/reserved.toml`): `articulation.base_resonator_lengths`, `articulation.vocal_tract_scale`, `articulation.hearing_resolution`, `articulation.producibility_threshold`, `articulation.word_min_len`, `articulation.word_max_len`. Determinism (Principle 3) and no-`RaceId`-branch (Principle 9) throughout: two races diverge in their sounds only through their `Articulation` data, one pipeline. Proven in `crates/sim/tests/world_build.rs` and the `langmod`/`language`/`sensorium`/`race` unit tests: a sharper ear yields a strictly richer producible inventory (a full one versus a fail-loud empty), bands coin and converge words from their derived inventory while separated bands and the two races diverge, a genesis-less build stays inert, and the language-armed build replays bit for bit. HONEST LIMITS: the founder step's `LanguageGenesis` is a caller-supplied bundle (its medium acoustics need the medium's bulk modulus, a reserved axis not yet on the medium profile, so a full `from_manifest` for it is a follow-on); the capability gate is a channel-wide scalar broadcast per value (a per-value producibility model is a follow-on); the vocal-tract scale and the word-length range are interim levers flagged for their eventual derivations. Gates green: build, test (sim/physics/core), fmt, clippy (zero warnings), verify.sh, real-manifest parse.

World-wiring increment 10 Part B (the anatomy-derived physiology producers LIVE in the embodiment step): BUILT (2026-07-04). The R-METABOLIZE and R-MEDIUM producers, built and unit-tested but dormant on the running tick, now drive an embodied being's survival from its body plan rather than the authored per-axis scalars. `crates/sim/src/runner.rs` gains an `EmbodiedPhysiology` config (the organ `BodyPlanRegistry`, the `MetabolicAnchors`, a uniform ambient medium's respirable content, the reserved Fick transfer coefficient, and the base tick), sourced fail-loud through `EmbodiedPhysiology::from_manifest` (anchors from `MetabolicAnchors::from_manifest`, respirable content from the resolved `medium.{name}` profile, the transfer coefficient and base tick from the manifest) or a labelled `dev_fixture`; it installs on an `Embodiment` through `set_physiology`, opt-in so the evolve harness and the thermal fixtures keep the scalar path untouched. When installed: `step_embodiment` builds each being's per-axis `DerivedDrain`, deriving the metabolic (energy-density-backed, keyed off the floor axis id not a hardcoded constant) axis's drain through `derive_base_drain` (read against the being's LIVE post-exchange core temperature as the effective ambient and its own comfort set point, so the base drain tracks the medium each tick) plus a work-derived `derive_exertion_coupling`, while every other axis keeps its authored per-axis rate, then drains through `Homeostasis::metabolize_derived` inside `locomotion::step_with_field_dirs` (a new `drains` parameter reconciles metabolism with locomotion cleanly: the being's own exertion signal scales the coupling where it is computed, and the scalar `metabolize` is retired on the embodied+physiology path while kept for the fixture callers); a respiration sub-phase runs `medium::respire` per being in canonical id order (breathe in before the tick's metabolic draw) where the registry carries a `RESPIRATION` axis; and `with_embodiment` seeds each being's static derived `h*A/(m*c)` body-to-medium exchange rate through `set_body_exchange_rate`, so `phase_body_exchange` couples at the anatomy-derived rate rather than the flat `FieldCalib.exchange`. One new reserved-with-basis value, surfaced never fabricated (`calibration/reserved.toml`, dev-fixtures set): `metabolism.respiration_transfer_coefficient` (the Fick membrane gas-transfer coefficient); the respiration flux representability cap is an engine-mechanics const (`RESPIRATION_FLUX_MAX`), not an owner value. Determinism (Principle 3): the derived drains are recomputed each tick and the exchange rate is static config, so no new canonical state escapes the existing `state_hash` fold (reserves and body temperatures are already folded); the walks are canonical id order and draw no RNG. No-`RaceId`-branch (Principle 9): the divergence keys off body-plan, tissue-composition, medium, and temperature data, never a label. Proven in `crates/sim/tests/physiology_embodiment.rs`: two beings differing ONLY in body plan diverge in per-tick energy drain and time-to-death through the live step, with the larger, denser body draining a SMALLER fraction per tick and outliving the small one (the Kleiber signature, end to end); a body lives in a rich medium and suffocates in a poor one from the medium's content; the coupled physiology runner replays bit for bit and is bit-identical under the scheduler variant (`step` equals `step_scheduled`); and `EmbodiedPhysiology::from_manifest` reads a set manifest and fails loud on a reserved input. HONEST LIMITS and DEVIATIONS, surfaced: the ambient medium is a single uniform value this increment (a spatially-varying per-cell `MediumField` a being reads at its coordinate is the named refinement, the respiratory sibling of the per-cell temperature field); the exertion coupling's work force is the being's normalized body mass as a proxy pending the Part 35 work-force datum, its velocity the body's full-exertion ground speed; the R-METABOLIZE unit limits stand (the kJ/g-to-joule R-UNITS-PIN bridge, the base-versus-exertion power-scale gap, and the nonlinear-mass pool-tier Jensen gap); and the physiology is installed on the `Embodiment` (evolved-controller) path, not on the cognition-world `build_dawn_runner` path, since no production builder yet unifies the two populations. Gates: `cargo build`, `cargo test -p civsim-sim -p civsim-physics -p civsim-core` (all green), `cargo fmt --all -- --check`, `cargo clippy --workspace --exclude civsim-gpu --lib --tests` (zero warnings), `scripts/verify.sh` clean, and the real-manifest parse and scenario resolution green. This completes the world-wiring arc (increments 1 through 10, Parts A and B).

Real-world unification arc (one runner carrying minds and bodies): BUILT (2026-07-04), `docs/working/REAL_WORLD_UNIFICATION_HANDOFF.md`, on branch `claude/real-world-unification`. The wired substrate now runs as one deterministic world: a founder's `StableId` owns at once a `World` mind and an `Embodiment` walker on the field, and the runner ticks N generations. Five steps plus the lifecycle half, each determinism-audited and tested. Step 1, census-Ne close (retiring audit deviation 23 for the post-dawn tier): `build_dawn_runner` arms `World::set_reproduction` and `arm_generational_drift`, and `World::life_cadence` resets the reproductive census window once per generation after `drift_pools` reads it, so each generation's drift keys off its own census-derived Ne, not the authored founder size (`crates/sim/src/world.rs`, `crates/sim/src/worldbuild.rs`; R-REPRO). Step 2, run-path unification (the crux): `Runner::with_world_and_embodiment` carries both Options under one shared id space (the world's `Registry` is the sole minting authority; walkers reuse founder ids, never a second mint), and a `RES_BEING` resource declared by both `SYS_EMBODIMENT` and `SYS_WORLD` forces the deterministic scheduler to serialize the two systems in the pinned `SYS_EMBODIMENT` < `SYS_WORLD` order once a being is shared, so the composite stays bit-identical across worker widths with the shared being present. Step 3, the dawn embodiment: a `body: Option<BodyPlan>` data home on `Race` (sibling to articulation), and `assemble_dawn_embodiment` gives each founder whose race carries a body plan a located, metabolizing body sharing its mind id, its controller expressed from its genome and its comfort band the reserved thermal set point and half-band; a bodiless-race mind stays a mind with no walker (owner ruling: the pairing is optional, so a future disembodied mind is a clean extension). Step 3c, lifecycle pairing: a new `reconcile_lifecycle` beat runs after `world.tick` on both the pinned and scheduled paths so a `World` birth mints a paired body (expressed from the newborn's race and genome, reusing the mind id), a locomotion death ends its mind in the world, and a world-mortality death retires the paired body (walker, comfort band, body temperature, exchange rate, and located-index entry all dropped); it is a pure deterministic function of post-tick state (no RNG, canonical id order, worker-count independent). Step 4, the per-cell medium field (closing the increment-10B uniform-medium limit): `MediumField::from_map` folds the worldgen map into a per-cell medium by physical elevation (below the reserved `medium.submersion_elevation` a cell holds the submerged medium, else the emergent medium, no biome-label branch, owner ruling), `EmbodiedPhysiology` carries the field, and `step_embodiment` swaps the scalar `medium::respire` for `medium::respire_at` at the being's coordinate; only respiration is wired (the field's temperature vector is sourced from the worldgen tile but unread, the canonical diffused `Field` stays authoritative for body temperature, so the G5 temperature desync cannot manifest), with buoyancy and in-medium thermal exchange deferred until that desync is resolved (R-MEDIUM). Step 5, the Part 35 muscle-force datum (closing the increment-10B body-mass-proxy limit): `physiology::whole_body_muscle_force(plan, organs, anchors)` is the development-weighted sum over the organs of `mat.fracture_strength` times body mass, mirroring the individual-tier `Body::strength` (muscle mass times material strength) so the two tiers stay dimensionally consistent (owner ruling), and the runner exertion coupling reads it in place of the raw `body_mass` proxy, so two bodies of equal mass but different muscle endowment now drain differently under exertion and a body with no muscle tissue exerts no force (the absence convention). Two new reserved-with-basis values, surfaced never fabricated (`calibration/reserved.toml`, dev-fixtures set): `reproduction.mutation_spread` (the one spread the belief-seed and mate-preference inheritance share) and `medium.submersion_elevation` (the waterline on the normalized elevation field the biome classifier reads); the muscle-force axis reuses the existing `mat.fracture_strength` figure. Determinism (Principle 3): proven bit-identical across worker widths [1,2,3,8] and replay, and `step` equals `step_scheduled`, for the shared-id dawn runner, the multi-generation reproducing-and-drifting runner, and the birth-and-death lifecycle runner. Principle 9: every divergence keys off data (genome, body plan, tissue composition, census, elevation), never a `RaceId` or label; the `has_behaviour` refusal survives into `with_world_and_embodiment`. Principle 11: every reserved value is fail-loud from the manifest. Proven in `crates/sim/tests/world_build.rs` (census-Ne growth, embodied founders, newborns paired to bodies across generations, culled minds' bodies retired), `crates/sim/tests/determinism_harness.rs` (the shared-id path across widths, `step` versus `step_scheduled`, the authored-repertoire refusal), `crates/sim/tests/physiology_embodiment.rs` (per-cell respiration through the runner, the muscle-force datum with mass scaling), and `crates/sim/src/medium.rs` (the elevation fold and its single-medium regression). TOMBSTONES, the increment-10B honest limits this arc closes: the uniform ambient medium is now the per-cell `MediumField` (Step 4); the exertion work force is now the Part 35 muscle-force datum, not the normalized-body-mass proxy (Step 5); the physiology and the cognition-world `build_dawn_runner` path are now one unified population (Steps 2, 3). HONEST LIMITS that stand: `PlaceId` stays frozen at the dawn band (deriving it from the cell is research-gated), so movement is thermoregulation-only while social geography stays at the dawn band; buoyancy and in-medium thermal exchange are deferred behind the medium-temperature desync; the edibility physiology on the dawn embodiment is the temperature-only dev fixture; and the R-METABOLIZE unit limits (the R-UNITS-PIN bridge, the base-versus-exertion power-scale gap, the pool-tier Jensen gap) stand. Gates: `cargo fmt --all`, `cargo clippy --workspace --exclude civsim-gpu --lib --tests` (zero warnings), `bash scripts/verify.sh` clean, the full `civsim-sim` suite green, the real-manifest parse and scenarios resolve. GPU oracle out of scope for this arc (verified separately on the 5090). The arc was fully-blind audited before merge (the muscle-force datum's missing body-mass factor was caught by that lens and fixed before the panel ran).


## World-wiring stood up and first real runs (2026-07-04)

The run harness `crates/sim/examples/run_world.rs` drives `build_dawn_runner` into one unified runner (minds and located, metabolizing bodies), ticks N life-cadence generations, and emits emergence readers (population and lineages, per-race census Ne, language consensus and cross-band cognate overlap, per-band belief stance, births/deaths, mean body temperature) plus a `state_hash`. Runs are bit-identical on repeat and seed-sensitive (different seed, different world); the field derives from the medium end to end (air and water hash differently). Dev run on the dev-fixtures manifest, not a Calibrated run.

Remaining-wiring fix applied: `World::birth` now inherits the child's NATIVE LANGUAGE (its first parent's `lang_of` lineage and a copy of its lexicon), so a tongue is transmitted across generations and drifts through the naming game and the drift step rather than each newborn starting speechless. Folded into `state_hash` through the per-mind lexicon fold; a deterministic copy, no draw. Imperfect acquisition (per-birth transmission loss) is a refinement.

FIRST-RUNS FINDINGS (Crucible, Confluence, Mirror, 50 generations, several seeds): the dominant dynamic is an unchecked Malthusian population explosion (Crucible 24 to 4090 in 50 generations, births far outpacing deaths) because there is NO carrying capacity yet. Language consensus collapses in lockstep (70 percent to 18 percent) as the naming game is swamped by the flood of new speakers, while per-race belief stances stay distinct and stable through the churn (inherited culture persists; actively-negotiated culture fragments under population pressure). Per-race census Ne is tracked and drifts. This is the vivid case for the environmental-fields arc below: without carrying capacity, life multiplies without limit and negotiated culture cannot keep up. NOT-YET-OBSERVABLE: a canonical speciation reader, design origination (knowledge reads zero), and institution crystallization on the run path.

Priority after the real-world unification stands up and runs: (1) the ENVIRONMENTAL-FIELDS arc, UP NEXT, foundational and gating a true culture and society (owner call 2026-07-04); (2) the CELESTIAL / ASTRONOMY arc, later, the deep-end fun.

======================================================================
ARC A (UP NEXT): Environmental fields, the basal physical substrate
======================================================================

Today there is exactly one live field, temperature (runner.rs:44 names moisture, wind, and resource as the fields that follow the same pattern), plus static per-cell worldgen elevation/moisture/temperature (worldgen.rs:32) and biome classification. A world's habitability contrast (the Crucible's fertile greenwells in a lethal waste) is currently PAINTED by the biome classifier, not emergent from physics. This arc builds the sibling fields so scarcity, habitability, and adaptation emerge:

- Hydrology: water moves over the elevation map, pools in basins, evaporates faster where hot, so the greenwells fall out as where water collects in an arid world. A dynamic field on the temperature diffusion/advection stencil (GPU-ready, bit-identity-gated the same way).
- Productivity / primary production: the biomass a cell can support, a physical potential from water, light, temperature, and soil nutrients. NOT an authored dead-zone scalar.
- Wind and a particulate (dust/ash) field: advects heat and carries a dust load that couples into respiration and the per-cell medium, and produces rain shadow so aridity emerges behind mountains.
- Soil chemistry (salinity, nutrients): a per-cell physical property.

GOVERNING PRINCIPLE (Principle 8, the owner-directed correction 2026-07-04): every environmental field is a GRADIENT organisms adapt to, NEVER a hard gate. A salt flat is not dead by fiat. Salinity is a toxin-class DOSE on the biology-floor substrate (a per-cell field value), and an organism's harm from a salt cell is its dose measured against its OWN tolerance through the EXISTING edibility mechanism (edibility.rs: Composition carries the dose per toxin class at :75, Physiology carries a per-organism tolerance and integer-Hill exponent per class at :142-151, harm is dose versus tolerance). Tolerance is per-organism and heritable through the genome, so the homeostatic-survival and selection loop ADAPTS it: a salt flat is lethal to the intolerant and a NICHE for halophile lineages that evolve to tolerate it. Heat, drought, dust, and low-oxygen tolerance are the same shape, all heritable, all selected, so extremophiles and specialists emerge and the waste is a mosaic of niches rather than a dead zone. Carrying capacity is therefore organism-relative: a salty-but-wet cell has high capacity for a halophyte and near-zero for the intolerant, so scarcity is measured per people, not an authored per-cell scalar. A lineage that adapts to the waste can cross and contest it, so the killing ground itself becomes contested range and the emergent conflict deepens. No per-cell dead-zone template, no per-race branch (Principle 9): the environment supplies the gradient, selection supplies the adaptation.

CONFLICT-COEFFICIENT DERIVATION (closing the last steer, coupled to this arc): once the productivity/carrying-capacity field exists, retire the free authored value_metric.conflict_coefficient dial (crucible.toml sets it high) into a DERIVATION from measured scarcity (population pressure over what the land supports per lineage). value.rs:525 conflict_pressure already reads emergent pairwise inputs (value distance times the coefficient times one-plus-measured-niche-overlap, plus grievance, minus trust); only the coefficient is authored, and crucible.toml's own comment states the intent that its regime key on the generated scarcity physics, not the world's name. The carrying-capacity field is what makes that derivation possible. Then the Crucible's war is fully bottom-up: physics, then water and fertility, then per-lineage carrying capacity, then measured scarcity, then conflict-proneness, then the pairwise pressure, then war, with nothing telling the world to fight.

Not Crucible-only: these fields serve every world (a Confluence's rivers, a Tempest's storms), and they pair with the celestial arc's insolation (insolation drives temperature, which drives evaporation, which drives hydrology). Gate: determinism (the fields on the pinned diffusion/advection stencil, folded into state_hash, GPU oracle bit-identity verified on the 5090), Principle 8 (gradient not gate), Principle 9 (organisms key off their own heritable tolerances), Principle 11 (the physical constants reserved-with-basis).

======================================================================
ARC B (LATER, deep-end fun): Celestial / astronomy
======================================================================

The whole celestial model today is two scalars, orbital_period_seconds and rotation_period_seconds (crates/world/src/celestial.rs), feeding only the calendar; nothing positional is mapped (no star, no moon, no bodies, no sky). The unlock is a deterministic celestial-mechanics layer: a set of bodies (star(s), planet, moon(s), maybe wanderers) with orbital elements whose positions are pure functions of the tick. From positions, two cascades derive, on the authored-physics / emergent-culture line: a PHYSICS cascade (insolation, eclipses, moon phases, tides) and a CULTURE cascade (calendars, constellations, navigation, omens, astrology, all emergent through the belief/language/institution substrate, never authored).

- Insolation (the first increment, already flagged): today the surface temperature field is diffusion plus relaxation toward a STATIC per-cell baseline (Field::step, Field.baseline, runner.rs:262), the baseline the worldgen tile temperature (a standing latitude gradient, blend_latitude, worldgen.rs:113) the doc calls the solar and biome forcing (runner.rs:137). The orbital and rotation periods feed only the clock, never the heat, so there is no diurnal cycle, no seasons (no obliquity datum), and no distance-to-star or luminosity term. The increment: a time-varying baseline or an explicit insolation source term in Field::step, the diurnal term from the rotation phase, the seasonal term from the orbital phase and a reserved obliquity datum, the mean level from orbital radius and stellar luminosity. Determinism (the phase is a pure function of the tick and the periods), Principle 9 (forcing from the world's own star and orbit, never a terran constant or hardcoded day length), Principle 11 (obliquity, orbital radius, luminosity reserved-with-basis).
- Eclipses: geometry from the bodies' positions (star-planet-moon alignment inside a shadow-cone threshold), deterministic and predictable, so the astronomer-priest and the eclipse-omen emerge as knowledge and institutions. Needs a moon body plus the star.
- Moons and phases, tides (moon plus sun gravity), comets (bodies on eccentric orbits with periodic, derivable apparitions; fixed-point Kepler via deterministic eccentric-anomaly iteration), meteor showers (a comet's debris trail crossing the orbit, deterministic; sporadics counter-keyed RNG), a generated deterministic star field with EMERGENT constellations (a race groups salient stars by its own sensorium and semantics, so two races draw different skies), a pole star and axial precession, the star's own properties (luminosity, color, mass) shaping insolation and sky color and the habitable band, planets as wanderers feeding astrology, and the emergent calendar (day, lunar month, year, eclipse and comet cycles derived from the observable cycles, so a two-moon race invents a different calendar).

Sequence, once the unification lands: (1) celestial-mechanics layer, (2) insolation, (3) moon/phases/eclipses/tides, (4) star field with emergent constellations and navigation, (5) comets and meteor showers, (6) the emergent calendar/astrology/omen cultural layer. Owner call when scheduled: whether the first real runs want a living sky or a static climate.


The base-level liveliness arc is now fully scoped with an ordered, feasibility-grounded build plan in `docs/working/BASE_LIVELINESS_HANDOFF.md` (the five steps, the promotion policy, the observability additions, and the gates). The first runs proved its case: the world is dead for three concrete reasons (blank dawn controllers so no movement, no energy/water axis or depletable food so no carrying capacity, conversation half-wired and decoupled from movement). Recommended first step: field-coupled movement (pure data, no Rust change), the keystone the rest rides on.

Biosphere depth probe (2026-07-04): the pre-dawn biosphere (crates/sim/src/genesis.rs, biosphere.rs, epoch.rs, anatomy.rs) was tested end to end and is deep, and a dev inspector crates/sim/examples/biosphere_probe.rs was added (a longer, optionally-magical genesis that dumps each species' full anatomy and diet; read-only, float for display only, deterministic). Confirmed: aquatic life (the `swim` locomotion mode plus generated oceans), flying life (`fly`/`glide` plus magical `levitate`/`blink`), carnivorous plants (an emergent label, any autotroph that also draws on a prey species, kingdom from autotrophy not diet, so even a walking or teleporting plant stays a plant), magical plants and animals (the `fantasy` body-plan kinds `mana-lash`/`ember-breath`/`frost-fang`/`curse-touch`/`mana-ward`/`stone-skin`/`phase-hide`/`mana-sight`/`aura-sense`/`levitate`/`blink`, drawn only on a magic WorldProfile), and anatomy-drives-ability (a structured BodyPlan of weapons, covering, senses, locomotion, temperament, and mass; function derived from tissue composition; edibility a per-eater relation). A 160-generation magical run grew 960 species (852 alive) across 15 regions with a four-level food web (carnivores that eat carnivores) and full determinism. HONEST FINDING to fold into the biosphere-into-the-run addendum: morphology-to-role coherence is loose. The food web assigns what a species IS, but the niche/trophic role does not yet strongly constrain the body-plan draw, so a rooted plant can roll antlers and echolocation and an autotroph can roll blink. Tightening the niche-and-trophic constraint on the body-plan sample (so a plant's body fits a plant's life, pruned further by selection once the biosphere is wired into a running world) is a follow-on sub-item of the biosphere addendum. (SUPERSEDED 2026-07-05: the fix is not a tightened catalog draw but grow-not-draw, goal 4b in the arc-order entry below, where each biosphere species grows its body from its genome through the morphogen substrate and selection prunes, so a plant's body fits a plant's life because it emerged and was selected, never because the sample was constrained.) Gate: the addendum in the hand-over text; biosphere_probe.rs for re-inspection.

The emergent-anatomy / morphogenesis arc is fully scoped in `docs/working/EMERGENT_ANATOMY_HANDOFF.md` (owner ruling: THE next arc after the base-liveliness arc lands and is tested, and BEFORE the biosphere-into-the-run addendum). It retires the authored `BodyPlanRegistry` parts catalog and the `F_*` function tags for a generative developmental substrate whose part function (weapon, sense, locomotion, covering, magic) is DERIVED from grown physics through the composition-evaluator pattern, unifying biosphere and sentient bodies, with magic recast as a reserved thaumic floor (a `thaum:i8` physics dimension) a tissue couples to rather than a `fantasy:bool` catalog flag. Incremental: (1) derive function from material+geometry not the labeled kind; (2) a real developmental program grows structure from the genome; (3) selection prunes incoherent bodies. Affordable via a three-tier species-archetype content-id cache. Recommended first step: generalize the compose leaf's function dispatch and retire the `F_*` tags, the smallest change that proves the thesis. STEP 1 LANDING (gate: PR #91, review/gating surface): the function-law dispatch is built (`crates/compose/src/capability.rs`: PIERCE/LOCOMOTE/REFRACT kernels, `FunctionLawRegistry`, `derive_capabilities`); the individual-tier `F_STRIKE`/`F_SIGHT`/`F_LOCOMOTION` tags are retired and `Body::can_strike`/`can_move`/`can_sense` derive from grown physics (`crates/sim/src/body.rs`, gated 1b/1d); the run-path `MorphCategory` affordance gate is retired for a capability-derived MOVE/STRIKE gate (`crates/sim/src/homeostasis.rs`, gated 1e, hash-neutral); and the `sqrt(body_mass)` `locomotion_speed` proxy is retired for grown-limb physics (stride from the LOCOMOTE limb's `mech.arm_length` scaled by its structural capability; `crates/sim/src/locomotion.rs`, 1e-speed, hash re-baselines, R-BEHAVIOR-EVOLVE fixtures re-tuned deliberately). STEP 2 SLICE A LANDING (gate: PR #91): the `Channel::Morphogen` genome channel and the developmental-growth kernel are built, unit-proven and OFF the run path (hash-neutral), per the gate's cadence. `crates/sim/src/morphogen.rs` grows a `Structure` (a graph of `Segment`s each carrying `mech.*` geometry and `mat.*`/`opt.*` material) from a genome's expressed growth program under bounded, integer Fixed-point recursion, counter-keyed on a new `Phase::MORPHOGEN` (0x1B) with declared R-RNG-COORD slots, hard-capped in depth and segment count (a termination guarantee), folded into `state_hash` in canonical order; the Step-1 function-law dispatch reads each grown segment's function unchanged (a grown weapon reads PIERCE, a limb LOCOMOTE, an eye REFRACT, blind to any id). The growth program is heritable through `Channel::Morphogen(MorphogenParamId)` (`crates/sim/src/genome.rs`: `append_morphogen_block`) expressed by the existing `GeneSet::express`, so a body's SHAPE drifts/recombines/mutates/promotes through the pool with no per-channel code. STEP 2 SLICE B1 LANDING (gate: PR #91, hash-neutral): the digest and the direct-read bridge, unit-proven and off the run path, on the owner's slice-B ruling (2026-07-05: read the grown Structure DIRECTLY on the body, retire the kind-id registry indirection for grown bodies, not intern into the catalog; and split digest+bridge first, then the run wiring). `Structure::digest() -> BodyPlan` is the LOD-0 aggregate (body_mass from the grown structure's extent; the part-lists empty because a grown body's function is read from the structure, not the catalog part-lists; temperament and metabolic organs supplied by the caller in the documented hybrid). `AffordanceRegistry::afforded_structure` (homeostasis.rs) and `locomotion::locomotion_speed_structure` read a grown body's MOVE/STRIKE affordance and ground speed from the structure's segment capabilities directly, no organs registry, no kind id. STEP 2 SLICE B2a LANDING (gate: PR #91, hash-neutral): the run-read plumbing, split from the growth. `Walker` gains an `Option<Structure>` field (`crates/sim/src/locomotion.rs`; `with_structure` builder, not folded into `state_hash` directly since a static derived body folds only through the dynamic state it drives) and the run reads route through it: `step_with_field_dirs`'s affordance and speed reads, and the runner's exertion-drain velocity, use `afforded_structure` / `locomotion_speed_structure` when the walker carries a grown structure, else the catalog path. Hash-neutral (every existing walker carries `None`, so the catalog path is unchanged); proven by a test that a walker whose GROWN structure is rooted stays put though its catalog body is a walker, and one whose grown structure bears a limb moves. STEP 2 SLICE B2b LANDING (gate: PR #91, the payoff, hash-changing for a morphogen race only): a founder's run-body is now GROWN from its own genome at genesis, and the run reads it. `Race::with_morphogen(program)` (`crates/sim/src/race.rs`, an `Option<MorphogenProgram>` sibling to `Race::body`, fail-quiet-until-declared, opt-in per race) declares a developmental program; at the founder assembly (`worldbuild.rs assemble_dawn_embodiment`) and the newborn pairing (`runner.rs embody_newborn`), when the race carries a program the walker's grown structure is `grow(express_program(program, race.genes, world.genome_of(id)), seed, id)` handed via `Walker::with_structure` (the newborn keys on `emb.seed`), a pure function of `(program, genome, seed, id)` reproduced on replay and on a two-tier reload (walkers are regrown from the re-minted genome, never serialized). Genesis seeding is `append_morphogen_block` after `append_controller_block`, feeding `Channel::Morphogen`, promoting and evolving through the existing pool. The gate directed retiring the race-uniform `race.body.clone()`; this retires the RUN-GOVERNING body (per-member, genome-derived) while KEEPING the catalog `body` as the LOD-0 metabolic aggregate, a code-grounded scoped seam surfaced for the gate: `Structure::digest()` endows no organs (a grown segment carries `mech/mat/opt` function-geometry, not the `bio.*` organ kinds the reserves are sourced from), and `Homeostasis::new` sums reserve capacity over `body.organs`, so a founder metabolised off the digest would starve at birth; deriving the metabolic tier from grown physics is the Step 3 boundary. Blind concept-verification green (`world_build.rs a_founders_genome_grows_a_locomotor_the_catalog_body_lacks`): a race whose catalog body is rooted but whose genome grows a limb disperses on that grown locomotor (a limb the catalog never had), the no-limb control stays put, the run replays bit for bit, matches the scheduled order, and a rebuild plus a regrow-from-re-minted-genome reproduce each grown structure byte-identically. The opt-in guard keeps every catalog scenario hash-neutral (590 lib + all integration binaries green, no existing hash moved). B2b SIGNED OFF (gate, 2026-07-05): the thesis live, determinism and save/load nailed (regrowth from the re-minted genome), the metabolic-tier seam accepted as the correct Step 3 boundary; directive to proceed to Step 3 (viability cull plus metabolic-tier grow), the metabolic-grow scope call relayed to the owner. STEP 3 SLICE 1 LANDING (gate: PR #91, the viability cull, hash-neutral for existing scenarios): an audit-the-input catch first, the handoff's Step-3 mechanism ("generalize `birth_viable` ... dies through the runtime `Stock` collapse cull") rests on a premise that does not hold, `birth_viable` is test-only (no runtime or pool wiring) and that `Stock` cull is the pre-dawn pool tier not wired to morphogen growth; grown bodies live at the run/individual tier. Owner ruling on the surfaced fork: functional viability at the run tier. `Structure::whole_body_viability(fns, refs, caps)` (`crates/sim/src/morphogen.rs`) is the greatest capability any grown segment reads on ANY function law, a pure physics read over the same per-segment dispatch the affordance and speed reads use, blind to id; a body reading no viable function reads zero. The run sets a grown being's derived INTEGRITY reserve to this each tick (`runner.rs step_embodiment` block 1a, mirroring the TEMPERATURE-from-body-core-temp set), gated on the registry carrying the integrity axis and the walker carrying a grown structure, so a catalog body and a registry without integrity (every existing run scenario) are untouched (opt-in, hash-neutral). An incoherent grown body's integrity falls through the reserved death floor and it dies through the SAME `is_alive` to `metabolize` to `reconcile_lifecycle` to `remove_being` path as any other death, with no predicate that inspects morphology to reject (Principle 8). Proven: a morphogen unit test (functional body positive, all-zero body zero) and a dawn-run test (`world_build.rs an_incoherent_grown_body_is_culled_through_the_ordinary_reserve_floor_path`) where one race id's founders survive when their genome grows a viable limb and are culled when it grows an inert body, opposite verdicts for one race id proving the cull reads grown physics never a RaceId (Principle 9), replaying bit for bit; full sim suite green (591 lib + all integration binaries, no existing hash moved). Reserved-with-basis: the integrity axis's death floor for a grown body (the minimum whole-body functional capability sustaining any life function, dev fixture 1/32). Slice 1 SIGNED OFF (gate, 2026-07-05), the audit-the-input catch praised. STEP 3 SLICE 2 LANDING (gate: PR #91, the metabolic-tier grow; owner ruled "Metabolic grow if the q failed" when the interactive scope-ask channel failed in the async webhook context; hash-neutral for existing scenarios): a race that declares a developmental program and NO catalog body founds embodied members whose metabolism is sourced from their grown tissue, so the catalog metabolic body retires for a grown race. 2a (the read, off-path): `MorphogenProgram` gains a `bio_axes` vector (`bio.energy_density`, `bio.water_fraction`) whose parameters sit after branch/spawn so no existing index shifts; `grow` writes the bio composition into the per-segment material map (metabolic-only, blind to the function-law dispatch); `Structure::backed_capacity(axis_id)` sums the reserve capacity a grown body's tissue backs (Σ per-segment-development times composition, direct off segments, no organ kind id); `Homeostasis::from_structure(reg, structure)` builds the reserve set from grown tissue. 2b (the wiring): the `race.body` guard at `worldbuild.rs assemble_dawn_embodiment` and `runner.rs embody_newborn` is relaxed (embody if a catalog body OR a program); a catalog-body race keeps its catalog reserves (byte-identical, including the B2b hybrids), a fully grown race sources body (digest) and reserves (`from_structure`) from its structure; and `derive_base_drain`/`derive_exertion_coupling` take `energy_density` as a caller-supplied parameter (a grown body from `Structure::whole_body_energy_density`, a catalog body from `whole_body_energy_density` over organs) so a fully grown body metabolizes off its grown tissue instead of starving on the empty digest's zero energy density, byte-identical for catalog scenarios. Blind-verify (`world_build.rs a_fully_grown_race_founds_bodies_with_no_catalog_body_and_starves_without_grown_tissue`): a race with no catalog body founds eight embodied members (grown body, no catalog organs); a nourished grown founder survives on its grown reserves, an energy-less one starves through the ordinary cull, replaying bit for bit. Full sim suite green (593 lib plus all 36 integration binaries, no existing hash moved). Honest limit: the reserve and the drain's energy density are grown; the remaining derived-physiology reads (convective surface, muscle force, specific heat, thermal exchange) still read the empty digest and degrade to safe zeros, the follow-on. Slice 2 CODE-VERIFIED (gate) and held for owner scope; the owner ruled (2026-07-05): affirm the metabolic scope, grow the derived physiology in-arc, and route scope through the PR handback. STEP 3 SLICE 3 LANDING (gate: PR #91, the derived-physiology grow, hash-neutral for catalog scenarios): a fully grown body's thermoregulatory drain, exertion, and body-medium thermal exchange now read its exposed surface, muscle strength, and specific heat off its OWN grown tissue, so it is no longer thermally inert or exertion-free. 3a (read, off-path): the `MorphogenProgram`'s `bio_axes` is generalized to `composition_axes` (holding `mat.*`/`therm.*` metabolic axes too); `dev_default` gains `bio.convective_surface`, `mat.fracture_strength`, `therm.specific_heat` placed before energy/water so the reserve-backing axes stay addressable (hash-neutral, confirmed by replay); `Structure::composition_sum` (extensive) and `composition_mean` (intensive) generalize the reads, `backed_capacity` and `whole_body_energy_density` delegate. 3b (wire): `derive_base_drain`/`derive_body_exchange_rate` keep their catalog signatures (no test churn) and delegate to `base_drain_from`/`body_exchange_rate_from` cores taking the composition scalars explicitly, supplied by the caller from a catalog organ set or a grown structure; `being_derived_drains` and a `walker_exchange_rate` helper source surface/energy-density/muscle-force and the exchange rate from the grown structure when present, byte-identical for catalog bodies. Proven (`world_build.rs a_fully_grown_bodys_derived_physiology_is_read_from_its_grown_tissue`): a physiology-seeded fully grown founder's structure reads a positive surface, muscle strength, and specific heat directly with no catalog organs, and on the run the grown surface is load-bearing (a physiological body pays the thermoregulatory drain and does not outlast the run while the surfaceless one survives, opposite outcomes for one race id). Full sim suite green (36 binaries, no existing hash moved). Honest limit: the respiratory surface (used only with the RESPIRATION axis, absent from dev scenarios) still reads the catalog path, the same pattern when a grown race uses respiration. With this a grown race's body, function, metabolism, and physiology are all grown from its genome, the catalog body retired for a grown race. Remaining: (owner scope permitting) the thaumic-floor track, before the arc merges.

Blind concept verification is the standing acceptance test (AGENTIC_ADDENDUM.md section 8): every concept the base-liveliness and emergent-anatomy arcs wire (movement, scarcity biting, conversation and belief spread, promotion arcs, derived part function, and the rest) is validated by handing a blind agent the concept as a plain claim plus a deterministic run log, with no code, and confirming the concept manifests in the behaviour rather than only in the source. It caught that conversation was inert and unobserved in the first wired runs (the belief stances were race-clustered inheritance, not live transmission), so each arc's observable milestone is not done until a blind concept-verification run confirms it.

Arc order after the base-liveliness arc (owner rulings 2026-07-04, updated 2026-07-05): (1) the emergent-anatomy / morphogenesis arc (docs/working/EMERGENT_ANATOMY_HANDOFF.md), LANDED and merged (PR #91); then (2) the HARM-LEARNING arc (docs/working/HARM_LEARNING_HANDOFF.md, the experiential-learning plus belief-to-behaviour closer, LANDED and merged (PR #92), owner-ruled 2026-07-05 to land BEFORE materials, because a world whose beings cannot learn "this place harms me" and step around it is a mind without cognition, and the acceptance gate named belief persistence the single most important gap); then, all depending on the above, (3) the MATERIAL SUBSTRATE arc, a large arc that gives the world MATTER (substance in the ground, resources as structured objects, carriable matter, crafting, modifiable terrain, live fire, shelter, and the closed matter cycle), from which mining, harvesting, gathering, tool-making, building, hoarding, trade, and settlement emerge, the bridge from the ecological world to the civilizational one (held in the session's material-substrate directive; depends on the environmental fields from liveliness and the physics-derived affordances from anatomy); (4) the BIOSPHERE-INTO-THE-RUN arc (formal goal expanded 2026-07-05), which has two intertwined halves and is one arc, not two: (4a) SEED THE RUN WORLD WITH THE LIVING BIOSPHERE, so the run's abstract regrowing food stock (the `bio.energy_density` field beings currently graze as a bare number, since the run harness seeds only sentient DawnPeoples and skips `genesis()`) becomes the biomass of actual organisms and beings forage, hunt, and compete within a living ecology of producers, prey, and predators rather than over a field of numbers; and (4b) GROW EACH BIOSPHERE SPECIES' BODY FROM ITS GENOME through the same morphogen substrate the dawn founders already use (retiring `sample_body_plan` and the catalog `BodyPlan` for the biosphere in `biosphere.rs` and `genesis.rs`, which the emergent-anatomy arc never touched), so convergent and divergent morphology EMERGES across the radiation and selection prunes, closing the emergent-anatomy arc's stated goal of unifying biosphere and sentient bodies under one generative substrate (the half that did not land, since that arc grew only the opt-in dawn tier). Goal 4b SUPERSEDES the earlier "tighten the niche/trophic constraint on the catalog body-plan draw" follow-on (the loose morphology-to-role finding above) with grow-not-draw: a plant's body fits a plant's life because it grew from a genome and was pruned by its niche through selection, never because the catalog sample was constrained. The two halves are one arc because a living ecology is made of matter (plants are harvestable, prey are meat, corpses decay), so 4a rides the material substrate (3) and 4b rides the morphogen substrate from anatomy (1). Then (5) the communication-reach substrate (recorded in the anatomy handoff). Each behaviour in the material arc is emergent (need plus physics-derived affordance plus structured matter, never scripted) and gated by blind concept verification.

The read-no-high-level-fact gate (owner ruling 2026-07-04, now CLAUDE.md prime directive 4): if a proposed substrate reads a high-level social or emergent fact (genetic relatedness, family or group membership, a named emotion, a skill or status level) to produce a behaviour, it is authoring, and it is replaced by the general causal primitive plus a proxy that correlates so the outcome emerges from selection (kin-biased cooperation from helping the familiar-and-nearby, not from reading relatedness). It is a standing steering-audit gate on every arc, sibling to the blind concept-verification acceptance test. Consequence: the social layer (cooperation, family, specialization, affect, cumulative culture, and the governance, economy, religion, status, war, and cities that stand on them) is an EMERGENT LAYER over the individual, cultural, and material substrates plus selection, mostly not an arc of new mechanisms. The only missing pieces are a few general physical or biological primitives, not social ones: the real dependency of the young, lifetime use-dependent plasticity, and a rich-enough internal appraisal state for affect. The earlier social-fabric-arc framing is superseded by this general-primitives framing, held in the session's emergent-social directive.
