## Base-liveliness landed; belief-transmission finding (2026-07-04)

The base-liveliness arc merged (PR #89, all five steps plus the arc-scoped promotion policy and a self-run blind-audit remediation; new crates/sim/src/environ.rs). Verified green on CPU (579 sim tests) and on the 5090 GPU oracle (every gate, including the field-step and diffusion oracles the new environmental stack rides, bit-identical). The world is now alive and BOUNDED: beings disperse, scarcity bites locally (grazing pressure ~95% where beings graze), population self-bounds near 55 with births balancing deaths (the old unbounded 24->4090 is gone), salt tolerance selects up near salt (a gradient, not a gate), individuals live promoted survival arcs, and a hazard belief spreads by movement-coupled gossip.

Blind concept-verification acceptance gate (AGENTIC_ADDENDUM.md section 8) run on the wired concepts: MOVEMENT is PARTIAL (beings move but cluster onto resource cells rather than disperse across the world, max displacement pinned at 4); SCARCITY is PARTIAL (food-scarcity strongly realized, but water is a static field not a consumed resource, and death cause is untagged); CONVERSATION is NOT REALIZED (a belief spreads to ~12% of the founding cohort then decays to 0% by gen 3 and never circulates). Recorded follow-ons: water as a live consumed resource, death-cause tagging plus a tick-0 baseline for observability, and the dispersal max-displacement question. Note: the dev harness only differentiates scenarios on demographic postures (confluence and mirror produce an identical hash).

Belief transmission (branch claude/belief-transmission, held for owner direction). Root-caused why the learned salt-flat hazard belief decays to zero: NOT forgetting (zero within-mind decay; a committed belief holds for life, world.rs evidence intake is purely additive) and NOT a high commit bar (a single gossip reception commits a co-located listener), but transmission never reaching the next cohort. Fixed the transmission substrate (world.rs fn gossip): fan-out overhearing (a speaker's committed beliefs reach every co-located listener in id order, not one random draw, the multi-party overhearing follow-on), cross-promotion flow (a promoted holder reaches its non-promoted co-located listeners so a belief is not trapped among the promoted; test a_promoted_speaker_reaches_a_nonpromoted_listener_by_gossip updated), and committed_beliefs so the max-keyed hazard belief is not masked. Green (579 tests). But this did NOT make the salt-flat belief persist: the real blocker is spatial and behavioural, not transmission rate. The beings who learn the lesson are the ones who wandered onto the salt flats (marginal, low-food ground), so they die of scarcity fast and are isolated from the reproducing core, a lesson learned by the doomed. Co-located birth (a newborn born at its parent's live cell) was tried and REVERTED: it did not rescue the belief and it regressed the bounded-population win (the bound leaned on newborns dispersing to marginal death). THE REAL CLOSER for conversation persistence is belief->behavior coupling (a being that believes the salt is dangerous avoids it, survives, and carries the lesson to the populated core), so a belief persists because it is adaptive, never because its inheritance is authored (the emergent-social principle). Flagged as the genuine next step for the conversation concept, ahead of or alongside the emergent-anatomy arc per owner direction.

Belief transmission, resolution (2026-07-04). The transmission-substrate improvement SHIPS: gossip fan-out overhearing (a speaker's committed beliefs reach every co-located listener in canonical id order, not one random draw), cross-promotion belief flow (a promoted holder reaches its non-promoted co-located listeners), and committed_beliefs so the max-keyed hazard belief is not masked (world.rs fn gossip; test a_promoted_speaker_reaches_a_nonpromoted_listener_by_gossip). This is the multi-party overhearing follow-on and the right mechanism for when a belief forms and needs to travel. It does NOT close the conversation-persistence concept, and forcing it closed was rejected as steering: an observational death-mark (a corpse proxy on the Trace substrate, dropped at a dead being's band so the whole band learns) was built and REVERTED because beings do not die in the flats (instrumented: 125 deaths, 0 on hazard cells; the salt is a chronic condition drain, not an acute kill), and making the flats acutely lethal to force corpses is authoring the outcome. The deeper finding, owner-identified: even the current first-hand belief formation is authored, the engine INJECTS the hazard belief when a being stands on salt (runner.rs couple_conversation Observe), the being never reasons it. THE REAL CLOSER is a general EXPERIENTIAL / ASSOCIATIVE-LEARNING primitive: a being correlates its own interoceptive harm signal (falling condition) with a perceived external feature (the ground it is on) and forms the belief itself (I am harmed here, not there), then acts on it and transmits it. Nothing hazard-specific; it learns any hazard, any good place, any food that sickens, the same way. This supersedes the injected first-hand formation and is the substrate that makes belief->behavior real. It is a later-arc capability (the deliberative/experiential-reasoning layer), deferred, not hacked. Observational learning from corpses returns as a secondary path when the material-substrate arc gives literal, decaying corpses. Sequence unchanged: ship overhearing, proceed to the emergent-anatomy arc, and queue experiential/associative learning plus belief->behavior as the conversation-persistence closer.

The harm-learning arc is fully scoped in docs/working/HARM_LEARNING_HANDOFF.md (owner ruling 2026-07-05: lands BEFORE the material-substrate arc). It closes the conversation-persistence gap the acceptance gate named #1, by building one general experiential-learning primitive plus belief-to-behaviour: a being correlates its own interoceptive harm signal (a raw reserve delta) with a raw perceived feature of the cell it stands on, forms the belief itself (retiring the injected HAZARD Observe at runner.rs couple_conversation), acts on it (a belief-derived expected-harm gradient enters the evolved controller as a weighted input so avoidance emerges from selection, never an authored branch), survives because of it, and the belief then persists because it is adaptive and rides the shipped overhearing transmission, never authored inheritance. The associative learner IS the existing evidence engine rekeyed on a per-feature subject, so the substrate needs little structural change. Four slices on the read-then-wire cadence: (a) the interoceptive delta + raw feature percept; (b) the associative learner, retiring the injection; (c) belief-to-behaviour; (d) persistence emerges, with the acceptance being a blind concept-verification that a belief forms from experience, guides avoidance, raises survival, persists across generations, and dies out if the hazard is removed. Recommended first slice: (a). The observability event-stream (below) makes the loop legible and the slice-d acceptance reader depends on it.

Observability gap (branch claude/observability, part 1 merged to main 2026-07-05). The blind concept-verification acceptance gate on the wired package found all four wired concepts PARTIAL: the substrates hold, the payoffs do not, and three of the four causal cores were NOT OBSERVABLE from per-snapshot aggregates (scarcity as the agent of checking, individual-to-individual belief transmission, promotion-on-struggle). Closing that gap with a per-being event stream, all non-canonical and NOT folded into state_hash (a pure read of already-folded state, hash-neutral, verified). Part 1 merged as the harm-learning arc base: the migration reader firmed (occupied cells reported against the 768-cell world extent, plus mean displacement alongside max, so a tight clump is unmistakable from a spread), and a cause-of-death reader (runner.obs_deaths tallies the reserve axis behind each locomotion death via Homeostasis::dead_axis, drained by the harness) which shows the crucible deaths are STARVATION, so scarcity as the killer is now observable, not inferred. Part 2 folds into the harm-learning arc's slice d: a belief-transmission event count (source-to-recipient tells fired, so beings-in-contact conveying a belief is observable even when the standing holder fraction is zero) and named promotion/demotion events tied to condition.

HARM-LEARNING SLICE (a1) LANDING (branch claude/harm-learning, hash-neutral, off the run path): the read half of slice (a), the interoceptive delta and the raw perceived-feature substrate, built as pure mechanism and unit-proven with no run-path touch, so no scenario hash moves (601 sim lib tests plus the world_build replay-bit-for-bit suite green). New module crates/sim/src/percept.rs: a data-defined PerceptRegistry (class-string keyed, sibling to the homeostatic and affordance registries, EMPTY by default so a world declaring no percepts grows the controller not at all), PerceptRegistry::perceive reads the raw amount of each declared class off a cell's Composition in canonical id order (the valence-blind feature percept, via the new Composition::sensed helper that reads a substance whether the floor filed it nutrient or toxin), and feature_bucket floor-quantizes a raw feature to the perceptual grid (the stable key a per-feature belief subject is minted from in slice b). crates/sim/src/homeostasis.rs: ReserveMemory retains the previous-tick per-axis level so delta(axis) = level_now - level_prev is a pure fixed-point subtraction (CONDITION's delta nets condition_recovery - harm for free, generalized to any reserve), and is_harm_tick classifies a fall beyond the harm-noise floor as harm. Reserved-with-basis surfaced early for the owner to rule on before the learner consumes them (slice b): the feature granularity (basis: the sensorium's per-class just-noticeable difference, coarse enough that ordinary spatial variation in a hazard reads as one kind) and the harm-noise floor (basis: the largest per-tick reserve fall a resting unharmed body incurs, so only a fall beyond ordinary living registers as harm). Next: slice (a2), the one hash-changing commit, grows the controller feature block (opt-in, empty-default hash-neutral) and folds the ReserveMemory into state_hash.

HARM-LEARNING SLICE (a2) LANDING (branch claude/harm-learning, the one hash-changing commit, opt-in so existing scenarios are byte-identical): the controller feature block grows and the run feeds it, and the interoceptive delta memory folds into state_hash, all gated on a world declaring percepts. crates/sim/src/controller.rs: ControllerLayout gains an n_features field and a with_percepts constructor (ControllerLayout::new delegates to it with an empty registry, so every existing call site is unchanged); the feature block sits between the per-axis blocks and the bias, so axis_input_base and the bias-as-last-input convention the seed helpers use both hold, and build_input delegates to a new build_input_with_features that writes the feature channels and keeps the bias at n_in - 1 (byte-identical for zero features). A founder expresses zero for the new feature weights, so the percept has no behavioural effect until selection lifts a weight (the emergent pattern). crates/sim/src/locomotion.rs: Walker carries a ReserveMemory, snapshotted at the TOP of each body-tick (so the delta read after metabolism is the tick's net change), gated on percepts non-empty; step_with_field_dirs takes the PerceptRegistry, perceives the cell's features, and feeds build_input_with_features. crates/sim/src/runner.rs: Embodiment carries the PerceptRegistry with a set_percepts opt-in setter that REBUILDS the layout (set before the beings are built, like set_organs/set_physiology); the embodiment step passes it; state_hash folds each being's ReserveMemory prev levels after the hidden state, only when non-empty (so an opted-out run folds nothing). Milestone proven (locomotion.rs the_feature_channel_and_interoceptive_delta_are_read_on_the_flat): declaring one percept grows n_in by exactly one, a being on the salt flat reads the raw bio.salinity dose in its controller feature block, and its interoceptive CONDITION delta goes negative as the salt wears it, replaying bit for bit. Determinism proven (physiology_embodiment.rs the_interoceptive_delta_fold_is_deterministic_and_scheduler_invariant): with percepts declared, the coupled runner is bit-identical across runs and between the pinned order and the scheduler variant, so the new fold is worker-width invariant. Full sim suite green (602 lib plus all integration binaries), no existing hash moved (the feature block and the delta snapshot are both opt-in). Next: slice (b), the associative learner that forms the belief from the delta and the feature, retiring the injected HAZARD Observe.

HARM-LEARNING SLICE (b) LANDING (branch claude/harm-learning): the associative learner forms the belief and the injected HAZARD Observe is retired, so a being reasons the belief for itself. b1 (read, off run path, hash-neutral): crates/sim/src/learn.rs (new) is the experiential associative-learning substrate, the existing evidence engine keyed differently. HARM_ATTR is the one generic "does this feature harm me" attribute; feature_subject(channel, bucket) mints a per-feature belief subject in a reserved band packed above every being id and below the reserved-high landmark ids; feature_observations() produces, per PRESENT feature of the cell, one piece of evidence toward HARMS (a harm tick) or BENIGN (a harm-free tick), weighted by good_weight of two reserved likelihoods and scaled by the being's plasticity. HarmLearningCalib carries the reserved-with-basis calibs that REPLACE the retired hazard calibs (harm-noise floor, feature granularity, the two harm likelihoods, the certainty clamp set equal to the evidence log-odds clamp). Unit-proven: a mind fed repeated harm-while-on-a-feature commits HARMS on its own, a being never on the feature never forms it, harm-free ticks self-correct to BENIGN (the falsifier for free). b2 (wire, the hash change for a percept-declaring run): couple_conversation replaces the salinity-dose injection with the learner (harm = any reserve fell beyond the noise floor via the reserve-memory delta; features = percepts.perceive of the current cell; observations pushed as Observe TickInputs through the existing consider path, scaled by the being's Mind::plasticity); the HAZARD_* constants, ENV_HAZARD_ORDINAL, and LivelinessCalib.hazard_dose_threshold/hazard_weight are retired (manifest hazard.* entries replaced by harm.* in reserved.toml and dev-fixtures.toml); the world-build declares the percept registry from the world's tolerance classes (PerceptRegistry::from_tolerances, data-driven, so a world with no declared toxins declares no percepts and the learner stays inert) and arms HarmLearningCalib from the manifest; the run_world reader is repointed from the hazard subject to any committed HARM_ATTR->HARMS feature belief, and the dawn hazard seed is retired. Confirmed live on the crucible (20-gen run): a being forms a learned feature-harm belief for itself with no injected observation, and it spreads 6% to 33% as the origin cohort's belief rides gossip. The world_build determinism suite stays green (empty tolerances -> empty percepts -> learner inert -> hash-neutral); a structural test asserts no HAZARD_* remains on the runner's canonical path. Honest limit: belief holders are few because the beings that learn are the marginal ones on the flats who die before the belief pays off; that anti-adaptive gap is what slice (c) belief-to-behaviour and slice (d) persistence close. Next: slice (c), the belief-derived avoidance gradient as an evolved controller input.

HARM-LEARNING SLICE (c) LANDING (branch claude/harm-learning): belief-to-behaviour, avoidance as an evolved weighted input (the S path). c1 (read, off run path, hash-neutral): crates/sim/src/learn.rs avoidance_gradient() sums the inverse-distance repulsion away from every cell within a being's sense range whose feature-kind it holds a committed HARMS belief about; the raw sum points away from the bulk of believed harm and the caller normalises it to a unit percept. It is a PERCEPT, not a heading: it reads the being's own beliefs and the raw features it senses, never a hazard label or a race id. Unit-proven: a being that learned the salt harms it reads a gradient pointing away (west when the salt is due east), a being that learned nothing reads zero, and a world with no percepts short-circuits to zero. c2 (wire into field_dirs): step_embodiment supplies the avoidance gradient through the EXISTING field_dirs map into CONDITION's already-allocated-but-dead direction slot (only where the world carries the being's mind and the registry the CONDITION axis; a zero gradient is not inserted). The gradient sums into the MOVE heading through the heritable CONDITION-dir-to-heading weights exactly as the temperature gradient does, so avoidance EMERGES when selection lifts those weights off founding-zero, with zero change to the controller mechanism and no harm term subtracted in the MOVE arm (Principle 9). Milestone proven (locomotion.rs the_belief_avoidance_gradient_steers_a_being_only_through_an_evolved_weight): given a westward avoidance gradient, a being whose evolved CONDITION-dir weight is non-zero steers away (west), while a blank being with the founding-zero weight ignores it and only explores, so avoidance appears only with the evolved weight, never authored. Determinism holds (world_build replay and scheduler-match, determinism_harness all green): the S path leaves n_in, weight_count, and the ControllerParamId space untouched, and for an opted-out scenario (empty percepts) the gradient short-circuits to zero so no CONDITION direction is inserted, hash-neutral. The generic field_dirs->controller->heading path the CONDITION gradient rides is the same one the temperature thermotaxis tests already prove. Honest limit: the founding seed leaves the CONDITION-dir weight at zero, so the crucible only diverges as mutation and selection lift that weight over generations; that emergence, and the persistence it buys, is what slice (d) measures. Next: slice (d), let persistence emerge, the acceptance instrumentation, and the blind concept-verification with the hazard-removal falsifier.

HARM-LEARNING SLICE (d) LANDING (branch claude/harm-learning): the acceptance. First an audit-the-run catch that the gate praised: b2 declared the percept registry but the founder controllers were still seeded and expressed against the pre-feature layout, so their forage weights were misplaced and founders barely foraged (the 164131f0 the gate signed off was a broken-foraging run). Fixed by aligning genesis-seed, founder-expression, and run on the one percept layout (worldbuild.rs set_percepts before the layout clone; run_world.rs dawn_layout carries the salinity percepts); hash-neutral for empty-percept scenarios (world_build 16 green), crucible re-baselines to 254bc17c. Two honest findings surfaced to the owner: (1) with foraging restored, good foragers avoid the barren flats and so rarely ENCOUNTER the hazard to learn it (the handoff's own prediction; the mechanism is correct, the default scenario just does not route beings through the hazard), and (2) the default small crucible's population collapses to extinction REGARDLESS of this arc (isolated against the pre-arc a2 commit, which collapses identically 18 to 0; a 36-founder run holds around 47), a pre-existing viability property. Owner/gate ruling: proceed with a controlled deterministic acceptance (B) showing the FULL loop, and flag the free-running-population form (A) plus the pre-existing collapse as a follow-on scenario-and-viability arc. The controlled acceptance (runner.rs tests) shows the whole thesis deterministically through the actual runner/world: LEARN (a_being_forms_the_harm_belief_through_the_runner: a being on a salt cell feels its own CONDITION fall, senses the salinity, and commits the belief for itself, no injection), FALSIFIER (same test: a fully tolerant being on the identical salt forms no belief, so the belief tracks felt harm, the separator from an injected belief), AVOID + SURVIVE (a_holder_that_avoids_the_hazard_outlives_a_naive_being_on_the_same_harm: two beings holding the same belief, only the one with the evolved CONDITION-dir weight steers off the salt and keeps its condition, so the belief pays off only through the evolved weight, no authored flight), and TRANSMIT (a_learned_feature_harm_belief_rides_the_shipped_gossip_to_a_co_located_naive_being: the learned belief, an ordinary (subject, attr) frame, rides the shipped overhearing to a co-located naive being by presence). 614 lib tests green. The blind concept-verification battery runs on this assembled acceptance. The arc's forward mechanism is complete and signed off (a through c plus the layout fix); the remaining owner-flagged item is the scenario-and-viability follow-on arc that lets persistence emerge in a free-running population.

HARM-LEARNING ARC MERGED to main 2026-07-05 (PR #92, merge commit 1c571df). The gate SIGNED OFF slice (d): it re-verified the founder-layout fix (opted-out scenarios hash-neutral, the crucible re-baselined to 254bc17c replay-identical, 781 tests green) and confirmed by reading the asserts that LEARN, the FALSIFIER (a fully tolerant being on the identical salt forms no belief, because is_harm_tick fires only on a reserve fall, the one result an inject-on-presence hardcode cannot produce), AVOID plus SURVIVE, and TRANSMIT are each tested through the real runner. The owner gave the merge go and the arc landed with a merge commit, and the session auto-unsubscribed from the PR. The gate's independence note is on record: the load-bearing verification is the direct real-runner acceptance (a builder-run panel on a builder-written log is not fully independent), and a fully independent blind panel on a NEUTRAL log-emitting run is a clean, non-blocking addition that rides with option (A). DEFERRED to the follow-on scenario-and-viability arc (owner-endorsed, gate-recommended): option (A), a scenario that routes a free-running population through the hazard so avoidance pays off and persistence emerges from selection (the default good foragers avoid the barren flats, so they rarely encounter the hazard); the pre-existing small-population collapse fix (the default small crucible goes extinct regardless of this arc, isolated against the pre-arc a2 commit); and observability part 2 (the transmission and promotion event stream). The next arc in the order is the MATERIAL SUBSTRATE arc (3) unless the owner takes the (A) follow-on first.
The material-substrate arc is fully scoped in docs/working/MATERIAL_SUBSTRATE_HANDOFF.md (the next arc, after harm-learning which merged as PR #92). Its one job: add MATTER as a data-defined MaterialField (a Coord3-keyed sibling of ResourceField carrying located substances off the physics floor), from which mining, harvesting, carrying, crafting, terrain-modification, fire, shelter, and the matter cycle EMERGE from the single equation need + physics-derived affordance + structured matter, never scripted. The eight-item cascade in dependency order: (1) substance-in-the-ground [the base and recommended first slice], (2) resources-as-objects, (3) carriable-matter [the hinge that unlocks the economy], (4) crafting via the provenance-blind derive_capabilities dispatch, (5) modifiable-terrain (an earthwork-delta field the hydrology recomputes against), (6) live-fire (a FIRE field in EnvironFields where spread and extinction emerge from combustion plus the temperature diffusion stencil), (7) shelter (a per-cell thermal-exchange attenuation), (8) the matter cycle closing the deferred trace follow-on; plus the riders (persistent object identity, force affordances DIG/EXTRACT as a new FRACTURE FunctionLaw). Read-then-wire slice cadence, opt-in so existing scenarios stay byte-identical. Feasibility favorable: the density/hardness axes, the cut/fracture/combustion laws, the hashed Coord3 field, the Substance registry, grown strength, StableId identity, and the affordance-by-derived-capability gate all exist; the unbuilt pieces are the tile-to-Substance material layer, inventory, vertical z-adjacency, worked-object wiring, the fire field, the terrain-delta field, and the hash extensions. OWNER-RULED (item 8, 2026-07-06, confirming the earlier lean): harden the closed DecayLaw enum to a data-defined TransformKindRegistry keyed to a physics kernel by id (sibling to the value/semantic/institution substrates), so decomposition, corrosion, combustion, cooking, and smelting are data rows over the fixed GENERAL-kernel set, never named-transform enum arms, with the no-registry north star (transforms emerge from the substance own physics) as the retirement target. Note: earlier the docs left this flagged-not-resolved while a verbal endorsement lived only in a memory and an agent relay; now formalized so the docs, memory, and agent agree (the agent caught the inconsistency per Prime Directive 1). Acceptance: a blind concept-verification per emergent behaviour on a run log (a being mines because it needs metal and can break rock, observed, not scripted). Recommended first slice: substance-in-the-ground, the READ half (the MaterialField and its registry-read hardness/density derivation, off the run path and hash-neutral).

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE SLICE 1 READ LANDING (branch claude/material-substrate, hash-neutral, off the run path). Cascade item 1 (substance in the ground) READ half, built as pure mechanism and unit-proven with no run-path touch, so no scenario hash moves (622 sim lib tests plus all integration binaries green, world_build and world_determinism replay bit-for-bit). New module crates/sim/src/material.rs: a MaterialField, a Coord3-keyed sibling of ResourceField, whose per-cell SubstanceMix maps a physics Substance id to the VOLUME of that substance present; the cell's bulk density and indentation hardness are DERIVED by reading a &PhysicsRegistry (the volume-weighted mean of the substance rows' mat.density and mat.indentation_hardness, reducing to a pure substance's own value for a single-substance cell), never stored on the tile, and the cell's matter MASS is the volume-weighted density sum the carry and extraction contests weigh. take and deposit are id-sorted sequential draws with no fresh RNG (the ResourceField::take discipline), and hash_into is DEFINED in canonical (Coord3, substance-id, volume) order but not yet called on the run path, so the substrate is hash-neutral until the wiring slice folds it into state_hash. Grounding finding that shaped the slice: the running sim world carries no PhysicsRegistry (physics is used only through civsim_physics::laws kernels), so the derivation takes the registry as a parameter exactly as ResourceField::source takes a HomeostaticRegistry, which keeps the READ half off the run path and defers threading a registry into the World to the WIRE slice. Steering: a matter kind is a Substance TOML row not a Material enum (P8), properties are registry-derived not tile-stored (P11), and the derivation reads only substance ids and floor axis ids, never a race, kind, or role (P9). No new reserved value (mat.density and mat.indentation_hardness are already SET floor data). The volume-weighted-mean aggregation over a mixture is the stated modelling choice, surfaced for the gate; item 4 may specialise the extraction contest's read (for example the dominant or hardest constituent) when it wires mining. Next: slice 1 WIRE, worldgen fills the empty z-column from substance rows and the MaterialField folds into state_hash behind the opt-in empty-default so existing scenarios stay byte-identical, then the first observable milestone, an extraction contest reading a cell's derived hardness, behind the flag. Slice 1 READ SIGNED OFF (gate, PR #93, 2026-07-05): steering clean (P8, P9, P11 held exactly), determinism verified (the crucible unchanged at 254bc17c), the grounding catch (no PhysicsRegistry in the running world, so the registry is a parameter) praised, no new reserved value. GATE NOTE CARRIED TO ITEM 4: the volume-weighted mean is physically correct for DENSITY (bulk density is total mass over total volume) but hardness does NOT average linearly, so when item 4 wires the extraction contest it must read the hardness the fracture law gates on (the load-bearing matrix or the hardest constituent, ore in rock breaks at the rock, not the composite mean); the bulk_hardness mean stands as a placeholder with no consumer until then.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE SLICE 1 WIRE LANDING (branch claude/material-substrate, the hash-changing fold, opt-in so existing scenarios are byte-identical). The located material substrate enters the canonical state. crates/sim/src/runner.rs: the Embodiment carries a material: MaterialField (EMPTY by default), with a set_material opt-in setter (like set_percepts and set_physiology, and needing no layout rebuild since matter does not touch the controller) and a material() read accessor; state_hash folds emb.material.hash_into beside emb.resources at the embodiment fold, in canonical (Coord3, substance-id, volume) order. An empty material layer (every existing scenario) folds no bytes, so the run is byte-identical (the opt-in empty default, the same shape as the harm-learning ReserveMemory fold); a populated layer is canonical dynamic state that will move, deposit, and deplete as the cascade wires up. Grounding: the fold needs NO PhysicsRegistry (it folds substance ids and volumes, not derived properties), so threading a registry into the World defers to item 4's first consumer of derived hardness. Determinism proven (physiology_embodiment.rs the_material_substrate_folds_into_state_hash_and_stays_deterministic): a runner carrying matter (a granite-and-soil ground cell plus a subsurface ore deposit) replays bit for bit and folds identically between the pinned order and the scheduler variant, and a populated layer changes the hash versus the empty opt-out, so the substrate is canonical and order-invariant. Full sim suite green (622 lib plus all 36 integration binaries, world_build and world_determinism unchanged, fmt and clippy and verify.sh clean). No new reserved value. Next: populate the ground (worldgen fills the empty z-column from real Substance rows added to the mechanical floor with cited density and hardness, opt-in per scenario), then item 3 carriable matter and item 4 the extraction contest that first reads a cell's derived hardness (reading the fracture-gating hardness per the gate's item-4 note, not the bulk mean).

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE GROUND VOCABULARY LANDING (branch claude/material-substrate, physics crate, hash-neutral for the sim). The substances a world's z-column is made of, plus a runtime loader for them. crates/physics/data/ground_floor.toml (new): granite, loam, clay, hematite, halite, each a real substance carrying its CITED bulk density (CRC Handbook; rock and soil mechanics references), and granite also carrying the rock-mechanics fracture, compressive, and tensile strengths the extraction contest reads (the fracture-gating strength per the gate's item-4 note). The ground floor EXTENDS the mechanical floor (the same way the fluids and optics floors add air and water) rather than editing it, so the mechanical floor's identity and its substance_count tests are untouched (this supersedes the WIRE-landing note that said the substances would be added to the mechanical floor). crates/physics/src/lib.rs: PhysicsRegistry::ground() builds the world material registry (the mechanical floor plus the ground substances) from the crate's EMBEDDED floor data via include_str!, so the sim's world-build obtains it with no filesystem path. Proven (floors.rs the_ground_floor_extends_the_mechanical_floor_with_cited_ground_substances): the ground registry loads, iron survives the extension, each ground substance reads back its cited density, granite carries its fracture strength, and the embedded build is content-hash-deterministic. No fabricated value: densities are cited, and each substance's mechanical-contest axes are added when the item that reads them is built (granite's now for the extraction contest; the dig and dissolve axes of soil, clay, and salt when items 5 and later read them). Physics suite green (all binaries), fmt and clippy clean. Next: thread PhysicsRegistry::ground() into the Embodiment (opt-in, hash-neutral, no fold), then worldbuild fills the z-column opt-in, then item 3 carriable matter and item 4 the extraction contest.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE GROUND POPULATION MECHANISM LANDING (branch claude/material-substrate, hash-neutral, off the default assembly path). The deterministic worldgen population of the ground. crates/sim/src/material.rs: a data-defined GroundProfile (a list of GroundLayers, each a substance id filling an inclusive z-band at a fixed volume; a new stratum is a data edit, never a Rock/Soil/Ore enum, P8 and P11) and GroundProfile::fill(width, height) -> MaterialField which deposits each stratum into every cell of its z-band in canonical (x, y, z) order with no randomness. GroundProfile::dev() is a labelled dev fixture (loam topsoil, granite bedrock, a hematite ore band within the bedrock, so a filled world exercises a single-substance cell and a mixed ore-in-rock cell). Off the default path (assemble_dawn_embodiment is unchanged), so a scenario that does not fill the ground stays empty and byte-identical; the WIRE fold carries a filled layer into state_hash when a scenario sets it. Proven: the fill places the expected substances and volumes deterministically, and an end-to-end test reads the placed substances' cited densities off PhysicsRegistry::ground() (a bedrock cell reads granite 2700, the ore band reads the granite-hematite mean 3980, the topsoil reads loam 1400). Full sim suite green (all lib plus 36 integration binaries, world_build and world_determinism unchanged, fmt and clippy and verify.sh clean). No new reserved value (the dev profile is a labelled fixture, the densities are the ground floor's cited data). Next: item 3 carriable matter (threading PhysicsRegistry::ground() into the Embodiment as its first consumer, to weigh a load's density) and item 4 the extraction contest (reading a cell's fracture-gating hardness).

GATE DIRECTION (PR #93, 2026-07-05): build ahead through the cascade toward the first observable milestone (a populated worldgen z-column plus an extraction contest reading a cell's derived hardness); the gate reviews the intervening slices in a batch as it catches up (it is mid-way through an independent blind concept-verification of the harm-learning arc on the owner's local model broker). Two things flag-and-hold rather than push past: a deliberate hash re-baseline (the first extraction milestone changes a material-declaring scenario's hash, which is fine, but keep it opt-in so every existing scenario stays byte-identical, and call it out when it lands) and any reserved physical constant (surface it reserved-with-basis, fail-loud, never fabricate). ITEM-8 OWNER RULING (carry to item 8, already decided so no hold): harden the DecayLaw seam to a data-defined TransformKindRegistry keyed to a physics kernel by id, each kernel a GENERAL physical law (oxidation, phase change, biological reduction), never a named-transform recipe (no combustion, cooking, or decay arms); the standing ideal is to need no registry at all, the transforms emerging from the substance's own physics, so build the registry as a thin dispatch over general kernels that could later dissolve into the floor.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 3 READ (carry-load weight primitive, branch claude/material-substrate, hash-neutral). The physics of a carried load's weight, the datum the carry limit contests. crates/sim/src/material.rs: SubstanceMix::weight(reg, gravity, force_max) = laws::weight(mass(reg), gravity, force_max), the load force a carried mixture exerts under gravity (density times volume times g, capped at the force ceiling), so a being can take up matter whose weight its grown whole-body muscle force covers and no more (the carry limit is grown strength versus derived weight, never a per-race carry table). Proven: a granite load of volume 2 weighs its derived mass 5400 at unit gravity, doubles under doubled gravity, caps at the force ceiling, and an empty carrier weighs nothing. Grounding for the run-path WIRE that follows: the carry capacity is whole_body_muscle_force(w.body, phys.organs, phys.anchors) (the Part 35 datum the run already computes at the exertion drain, runner.rs), the load is SubstanceMix::weight against the world gravity (a manifest value, the same datum the buoyancy physics reads) and the physics force ceiling; the run-path substrate (a Walker carried-load field folded into state_hash opt-in, id-sorted pick-up and put-down bounded by capacity, and the carried-weight to locomotion-cost coupling with a reserved load-penalty surfaced-with-basis) lands next. Full sim suite green, fmt and clippy clean, hash-neutral (the primitive has no run-path consumer yet).

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 3 SUBSTRATE (the carried-load field and its fold, branch claude/material-substrate, opt-in hash-neutral). The inventory the carry hinge binds to a carrier. crates/sim/src/locomotion.rs: Walker carries a carried: SubstanceMix (EMPTY by default), a mixture of substances by volume bound to the being. crates/sim/src/runner.rs: state_hash folds w.carried.hash_into after the reserve memory in canonical (substance-id, volume) order, gated on non-empty, so a being carrying nothing folds no bytes and every existing scenario is byte-identical (the same opt-in shape as the ReserveMemory fold). Determinism proven (physiology_embodiment.rs a_carried_load_folds_into_state_hash_and_stays_deterministic): a runner whose being bears a granite-plus-hematite load replays bit for bit and folds identically between the pinned order and the scheduler variant, and a carrying being changes the hash versus an empty one, so the load is canonical dynamic state. Full sim suite green (world_build and world_determinism unchanged), fmt and clippy clean. Next: the pick-up and put-down that move matter between the ground and the carrier, bounded by the being's whole_body_muscle_force capacity against SubstanceMix::weight (this threads the world gravity and the ground registry to the Embodiment as the first run-path consumer), then the carried-weight to locomotion-cost coupling (a reserved load-penalty surfaced-with-basis) so an over-laden being slows.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 3 ACTIONS (pick-up and put-down, the carry hinge comes alive; branch claude/material-substrate, opt-in hash-neutral). A being now moves matter between the ground and its carried load, bounded by its grown strength. crates/sim/src/runner.rs: the Embodiment gains an opt-in material_registry (PhysicsRegistry::ground() via set_material_registry, the first run-path consumer of a substance's derived properties); Embodiment::pick_up takes as much of a substance at a cell as the being's carry headroom bears (its whole-body muscle force minus the weight it already carries, over the substance's weight per unit volume), an id-keyed sequential draw with no fresh randomness; put_down deposits carried matter back at a coordinate. Carry capacity is being_muscle_force (a grown body sums its tissue's MUSCLE_STRENGTH scaled to mass, a catalog body reads its organs, the same read the exertion drain uses at runner.rs), the load's weight is SubstanceMix::weight against standard gravity (a cited physical constant 9.80665, not a reserved value per the gate) and the mech.force ceiling (a representability cap). Proven (physiology_embodiment.rs a_being_picks_up_and_puts_down_matter_bounded_by_its_grown_strength): a being with no material registry no-ops, a being with no muscle lifts nothing (zero capacity), a strong being lifts a positive but limited amount of a large granite heap and its strength is then spent (a second pick-up takes nothing, the bound was strength not availability), the ground loses exactly what was taken, and put-down restores it (conservation). Opt-in (no existing scenario declares a material registry or picks up), so world_build and world_determinism are unchanged and every existing scenario is byte-identical. Full sim suite green, fmt and clippy clean. No new reserved value (gravity is a physical constant, the force ceiling a representability cap, capacity and weight are derived). Next: the carried-weight to locomotion-cost coupling (a reserved load-penalty surfaced-with-basis, a deliberate opt-in hash re-baseline for carrying scenarios) so an over-laden being slows, closing item 3's milestone with a blind concept-verification; then item 4 the extraction contest.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 3 LOCOMOTION COUPLING (the carried-weight speed penalty; branch claude/material-substrate, DELIBERATE OPT-IN HASH RE-BASELINE for carrying scenarios only). A carried load now slows a being, closing the physical half of item 3's milestone. crates/sim/src/locomotion.rs: LocomotionParams gains a RESERVED load_penalty (basis: the fractional march-speed slowdown at the limit of what a body can bear, from the load-carriage literature; dev fixture 1 so a being at full capacity moves at half speed); step_with_field_dirs takes a per-walker load_factors map and divides the computed ground speed by the walker's factor (a factor of one, or an absent walker, is a no-op). crates/sim/src/runner.rs: the embodiment step precomputes each walker's load_factor = 1 + load_penalty * carried_weight / carry_capacity (carried_weight from SubstanceMix::weight, capacity from being_muscle_force), only where the embodiment declares a material registry AND a being carries a load, so an opted-out run inserts no factor. HASH RE-BASELINE, called out clearly: this is the arc's first deliberate hash change on the run path, and it is OPT-IN, an unladen being (empty carried, so no load_factor entry) is byte-identical, so world_build and world_determinism are unchanged and every existing scenario replays bit for bit; only a scenario that declares a material registry and has a being pick matter up sees a changed hash. Proven (locomotion.rs a_carried_load_slows_a_moving_being): two identical exploring beings drawing the same heading sequence, the one with a load factor above one covers less ground, and a unit factor leaves the walk byte-identical. Full sim suite green (626 lib plus all integration binaries, world_build and world_determinism unchanged), fmt and clippy clean. One reserved value added, locomotion.load_penalty (surfaced-with-basis, dev-fixture set, fail-loud manifest home a follow-on like the sibling locomotion reserveds). This closes item 3's PHYSICAL milestone (pick up, movement cost rises, put down); the DRIVER (a being DECIDES to pick up from a need plus an evolved affordance, the emergence check the gate will gate hard) is next, entangled with item 4's need-driven extraction.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 3 DRIVER (the evolved decision to grasp; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, hash-neutral for existing scenarios). A being now picks matter up only because its evolved controller decided to, never because the engine scripts carrying, closing item 3's emergence crux. crates/sim/src/homeostasis.rs: a GRASP affordance (AffordanceId 3, a scalar operation, requires None so any body may attempt to lift and the physical gating is the strength-versus-weight bound the enactment applies, never a capability label) and a dev_carrier fixture (move, ingest, grasp) sibling to dev_predator, so a carrier world's controller layout carries a grasp output the evolved weights can drive while every dev_default scenario keeps its two-affordance layout untouched. crates/sim/src/locomotion.rs: step_with_field_dirs takes a per-being grasp_intents out-map and records the grasp activation when a being's GRASP output wins its decision (a new match arm beside MOVE and INGEST), the decision staying where the evolved controller makes it. crates/sim/src/runner.rs: the embodiment step, after the locomotion decision, enacts the recorded grasps in id order through a new Embodiment::grasp_underfoot, which lifts the cell's substances in canonical id order each bounded by the being's remaining strength headroom (the item-4 extraction contest will gate WHICH substance yields by the fracture hardness; this generic carry gates only by weight). The decision is an evolved phenotype: a blank founder expresses zero on the grasp channel and never grasps, so no grasp is enacted and the run is byte-identical for it. Proven (physiology_embodiment.rs a_being_grasps_matter_only_through_an_evolved_controller_weight): two beings share one embodiment, one body plan, one strength, and one identical granite heap each, differing in ONE gene, the controller weight feeding the grasp output; the being whose grasp weight is lifted grasps (its cell loses exactly what it carries, bounded by strength so matter remains), and the blank founder on the same matter affording the same operation grasps nothing and leaves its heap untouched. This is the emergent pattern (Principles 8, 9): the affordance and the physics are fixed, the DECISION is an evolved weight, and a founder does nothing until selection gives it a reason. Opt-in and hash-neutral for existing scenarios (only a dev_carrier scenario carries the grasp output, and only a nonzero grasp weight enacts a pick-up), so world_build and world_determinism are unchanged and the whole sim suite is green (626 lib plus all integration binaries), fmt and clippy clean, no new reserved value. HONEST LIMIT and coupling: the selection PRESSURE that would lift a founder's grasp weight (a homeostatic need the carried matter serves) arrives with item 4's extraction contest; item 3 proves the mechanism at the decision, the same standard the STRIKE affordance holds (a body affords and decides, the payoff wired later). Next: item 4, the extraction contest, where a need makes the carried matter worth something and the fracture-gating hardness (not the bulk mean) decides which substance yields, the first big observable milestone.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 4 SLICE A READ (the fracture-gating hardness; branch claude/material-substrate, hash-neutral, off the run path). The extraction contest's target resistance is now a distinct, tested read, landing the gate's item-4 note. crates/sim/src/material.rs: SubstanceMix::fracture_hardness and MaterialField::fracture_hardness derive a cell's FRACTURE-GATING hardness as the GREATEST mat.fracture_strength among its constituents (a new constituent_max helper), NOT the volume-weighted mean that bulk_hardness takes, because hardness does not average linearly and a composite breaks at its strongest bond, so ore embedded in granite breaks at the granite. A new AXIS_FRACTURE const names the mat.fracture_strength axis the fracture law gates on, distinct from the indentation-hardness axis a plastic cut gates on. Off the run path with no consumer yet (like bulk_hardness before it), so hash-neutral, every existing scenario byte-identical. Proven (material.rs the_fracture_gating_hardness_is_the_hardest_constituent_not_the_mean): a pure cell reads its substance's own fracture strength at any volume, a granite-in-soil cell fractures at the granite (20) not at the ~7 the mean would give, a constituent carrying no fracture datum contributes zero to the max (the absence convention, so granite plus peat still gates at the granite), and a fracture-datum-less or empty cell reads zero. 617 lib tests green, fmt and clippy clean, no new reserved value (mat.fracture_strength is cited floor data). HONEST LIMIT surfaced: the strongest constituent is the proxy for the load-bearing matrix; where the continuous binding phase is not the hardest constituent, a matrix-phase datum would refine this, deferred until a substance declares which phase binds. Next: slice B, the extraction-yield kernel (a being's contact pressure over its working area against this fracture hardness, yielding a bounded volume) and the DIG/EXTRACT affordance driven by a homeostatic need, which supplies the selection payoff the item-3 driver deferred.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 4 SLICE B KERNEL (the extraction-yield contest; branch claude/material-substrate, hash-neutral, off the run path). The extraction physics is now built and proven in isolation, composing floor laws rather than a bespoke rule. crates/sim/src/material.rs: a module-level extraction_yield(force, working_area, fracture_hardness, delivered_energy, specific_cut_energy, pressure_max, depth_max) composes laws::contact_pressure (the being's force over its working area is a contact pressure) and laws::cut_penetrate (that pressure must clear the cell's FRACTURE-gating hardness to break anything loose, and above the gate the cut depth sizes with the delivered work over the material's specific cutting energy); the detached volume is the cut depth over the working area. The two axes are the fracture physics itself: STRENGTH decides whether the rock breaks (the pressure-over-fracture-strength gate), ENERGY decides how much comes off (the work over the specific cutting energy). Off the run path with no caller yet (the sibling of the carry weight, which composes laws::weight the same way), so hash-neutral and every existing scenario byte-identical. Proven (material.rs the_extraction_contest_gates_on_fracture_strength_and_sizes_on_cutting_energy): a being too weak to raise its pressure over the fracture strength mines nothing, a strong force clears the soft rock and detaches an exact swept volume, the same force on a rock too strong for its pressure yields zero while an even stronger force breaks that harder rock, a tougher-to-cut material yields less to the same work, and more delivered work detaches more. 628 lib tests green, fmt and clippy clean, no new reserved value (the kernel takes its inputs as parameters; the sourcing of force, working area, delivered energy, and specific cutting energy from the being's physiology and the substance floor, plus any reserved values, lands in slice C's wiring). Next: slice C, the DIG/EXTRACT affordance (a new evolved-controller output, the sibling of GRASP) driven by a homeostatic need for the mined substance, which supplies the selection payoff the item-3 driver deferred and makes mining observable end to end, need plus contact-pressure-vs-fracture affordance plus structured matter.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 4 SLICE C DRIVER (extraction wired into the run, mining becomes a behaviour; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, hash-neutral for existing scenarios). A being now breaks bonded rock loose and takes it, but only because its evolved controller decided to AND its contact pressure clears the rock's fracture strength, the first mining behaviour. crates/sim/src/homeostasis.rs: an EXTRACT affordance (AffordanceId 4, scalar, requires None so the physical gating is the fracture contest not a capability label) in a dev_miner fixture (move, ingest, extract), sibling to dev_carrier. crates/sim/src/locomotion.rs: the per-affordance grasp_intents out-map is generalised to a deferred_actions map of (AffordanceId, activation), so GRASP and EXTRACT both record their decided affordance through one path (no new param per affordance; the six test call sites are untouched since BTreeMap::new() infers the new type). crates/sim/src/runner.rs: the embodiment step dispatches the recorded actions by affordance, GRASP to grasp_underfoot and EXTRACT to a new Embodiment::extract_underfoot, which gates on the fracture contest (the being's being_muscle_force pressed over its reserved working area is a laws::contact_pressure; if that pressure does not exceed the cell's fracture_hardness the rock holds and nothing is taken) and, above the gate, takes a strength-bounded load through grasp_underfoot (extraction is fracture THEN carry, the distinction from a bare grasp which has only the weight gate). crates/sim/src/material.rs: an ExtractionParams struct (opt-in on the Embodiment via set_extraction_params) carries the one reserved value and the pressure cap. Proven (physiology_embodiment.rs a_being_mines_bonded_rock_only_when_it_decides_to_and_can_fracture_it): a deciding being whose force is concentrated over a small working area fractures granite and mines a strength-bounded load (the cell loses exactly that, rock remains), a blank founder on the same rock affording the same operation never mines (no decision), and the SAME deciding being with its force spread over a large working area mines nothing (the contest is pressure, not raw force, so the fracture gate holds). Opt-in and hash-neutral for existing scenarios (only dev_miner carries the extract output, only extraction params plus a nonzero extract weight enact a mine), so world_build and world_determinism are unchanged and the whole sim suite is green (628 lib plus all integration binaries), fmt and clippy clean. ONE reserved value added, extraction working_area (surfaced-with-basis: the bearing area of the body's working surface, a bare limb's tip or a hafted tool's edge, a body-and-tool geometry the anatomy arc will derive per-part, a smaller area concentrating the same force to a higher pressure; dev-fixture 0.001 m^2). HONEST LIMIT and coupling, per the gate's note: the yield AMOUNT is the strength-bounded carry here (the fracture STRENGTH gates whether the rock breaks); the energy-sized per-stroke yield (slice B's extraction_yield, built and proven) wires in when the mineable substances carry a cited mat.specific_cut_energy. And, as with the grasp driver, mining is proven at the decision plus the physics contest; a being mining because a NEED for the matter drives it (the reserve backing and the payoff that makes extraction EMERGE under selection) is the next slice, where the first mining behaviour's blind concept-verification comes due.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 4 CRAFTING SEAM (the cut contest reads the target's material; branch claude/material-substrate, hash-neutral, off the run path). The load-bearing crafting seam the handoff flags is landed as a distinct, tested read. crates/compose/src/capability.rs: cut_capability_against_target runs the same contact-pressure-into-penetration contest pierce does, but the resistance it must defeat is read from the TARGET's own material axes (mat.indentation_hardness, mat.specific_cut_energy) rather than the single global reference target (CapabilityRefs.target_hardness) pierce measures every part against. So the same edge parts soft hide and stalls on hard granite, and a harder sharper edge parts stone a softer blunter one cannot, diverging on the target's substance DATA alone with no per-material branch: mining flint versus granite and cutting hide versus wood become one contest over different substance rows, never a code branch (the handoff's crafting seam, called the load-bearing one for the whole arc). The part's own hardness still caps the pressure a soft edge sustains, so a soft tool cannot exceed a hard target's resistance however sharp. Opt-in beside derive_capabilities with no existing caller changed, so every existing capability score and every scenario is byte-identical (hash-neutral); a target axis the substance does not carry reads zero (the absence convention). Proven (capability.rs a_cut_reads_the_targets_own_material_so_the_same_edge_diverges_by_target): the same flint edge parts hide (positive) and cannot part granite (zero, its pressure below the harder target), a harder sharper pick parts the granite the flint could not, and the divergence is the target's data not the edge. 9 compose lib tests plus 15 evaluator tests green, fmt and clippy clean, no new reserved value (the contest reads substance data and the existing reserved references). HONEST LIMIT and follow-on: this is the READ half, opt-in; folding CUT into the FunctionLawRegistry as a data-bound kernel (retiring pierce's global reference target) lands when a consumer reads it, and wiring a wielded worked-object tool into the sim's extraction contest (so a crafted point's small contact area lets a being mine harder rock, the tool-multiplies-affordance payoff that gives mined matter its use and lets mining EMERGE under selection) is the next slice.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 4 TOOL-IN-EXTRACTION (a wielded tool multiplies the affordance; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, hash-neutral for existing scenarios). A crafted tool now makes a being mine harder matter, the crafting payoff's hinge wired into the extraction contest. crates/sim/src/material.rs: a WieldedTool struct, the CONTEST INTERFACE of a tool, carrying the two things an extraction or cut reads, its working GEOMETRY (the contact_area its edge presses over) and its MATERIAL (the substance it is made of, whose hardness the registry supplies); a crafted FormDef-plus-Substance tool populates exactly these, so it is the forward-compatible view a tool presents to a contest, never a tool catalog. crates/sim/src/locomotion.rs: the Walker gains an opt-in wielded: Option<WieldedTool> (None by default, so a being wielding nothing folds nothing and its contest is unchanged). crates/sim/src/runner.rs: state_hash folds the wielded tool when present (after the carried matter, opt-in), and Embodiment::extract_underfoot reads the wielded tool: the being's force presses over the tool's (smaller) contact_area instead of the bare reserved working area, and the effective pressure is capped by the tool's own indentation hardness (a soft tool blunts before it reaches a hard rock's resistance, the same cap the weapon and cut reads apply; a tool whose substance declares no hardness reads zero and blunts to nothing, so a tool must declare its hardness to work matter). A bare being (None) keeps its unchanged reserved-working-area contest. Proven (physiology_embodiment.rs a_wielded_tool_multiplies_the_extraction_affordance_by_its_geometry_and_material): the same deciding being that mines nothing bare-handed (its force spread over a large working area) fractures granite when it wields a sharp HARD flint tool (small contact area, hard material), and mines nothing when it wields an equally sharp but SOFT chalk tool (it blunts at its own low hardness before it clears the granite), so the tool multiplies the affordance by BOTH its geometry and its material, all against substance data with no tool catalog. Opt-in and hash-neutral for existing scenarios (the wielded slot is None by default, folding nothing), so world_build and world_determinism are unchanged and the whole sim suite is green (628 lib plus all integration binaries), fmt and clippy clean, no new reserved value (the tool's geometry is a worked-object property a crafted tool supplies, not a manifest datum). HONEST LIMIT and the remaining loop: a wielded tool multiplies extraction, but the tool is set directly here (a fixture), not yet CRAFTED from mined stone; the CRAFTING that shapes a tool from a mined Substance (knapping a FormDef, its function derived by the same cut_capability_against_target read) is the next slice, and it closes the full emergence loop (mine stone, make a better tool, mine more), where the first mining behaviour's blind concept-verification comes due. A bare being also carries no working-surface-hardness cap yet (an anatomy-arc follow-on), so only the wielded path reads a material cap so far.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 4 INGEST-FOR-COMPOSITION (geophagy, the mineral is worth something; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, hash-neutral for existing scenarios). The owner's force-and-manipulation addendum (PR #93, handoff main 7065d65) named INGEST-FOR-COMPOSITION as the need-side complement to harm-learning; it is built, and it is the direct answer to the gate's standing note that mining will not EMERGE until the matter is worth something. A being now eats the matter it stands on for a reserve that needs it, so a mineral in the ground has fitness value. crates/sim/src/homeostasis.rs: a GEOPHAGE affordance (AffordanceId 5, scalar, requires None) in a dev_geophage fixture (move, ingest, geophage), sibling to dev_carrier and dev_miner. crates/sim/src/locomotion.rs: the deferred_actions match arm records GRASP, EXTRACT, and now GEOPHAGE through the one enactment path. crates/sim/src/runner.rs: the embodiment step dispatches GEOPHAGE to a new Embodiment::geophage, which for each homeostatic axis whose backing substance the cell holds draws it through the SAME edibility satisfaction the forage ingest uses (laws::satisfaction over the being's own assimilation and requirement, bounded by the reserve room, grossed up by the ingest efficiency, taken from the cell, the assimilated part credited), so a being with a mineral deficit standing on that mineral refills from it and a full one draws nothing. This is the need-side complement to the harm-learning read: the same cell composition a being learns to AVOID for a harm, another SEEKS for a nutrient it lacks. Proven (physiology_embodiment.rs a_being_geophages_a_needed_mineral_and_outlives_one_that_does_not): two beings share one body, one draining halite-backed mineral reserve, and one identical rock-salt seam each, differing in ONE gene (the geophage-output weight); the evolved-weight being eats the salt it stands on each tick and OUTLIVES the blank founder, which never eats though it stands on the same salt, drains its reserve, and dies (and the eater's seam is drawn down while the founder's is untouched). So a mineral's fitness value, the reason to seek it and (through EXTRACT) to mine a bonded one, is an evolved phenotype resolved by physiology against substance data, founder-zero, no per-race diet table (Principles 8, 9), the emergence-closer the extraction milestone was waiting on. Opt-in and hash-neutral for existing scenarios (only dev_geophage carries the geophage output, and an empty material field holds no substance so geophage draws nothing), so world_build and world_determinism are unchanged and the whole sim suite is green (629 lib plus all integration binaries), fmt and clippy clean, no new reserved value (the satisfaction reuses the being's edibility physiology and the ingest efficiency). HONEST LIMIT and ordering note: geophage is enacted in the post-step matter pass, so it tops a reserve up for the NEXT tick's drain rather than saving a being on the tick it would die; a being survives on its buffer and geophagy keeps the buffer full, which is why the reserve must be organ-backed (a mineral-storing tissue) to hold a buffer at all. This lands the addendum's INGEST-FOR-COMPOSITION; the remaining force-and-manipulation affordances (STRIKE-WITH-A-HELD-OBJECT and WEAVE the owner's top picks, plus THROW, PUSH/DRAG/ROLL, LEVER, DAM, FLOAT, BURROW, MIX, STACK, CACHE, GIVE) and CRAFT/knapping fold in next, before or alongside item 5.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 4 CRAFT / KNAPPING (a being shapes a tool from mined stone, the recursive loop closes; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, hash-neutral for existing scenarios). The tool-making step is built, so the wielded tool that multiplies extraction is now MADE from mined stone rather than fixture-set, closing the mine-stone -> make-tool -> mine-harder loop. crates/sim/src/homeostasis.rs: a CRAFT affordance (AffordanceId 6, scalar, requires None) in a dev_toolmaker fixture (move, ingest, extract, craft), so a being can both mine and shape. crates/sim/src/material.rs: a CraftParams struct (opt-in on the Embodiment via set_craft_params) carries the two reserved knapping values. crates/sim/src/locomotion.rs: the deferred_actions match arm records GRASP, EXTRACT, GEOPHAGE, and now CRAFT through the one enactment path. crates/sim/src/runner.rs: the embodiment step dispatches CRAFT to a new Embodiment::craft_from_carried, which consumes the reserved tool volume of the FIRST substance the being carries enough of (canonical id order, a deterministic tie-break, no per-substance preference) and wields a tool of that substance with the reserved working-edge area, replacing any prior tool; a new Runner::embodiment_mut exposes the write handle a caller drives a matter action through. So a being that mined and carried stone shapes it into a point, and the tool is only as good as the stone worked (the tool's function derived from its material and geometry by the crafting seam's cut read, never a recipe catalog). Proven: a_being_crafts_a_tool_from_its_carried_stone_only_through_an_evolved_weight (the evolved-weight being shapes its carried granite into a granite tool spending the reserved tool volume, and a blank founder carrying the same stone never crafts, founder-zero) and a_crafted_tool_closes_the_loop_and_mines_rock_the_bare_body_cannot (a being carrying flint cannot fracture granite bare-handed, shapes its flint into a tool, and wielding it breaks the granite its bare body could not, the recursive payoff end to end). Opt-in and hash-neutral for existing scenarios (only dev_toolmaker carries the craft output, only craft parameters plus a nonzero craft weight make a tool), so world_build and world_determinism are unchanged and the whole sim suite is green (631 lib plus all integration binaries), fmt and clippy clean. Two reserved values added, CraftParams.edge_area (the working-edge contact area a knapped tool presents, basis the contact patch of a shaping stroke, a tool geometry the crafting-physics refinement will derive from the worked stone's fracture) and CraftParams.tool_volume (the carried volume a tool consumes, basis the material a shaped tool of the working size embodies), both surfaced-with-basis, dev-fixture set. HONEST LIMIT: the tool's geometry is a reserved fixture shape, not yet derived from the fracture physics of knapping (the stone struck produces a flake whose geometry is physics, a refinement); and CRAFT shapes the FIRST carried substance by id order, a deterministic tie-break, where a being carrying a mix does not yet choose the best tool stone (which the tool's derived capability, a harder stone a better tool, lets selection favor without a preference in CRAFT). This lands the crafting half of item 4; the force-and-manipulation extension's remaining affordances (STRIKE-WITH-A-HELD-OBJECT and WEAVE the owner's top picks, plus THROW, PUSH, LEVER, DAM, FLOAT, BURROW, MIX, STACK, CACHE, GIVE) and the harm-half of INGEST-FOR-COMPOSITION (a food that sickens, routing the ingest paths through edibility::assess, the owner's just-flagged seam) fold in next, before or alongside item 5.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 4 GEOPHAGY HARM-HALF (a food that sickens; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, hash-neutral for existing scenarios). The owner flagged the seam that geophage applied only the nutrient benefit (laws::satisfaction) and never the toxin harm (edibility::assess), so eating a poison for a trace nutrient was free while standing on it harmed, backwards, and the harm-learning arc's "food that sickens" case could not happen. It is closed. crates/sim/src/runner.rs: Embodiment::geophage now tracks the substances it eats and, after the nutrient draw, harms the eater by each eaten substance's toxin concentration against its OWN inherited per-toxin-class tolerance and Hill exponent (laws::net_harm over the classes the being carries a tolerance for, read from each substance's registry vector, never the substance's mat.* axes), the harm applied to CONDITION (a no-op for a being with no CONDITION axis) so it feeds the EXISTING harm-learning loop. This is the harm side of edibility::assess wired into ingestion, symmetric with the exposure read: the same cell composition a being learns to AVOID standing on, it now also feels when it EATS, per consumer with no per-substance poison label (Principle 9). Proven (physiology_embodiment.rs eating_a_food_that_sickens_harms_the_sensitive_eater_and_spares_the_tolerant_one): two beings differing only in salinity tolerance eat the same brackish food (a mineral nutrient laced with a salinity toxin); the salt-sensitive eater's CONDITION falls (the food sickens it) while the salt-tolerant eater's holds (the same food spares it), the food read against each being's own inherited tolerance. So a being can now learn "this food sickens me", not only "this place harms me". Opt-in and hash-neutral for existing scenarios (only a geophage being with a material registry eating a substance that carries a toxin the being tolerates takes any harm; the loose-mineral geophage still applies no harm, halite carrying no toxin), so world_build and world_determinism are unchanged and the whole sim suite is green (632 lib plus all integration binaries), fmt and clippy clean, no new reserved value (the harm reuses the being's inherited tolerance, the floor harm caps, and laws::net_harm). HONEST LIMIT: the dose is the eaten substance's toxin concentration (matching the exposure read), not yet scaled by the amount eaten (eat-more-harm-more is a refinement); and the forage ingest's symmetric harm-half (for the ResourceField path) rides the same pattern when it is wired. The felt harm feeding a being to LEARN a food sickens it is now possible through the existing harm-learning loop; a blind concept-verify of that emergent avoidance rides the harm-learning follow-on. This closes the owner's ingestion seam; the rest of the force-and-manipulation extension (STRIKE-WITH-A-HELD-OBJECT and WEAVE the top picks, then THROW/PUSH/LEVER/DAM/FLOAT/BURROW/MIX/STACK/CACHE/GIVE) and items 5 through 8 fold in next.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 5 SLICE A READ (the earthwork-delta field; branch claude/material-substrate, hash-neutral, off the run path). Item 5 (modifiable terrain) begins with its substrate, built as pure mechanism and unit-proven with no run-path touch. crates/sim/src/material.rs: an EarthworkField, a sparse per-column elevation-delta field keyed by the ground Coord3 (z zero), a sibling of MaterialField, empty by default. The physics will read the EFFECTIVE elevation as the worldgen elevation plus the column's delta, so a dug pit (a negative delta) pools water and a raised mound (a positive delta) sheds it, the hydrology's downhill target recomputing from the effective elevation rather than a one-time worldgen precompute; digging is a fracture contest over the ground's derived hardness (the extraction contest, reused), the removed matter conserved as a carried load and set down elsewhere as a mound, and this field is the elevation bookkeeping that lets the dig and the deposit reshape the terrain, not only move matter. delta reads zero for an unreworked column (the absence convention), adjust accumulates digs and mounds and prunes a column back at the baseline to void, and hash_into folds in canonical (column, delta) order. Off the run path with no consumer yet (like the MaterialField READ half before it), so hash-neutral and every existing scenario byte-identical. Proven (material.rs the_earthwork_field_accumulates_digs_and_mounds_and_folds_canonically): an unreworked column reads zero, digs accumulate, a mound raises another column, filling a pit back to the baseline prunes it, the fold is canonical and insertion-order-independent, and an empty field folds nothing. 632 lib tests plus all integration binaries green, fmt and clippy clean, no new reserved value. Next: slice B wires a DIG affordance (a fracture contest lowering the column and producing spoil to the carried load, the extraction contest plus the elevation delta), the state_hash fold behind the opt-in empty-default, and then the hydrology coupling (effective elevation recomputes the downhill target so a dug pit pools water).

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 5 SLICE B DIG (excavation reshapes the terrain; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN hash change for digging scenarios; includes the slice-A clippy fix). A being now digs a pit, closing item 5's first observable, and the slice-A earthwork READ half's one clippy-DENY blocker (an unused `mut h0` in the test, which CI's -D warnings failed on) is fixed in the same push. crates/sim/src/homeostasis.rs: a DIG affordance (AffordanceId 7, scalar, requires None) in a dev_digger fixture. crates/sim/src/runner.rs: the Embodiment carries an earthwork: EarthworkField (empty default, opt-in), an earthwork() accessor, and folds it into state_hash after the material layer (empty for a non-digging scenario, so byte-identical); the deferred_actions dispatch routes DIG to a new Embodiment::dig_underfoot, which excavates in the SAME extraction fracture contest (extract_underfoot, the fracture gate plus taking the spoil into the carried load) AND lowers the column by the volume removed (earthwork.adjust by minus the spoil), so a pit forms where matter left, the ground conserved between the carrier and the lowered terrain. This is the distinction from a bare extract: extract takes matter, dig also reshapes the terrain. crates/sim/src/locomotion.rs: the deferred_actions match arm records GRASP, EXTRACT, GEOPHAGE, CRAFT, and now DIG through the one path. Proven (physiology_embodiment.rs a_being_digs_a_pit_lowering_the_terrain_only_through_an_evolved_weight): a deciding being that can fracture the ground digs a pit (its carried load gains the spoil, the cell loses exactly that, and the column drops by exactly the excavated volume), while a blank founder on the same ground never digs and the terrain is untouched, founder-zero and physics-gated. Opt-in and hash-neutral for existing scenarios (only a dev_digger being with extraction parameters that fractures the ground writes an earthwork delta; the empty earthwork folds nothing), so world_build and world_determinism are unchanged and the whole sim suite is green (633 lib plus all integration binaries), fmt and clippy (--all-targets -D warnings) clean, no new reserved value (dig reuses the extraction contest's working area). HONEST LIMIT: dig LOWERS a column (a pit); the symmetric MOUND (a deposit raising a column, put_down coupling to the earthwork) and the HYDROLOGY coupling (effective elevation = worldgen plus delta recomputing the downhill target, so a pit pools water and a mound sheds it) are the next item-5 slices, plus the ConservationRegistry and vertical z-adjacency the handoff names. This closes item 5's first observable (terrain lowers by digging); the mound-and-hydrology half and the rest of the cascade (items 6-8) and the force-and-manipulation extension fold in next.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE STEERING DISCIPLINE (owner, PR #93, "primitives coded, techniques emergent"; on the handoff main HEAD tail). Before building the force-and-manipulation and later extensions, hold every gap-list entry to a PRIMITIVE-versus-TECHNIQUE test. A PRIMITIVE is body-grounded and physics-gated (a limb closes is grasp, force meets fracture is extract/dig, a mouth ingests, a tissue heats, a hand releases): fine to code as an affordance. A TECHNIQUE is a composite of primitives against matter over time (cast, forge, ferment, knap, weave): it must EMERGE from sequencing primitives against real physics, never arrive as its own coded affordance. Casting is what happens when a being melts a substance (fire), pours it into a hollow (an earthwork pit), and it sets: no CAST verb. So the gap addendum is a COMPLETENESS CHECK on the physics substrate, not a to-build list of verbs: build the small primitive set the substrate is missing and let the techniques emerge from sequencing them. Two direction-of-travel debts already in the arc to walk back toward emergence when convenient (not blockers, both signed off as first cuts): CRAFT/knapping is a coded technique today (should emerge from strike-a-core-and-the-fracture-throws-flakes; the tool-geometry-from-skill refinement is the first step, TODOS #61), and DIG and EXTRACT are near-duplicates to unify into one ground-working primitive (selective versus bulk a parameter, not two verbs, TODOS #60). This reframes the remaining manipulation-extension work (TODOS #58) from a verb-build list to a primitive completeness check plus letting techniques emerge; the physics-consequence work already in flight (a dug pit lowering the terrain, a deposit raising it, a pit pooling water through the hydrology recompute) is aligned, being physics consequences rather than coded verbs.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 5 DEPOSIT-AND-MOUND (a release raises the terrain; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, hash-neutral for existing scenarios). Item 5's second half: setting a carried load down raises the column, so terracing (a mound beside a pit) emerges from the dig and release primitives with no MOUND verb, honoring the primitives-coded/techniques-emergent discipline. crates/sim/src/homeostasis.rs: a RELEASE affordance (AffordanceId 8, scalar, requires None), the inverse of GRASP, a body-grounded PRIMITIVE (open the grasp), in a dev_earthmover fixture (move, ingest, dig, release) so a being can both dig a pit and set the spoil down elsewhere. crates/sim/src/runner.rs: the deferred_actions dispatch routes RELEASE to a new Embodiment::release_underfoot, which deposits each carried substance onto the cell (put_down, in canonical id order) AND raises the column by the total deposited, conservation-symmetric with dig_underfoot lowering it. crates/sim/src/locomotion.rs: the deferred_actions match arm records GRASP, EXTRACT, GEOPHAGE, CRAFT, DIG, and now RELEASE through the one path. Proven (physiology_embodiment.rs releasing_a_carried_load_raises_the_column_the_mound_half_of_terraforming): a deciding being sets its whole carried load down (the cell gains the matter, the column rises by exactly the deposited volume, a mound, and the being carries nothing more), while a blank founder holding the same load never releases and the terrain is untouched, founder-zero. Combined with DIG, the conservation loop closes: what a being digs from a pit here (the column drops by the spoil) and carries to there and releases (that column rises by the same spoil) moves both matter and terrain height conservatively, so terracing is the emergent consequence of two primitives, not a coded verb. Opt-in and hash-neutral for existing scenarios (only a dev_earthmover being that releases writes an earthwork delta; the empty earthwork folds nothing), so world_build and world_determinism are unchanged and the whole sim suite is green (629 lib plus all integration binaries, 18 in the embodiment binary), fmt and clippy (--all-targets -D warnings) clean, no new reserved value. This gives item 5 both halves (dig lowers, release raises). NEXT: the HYDROLOGY coupling (effective elevation = worldgen + earthwork delta recomputing the downhill target so a dug pit pools water and a mound sheds it, retiring the one-time worldgen downhill precompute), plus the ConservationRegistry and vertical z-adjacency the handoff names; then items 6 (live fire), 7 (shelter), 8 (the matter cycle with the owner-ruled data-defined TransformKindRegistry), and the primitive completeness check for the force-and-manipulation extension.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 5 HYDROLOGY COUPLING (a dug pit pools water; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, crucible-safe).
