Item 5's payoff: the terrain a being reshapes now feeds the water physics, so digging is no bookkeeping delta but a change the hydrology reads. crates/sim/src/environ.rs: EnvironFields keeps the frozen worldgen elevation (a static input beside moisture and light, where before it was dropped after the one-time downhill precompute) and gains recouple_terrain(&EarthworkField), which rebuilds the downhill routing from the EFFECTIVE elevation (the worldgen base plus the per-column earthwork delta) by the same pure fold (compute_downhill) that seeded it. So a dug pit that drops a cell below its neighbours becomes a basin that routes to itself and ponds its water and its salt (the salinity stencil advects on the same routing), and a mound that lifts a cell sheds them, the terrain change feeding the physics with no water verb. A new is_basin(x,y) read exposes the routing for the reader and the test. crates/sim/src/runner.rs: a recouple_hydrology beat rebuilds the routing after the embodiment step, called identically in the pinned (step_inner) and scheduled (run_phase SYS_EMBODIMENT) orders, and the embodiment phase now declares it writes RES_FIELD (the write reinforces the existing field-step serialization and changes no batch, so the scheduled order stays bit-identical to the pinned one). OPT-IN and CRUCIBLE-SAFE: recouple_terrain skips an empty earthwork, so a run in which nothing digs keeps the seeded worldgen routing byte-identical (the fold is pure, base plus zero equals base); only a reshaped column pays the rebuild, so the crucible stays at 254bc17c and world_build/world_determinism replay unchanged. Proven three ways: an environ unit test (a plane whose interior drains eastward until a dug centre becomes a basin its four neighbours pond into, plus the empty-earthwork no-op that guarantees byte-identity), and an end-to-end runner test (a being digs through the FULL runner in both tick orders and its cell flips from draining to a basin, while a blank being that digs nothing leaves the routing untouched; the test selects the map's minimum-margin non-basin cell so one realistic scoop tips it, a clean causal separation). 631 sim lib tests plus all integration binaries green, world_build 16 and world_determinism 3 replay-identical, fmt and clippy (--all-targets -D warnings) clean, no new reserved value (the coupling reuses the frozen elevation and the earthwork delta already folded). This closes item 5 (modifiable terrain): a being digs a pit, mounds a hill, and the water now finds the pit. Next in the cascade: item 6 (live fire), item 7 (shelter), item 8 (the matter cycle), and the force-and-manipulation extension as a primitive-completeness check, gate catching up per slice.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 6 SLICE A LIVE FIRE (combustible matter burns when hot; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, hash-neutral for existing scenarios). The first slice of live fire: the resolved combustion law (civsim_physics::laws::combustion, already floor-built) wired into the run as a field process. crates/sim/src/material.rs: a FireField, a sparse Coord3-to-intensity sibling of EarthworkField, records the combustion energy each burning cell releases (unlit by default, pruned when a cell stops burning, folded when non-empty). crates/sim/src/runner.rs: a combustion beat (Runner::step_combustion, run inside step_field so both the pinned and scheduled tick orders source the fire from the settled temperature identically) scans the material field for combustible matter, and a cell holding a substance that carries therm.fuel_value and stands at or above its therm.ignition_temperature combusts, consuming a bounded fraction of its fuel from the material field (the reserved burn rate) and lighting the fire field with the released energy; the burned volume follows from the released energy over the fuel value and back through the substance density, the law's own relation rather than a coded rate. A CombustionCalib carries the two reserved values (the burn rate, basis: a fuel burns down over a timescale, not instantly, a reaction time constant against the tick; the energy cap, basis: a fixed-point representability bound), surfaced-with-basis on the struct exactly like ExtractionParams, armed opt-in via Runner::set_combustion and off the calibrated worldbuild path until a later slice wires it. OPT-IN and hash-neutral: the beat runs only when a combustion calib is armed with a material registry present, and the fire field folds into state_hash only when non-empty, so a scenario with no combustion armed or nothing hot enough burns nothing and stays byte-identical (crucible unchanged at 254bc17c, world_build 16 and world_determinism 3 replay-identical). Keyed off the substance's own combustion axes and the cell temperature, no race, kind, or role (Principles 8, 9). Proven: a FireField unit test (records burning cells, prunes the extinguished, folds canonically and empty-neutral) and an end-to-end runner test combustible_matter_burns_when_it_is_hot_enough_and_a_cold_cell_and_rock_do_not (oak in a hot field burns down and lights the fire field while granite in the same cell and the same oak in a cold field do not, in both tick orders). 632 sim lib tests plus all integration binaries green, fmt and clippy (--all-targets -D warnings) clean. HONEST LIMIT and next slices: the oxidiser is not supplied yet, so a self-oxidising fuel (oak, which declares no oxidiser demand) burns on the current data and an oxygen-demanding fuel reads oxidiser-limited to nothing; the medium-oxygen gate that makes fire need air (slice B) and the heat injection that lets fire warm the cell and spread through the temperature diffusion (slice C) are the next item-6 slices, then item 7 (shelter), item 8 (the matter cycle), and the force-and-manipulation extension.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 6 SLICE C HEAT INJECTION (fire spreads and burns out; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, hash-neutral for existing scenarios). The emergent payoff of live fire, and the slice the gate steered to after slice A. A burning cell now raises its own temperature by the heat its combustion releases, that heat spreads through the ordinary temperature diffusion (crates/sim/src/runner.rs Field::add_heat), and a neighbouring fuel cell whose temperature crosses its ignition gate catches: fire SPREADS from cell to cell and EXTINGUISHES when a cell's fuel runs out, both emergent from the physics with no coded spread rule (it is the combustion gate over the diffused temperature, tick after tick). The combustion beat computes each burning cell's temperature rise as the reserved heat-retention fraction of the released energy over the cell's heat capacity (the volume-weighted sum of its matter's density times specific heat, the /1000 converting the specific-heat J to the fuel value's kJ, overflow-guarded), a cell with no specific-heat data burning without heating (the honest degrade). Data and reserved: oak gains its cited therm.specific_heat (1700, CRC / Wood Handbook), and CombustionCalib gains the reserved heat_fraction (basis: the combustion efficiency and the radiative-and-convective loss fraction of an open fire, so a flame settles below the full adiabatic temperature the complete-combustion fuel value implies; surfaced-with-basis, dev-fixture one-tenth). OPT-IN and hash-neutral: the heat injection runs only inside the combustion beat, so a scenario with no combustion armed never touches the temperature field and stays byte-identical (crucible unchanged at 254bc17c, world_build 16 and world_determinism 3 replay-identical). Proven end to end (physiology_embodiment.rs fire_spreads_along_a_fuel_row_and_burns_out_behind_it): fire spreads down a fuel row cell to cell through the temperature field (a far cell cold at the start catches after the heat propagates), the source dims as its fuel depletes and finally drops out of the fire field when it burns out, and the scheduled order spreads it bit-identically to the pinned order. 814 sim tests plus 84 physics tests green, fmt and clippy (--all-targets -D warnings) clean. HONEST LIMITS: the lumped single-cell thermal model runs hotter than a real gas-plume flame, and the reserved heat fraction with the field's diffusion and relaxation rates jointly set how readily fire spreads (the owner's to calibrate; the test uses a labelled fire-timescale field calib with slow relaxation so the fire is not pulled straight back to the cold baseline). NEXT: the medium-oxygen gate that makes fire need air (slice B, reads the medium's respirable content as the oxidiser), then item 7 (shelter), item 8 (the matter cycle), and the force-and-manipulation extension.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 7 SLICE A SHELTER (insulating matter buffers a being; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, hash-neutral for existing scenarios). The first slice of shelter: a being's body-to-field thermal exchange is now attenuated by the insulating matter enclosing its cell, so a being under a roof of a low-conductivity material is buffered from a harsh field. crates/sim/src/runner.rs phase_body_exchange reads the matter in the air cells above a being (z >= 1 in its column), derives that matter's thermal RESISTANCE (its volume over its conductivity, summed), and divides the being's exchange rate by one plus that resistance times the reserved coupling (the series-thermal-resistance form), so the buffering is a physics consequence of the matter placed, keyed off the substance's own conductivity with no shelter tag (Principles 8, 9, 11). Data and reserved: oak gains its cited therm.conductivity (0.17, a strong insulator, CRC / Incropera), and a ShelterCalib carries the reserved insulation_coupling (basis: the ratio of the barrier's conductive resistance to the being's convective resistance, the conduction-versus-convection balance; surfaced-with-basis, dev-fixture one-tenth), armed opt-in via Runner::set_shelter and off the calibrated worldbuild path until a later slice wires it. OPT-IN and hash-neutral: the attenuation runs only when shelter is armed with enclosing matter present, so a scenario with no shelter armed or no overhead matter attenuates nothing and stays byte-identical (crucible unchanged at 254bc17c, world_build 16 and world_determinism 3 replay-identical). Proven end to end (physiology_embodiment.rs a_roof_of_insulating_matter_shelters_a_being_from_a_harsh_field): a being under an oak roof holds more of its warmth in a cold field than an identical exposed being that tracks the field, and the scheduled order attenuates bit-identically to the pinned order. 815 sim tests plus 84 physics tests green, fmt and clippy (--all-targets -D warnings) clean. HONEST LIMIT: building the roof (a being placing matter overhead) is the deferred emergent technique; this slice proves the primitive that makes a built roof matter. NEXT in the cascade: the deferred slices, all independent of the item-8 owner-call (item 6 slice B the medium-oxygen gate; the overhead-deposit technique that lets a being build the roof) and the force-and-manipulation extension as a primitive-completeness check. ITEM 8 (the matter cycle) is BLOCKED on an unresolved OWNER CALL, surfaced (not resolved) per workflow 5b: the handoff (MATERIAL_SUBSTRATE_HANDOFF.md:141) flags whether the closed DecayLaw enum (trace.rs:77) should become a data-defined TransformKindRegistry keyed to a physics-kernel id, sibling to the value/semantic/institution substrates, so decomposition, corrosion, combustion, cooking, and smelting are data rows over the fixed kernel set. (My own prior handoff entries mis-wrote this as owner-RULED; corrected.) The recommendation surfaced to the owner: harden to the registry, since a live matter cycle would otherwise grow a new DecayLaw enum arm per transform mode, the closed-enum-where-content-should-emerge defect Principle 8/11 forbids; but it is the owner's call and item 8 waits on the ruling.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 6 SLICE B OXYGEN GATE (fire needs air; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, hash-neutral for existing scenarios). Closes the honest limit slices A and C both named: fire now needs air. crates/sim/src/runner.rs step_combustion reads the OXIDISER the cell's medium supplies (the reserved oxidiser_supply times the medium's respirable content, civsim_sim::medium::MediumField::respirable_at) and passes it to laws::combustion, so an oxygen-demanding fuel burns where there is air and starves in a sealed or anoxic cell (the burn goes oxidiser-limited to nothing), while a self-oxidising fuel still burns on temperature alone; a cell with no medium field reads open atmosphere (full respirable), so the earlier combustion scenarios are unchanged. Data and reserved: oak gains its cited therm.oxidiser_demand (1.2, Turns stoichiometry), and CombustionCalib gains the reserved oxidiser_supply (basis: the oxidiser mass a cell's air holds and replenishes at full respirable concentration over the base tick; surfaced-with-basis, dev-fixture large so open air is fuel-limited and only a near-anoxic medium starves the fire), keyed off the fuel's own stoichiometry and the medium's respirable content with no coded rule (Principles 8, 9). OPT-IN and hash-neutral (crucible unchanged at 254bc17c, world_build 16 and world_determinism 3 replay-identical; the open-air default keeps the existing combustion tests burning). Proven end to end (physiology_embodiment.rs an_oxygen_demanding_fire_burns_in_air_and_starves_in_an_anoxic_medium): identical hot oak burns in a rich medium and is spared in a near-anoxic one. 816 sim tests plus 84 physics tests green, fmt and clippy (--all-targets -D warnings) clean. ITEM 6 (live fire) is now COMPLETE end to end: a fuel bed burns when hot (A), needs air (B), and its fire spreads across fuel and dies behind it (C).

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 8 OWNER-CALL RULED (2026-07-06, owner-confirmed and FORMALIZED in the source, commit 6e4aee7). The catch stands: item 8's DecayLaw seam had been mis-relayed as owner-ruled while the source docs still flagged it unresolved; auditing my own handoff against the source and surfacing (not building) was the Prime-Directive-1 discipline, and the owner confirmed it was the right call. THE RULING: harden the closed DecayLaw enum (trace.rs:77) to a data-defined TransformKindRegistry keyed to a physics-kernel id, sibling to the value/semantic/institution substrates. Each kernel is a GENERAL physical law (oxidation, phase-change, biological-reduction), NEVER a named-transform arm (no combustion / cooking / decay arm). Decomposition, corrosion, combustion, cooking, and smelting are DATA ROWS over the fixed general-kernel set. North star: build the registry as a THIN DISPATCH over general kernels that could later DISSOLVE into the floor once transforms emerge from the substance's own physics, so no registry is needed at all. Item 8 (the matter cycle) is UNBLOCKED and builds on that hardened seam, with mass conservation a hard ConservationRegistry invariant across every transform.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 8 SLICE 1 (harden DecayLaw to the data-defined TransformKind; branch claude/material-substrate, HASH-NEUTRAL). The owner-ruled hardening of item 8's seam, built. crates/sim/src/trace.rs: the closed DecayLaw enum (Organic / Corroding / Static arms) becomes a data-defined TransformKind, a general TransformKernelId (the FIXED kernel set: Reaction, Corrosion, Static, each a general physical law in civsim_physics::laws, never a named transform) plus a params map keyed by name (the reserved values as data). So a new transform mode (combustion, cooking, smelting) is a new DATA ROW binding an existing kernel, never a new enum arm, sibling to the value (Part 21), semantic (Part 33), and institution-function (Part 36) substrates (Principle 11). The two consumers (organic_salience, corroding_salience) dispatch by kernel id and read named params; dev_default and the tests build the same three transforms, so the salience is byte-identical (trace tests, world_build 16 and world_determinism 3 all replay-identical). The north star is on record in the type doc: the dispatch dissolves into the floor once transforms emerge from a substance's own physics. Proven (trace.rs a_new_transform_mode_is_a_data_row_over_the_fixed_kernel_not_a_new_arm): an organic-decomposition row and a hotter combustion-like row both bind the one fixed Reaction kernel, differing only in data (barrier and rate), so adding a transform cost no code. 817 sim tests plus 84 physics tests green, fmt and clippy (--all-targets -D warnings) clean, no new reserved value (the parameters are the same reserved data the DecayLaw arms carried, now keyed by name). NEXT (item 8 proper): apply the transform kinds to a cell's substances over time (the matter cycle), conserving mass in the ConservationRegistry, so decomposition/corrosion/combustion decay or transform a cell's matter as data rows over the general kernels; then the deferred overhead-deposit technique and the force-and-manipulation completeness check.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 8 PROPER SLICE A (the world registry carries the transform physics; branch claude/material-substrate, ADDITIVE, byte-identical). The foundational slice of the matter cycle, built. crates/physics/src/lib.rs PhysicsRegistry::ground() now loads the full physics floor stack (fluids, chemistry/optics, electromagnetism, biology) onto the mechanical and ground floors, so a cell's substances carry the physics the matter cycle reads to decompose, corrode, or burn: the corrosion electrode potentials and susceptibility (chem_optics_floor chem.standard_potential / chem.corrosion_susceptibility / chem.acidity), the combustion products' ash fraction (biology_floor bio.mineral_ash_fraction), and the ambient fluids (air). This is the "dissolve into the floor" direction made real: the matter cycle reads a transform's parameters straight from the substance's own floor axes rather than a transform-kinds file, so world variation lives in the substance rows. ADDITIVE and neutral: the material-substrate derivations read specific axes by id, so a fuller registry leaves them unchanged, and worldgen fills the z-column from the ground floor's strata alone. Verified byte-identical (physiology_embodiment 23, world_build 16, world_determinism 3, the full sim suite 817, all green; crucible unchanged at 254bc17c; 84 physics tests green with the composed stack, no id conflicts). fmt and clippy (--all-targets -D warnings) clean, no new reserved value. NEXT (slice B, the transform application, the matter cycle's first observable): a matter-cycle beat applying each substance's transform over time reading its physics. DESIGN grounded: DECOMPOSITION is the cleanest first transform because its PRODUCTS emerge from the substance's OWN composition physics (the bio.mineral_ash_fraction stays as a mineral residue, the organic fractions volatilize to the air substance), so it honors read-substance-physics for both the params AND the products, and it conserves TOTAL mass by splitting (no environmental inflow). It needs a new organic substance with cited composition, a decomposition rate/barrier, the beat, the composition-derived product routing, and ConservationRegistry mass balance. Corrosion is the harder sibling (its oxide product is a substance-to-substance mapping not derivable from a Fixed axis, and it gains environmental oxygen so it conserves the metal element, not total mass), a follow-on. Then the deferred overhead-deposit technique and the force-and-manipulation completeness check.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 8 PROPER SLICE B (the matter cycle, decomposition, mass conserved exactly; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, hash-neutral). The matter cycle's first observable, built. crates/sim/src/runner.rs Runner::step_matter_cycle (inside step_field so both tick orders decompose against the settled temperature identically): for a cell whose substance carries bio.mineral_ash_fraction (the mark of organic matter, read from the substance's OWN composition physics, no tag and no race) at or above the reserved decomposition barrier, the beat removes a reserved rate-fraction of that substance's volume and moves its EXACT per-substance mass decrease (the MaterialField's own rounded mass reads, so their difference is exact) into a scalar decomposed_mass sink on the Embodiment, matter dispersed to the environment. The conserved projection sum(cell masses) + sink is invariant by construction, the hard conservation the ConservationRegistry guards with no product-volume rounding. Data and reserved: ground() loads the ground floor LAST (after biology) so a z-column substance can carry cross-domain axes, a cited "carrion" substance (mat.density, bio.mineral_ash_fraction, USDA / food-composition data) is the decomposable organic matter, and a MatterCycleCalib carries the reserved decomposition barrier (basis: the freezing point of biological water near 273 K, below which decomposition halts) and rate (basis: the decomposition timescale), surfaced-with-basis, armed opt-in via Runner::set_matter_cycle and off the calibrated worldbuild path. OPT-IN and hash-neutral: the beat runs only when armed, the sink folds into state_hash only when non-zero, so a scenario with no matter cycle armed is byte-identical (crucible 254bc17c, world_build 16 and world_determinism 3 replay-identical). Proven end to end (physiology_embodiment.rs organic_matter_decomposes_when_warm_and_the_matter_cycle_conserves_mass): warm carrion rots down while a frozen cell is preserved, the ConservationRegistry sees the total mass invariant across many ticks, and the scheduled order matches the pinned. 818 sim tests plus 84 physics tests green, fmt and clippy (--all-targets -D warnings) clean. HONEST LIMIT: the decomposed mass disperses to a scalar sink (its gases and leached minerals leave the cell); re-materialising it into soil and air substances (the ash fraction to a mineral residue, the volatile to the air, which reintroduces the volume-rounding and needs a residual-mass mechanism) is slice C. NEXT: slice C (the product re-materialization), then the deferred overhead-deposit technique and the force-and-manipulation completeness check, then the whole-arc blind concept-verify and the gate's sign-off before merge.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 8 PROPER (decomposition parameters dissolve into the substance's own physics; branch claude/material-substrate, behaviour-preserving, hash-neutral). The gate's slice-B direction note applied: the decomposition barrier and rate were a GLOBAL calib, but the settled read-substance-physics direction is that a transform reads its parameters from the substance's OWN physics-floor axes. The barrier becomes a per-substance CITED biology-floor axis (bio.decomposition_barrier, unit K): carrion carries 273, cited to the freezing point of its tissue water, the substance's own thermal gate; the mechanism reads it per-substance and a substance with no barrier axis does not decompose (no global fallback, the barrier is its physical gate). The rate becomes a per-substance biology-floor axis (bio.decomposition_rate, the reserved per-substance timescale, fantasy-provenance not cited); no substance declares a concrete rate yet, so the matter cycle falls back to the global reserved MatterCycleCalib.decomposition_rate, now the only field on that calib. No value fabricated. Behaviour-preserving (carrion's floor barrier equals the retired calib barrier, its rate falls back to the same global), so the conservation test decomposes identically and the baseline stays byte-identical (crucible 254bc17c). The biology floor now carries 22 axes; the floors count test is updated. This is the north star made concrete: the parameters dissolved into the floor, the registry one step closer to needing no calib at all.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 8 PROPER SLICE C1 (the matter cycle re-materialises into located soil nutrients; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, hash-neutral). The decomposed mass no longer disperses to a placeless scalar: it re-materialises into a per-cell SOIL NUTRIENT store (crates/sim/src/material.rs SoilNutrientField, a sparse per-cell per-class mass store sibling to FireField, the opt-in empty-default), located at the cell where the carrion rots and split into nutrient CLASSES by the substance's own composition (the mineral-ash fraction to a mineral class, the remainder to an organic class). Mass-valued rather than volume-valued, so the deposit is EXACT (no volume-quantisation rounding, the friction that blocked depositing products as volumes), and the split conserves the loss bit for bit because the organic share is the REMAINDER after the mineral share. The Embodiment's decomposed_mass scalar becomes a soil: SoilNutrientField (decomposed_mass() now returns soil.total()); the state_hash folds the store only when non-empty. Sum(cell masses) + soil store total is invariant, byte-identical for the unarmed baseline (254bc17c, world_build 16, world_determinism 3). The conservation test now also asserts the located, class-split deposit (both classes present at the rot cell, summing to the whole loss, all at that cell, the organic residue outweighing the small mineral ash).

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 8 PROPER SLICE C2 (the matter cycle closes into the food web: soil fertilises productivity; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, hash-neutral). The loop's last leg: the nutrient the matter cycle deposits into the soil now feeds the cell's productivity, so a cell where a carcass rotted grows more where soil is the limiting factor. Dead matter becomes soil nutrient becomes producer biomass. crates/sim/src/environ.rs: EnvironFields gains a per-cell fertility vector filled from the soil store by set_fertility_from (scaled by the reserved fertility scale), and step_productivity reads soil_baseline + fertility as the soil Liebig supply (the soil_baseline was flagged in the code as a placeholder until a per-cell soil field lands; this is that field, sourced by decomposition). The fertility is a pure derived read of the embodiment's soil store (which folds itself), so it is not folded into state_hash; its effect enters through the capacity it shifts. MatterCycleCalib gains fertility_scale (RESERVED, basis: the decomposed nutrient mass that raises a soil-limited cell's soil supply by one soil requirement, so a carcass fully fertilises the ground it fell on; dev-fixture 1/1000, on the opt-in calib, no manifest key, no fabricated value). The runner fills the environ fertility from the embodiment's soil store before env.step, only when the matter cycle is armed, so the baseline stays byte-identical (254bc17c, world_build 16, world_determinism 3). Proven (environ.rs decomposed_soil_fertility_lifts_productivity_where_soil_is_the_limiting_factor): under a soil-limited calibration every cell is soil-starved to zero capacity, and depositing nutrient at one viable cell lifts its capacity above zero while an equally-viable unfertilised cell stays barren, the lift local to the deposit. THE MATTER CYCLE IS CLOSED: a corpse rots, its mass enriches the ground it fell on by nutrient class, conserved, and that enrichment feeds the food web. HONEST LIMIT: fertility raises the soil supply catalytically (the abstract Liebig source is not mass-conserved through plant uptake, the productivity model's existing limit), and volatilising the organic share to the air is a follow-on. NEXT: corrosion (the harder transform sibling), the deferred overhead-deposit technique, the force-and-manipulation completeness check, then the whole-arc blind concept-verify and the gate's sign-off before merge.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE ITEM 7 OVERHEAD-DEPOSIT TECHNIQUE (a being builds its own roof; branch claude/material-substrate, OPT-IN, hash-neutral). The emergent build the shelter primitive (item 7 slice A) was waiting for, completing item 7: a being sets the insulating matter it carries down into the cell directly OVERHEAD, so the roof it raises is one it CHOSE to build, and that self-built roof then attenuates its own body-to-field thermal exchange (slice A's shelter read). Shelter EMERGES from need plus the deposit affordance plus carried matter, no shelter verb (Principles 8, 9). The new SHELTER affordance (AffordanceId 9, in the builder fixture only so the crucible path is untouched) is the upward sibling of RELEASE: where RELEASE mounds the ground underfoot, SHELTER (Embodiment::deposit_overhead) sets the carried load into the cell one z above the being, placing matter in the air where the exchange reads it as enclosing matter (no earthwork column rises, the matter is a roof in the air). The run-path decision layer defers a winning SHELTER decision alongside the other matter affordances, and the enactment calls deposit_overhead; AffordanceRegistry::dev_builder adds the shelter output. OPT-IN and hash-neutral (fixture-only, so the crucible is byte-identical at 254bc17c, world_build 16, world_determinism 3). Proven (physiology_embodiment.rs a_being_builds_its_own_roof_overhead_and_that_self_built_roof_shelters_it): a being whose evolved controller decides SHELTER raises its carried oak as a roof and carries nothing more, a blank founder holding the same load never builds, and over a cold field the being under the roof it built holds more of its warmth than the identical founder that never raised it. So the shelter is one the being chose to build, the physics consequence of the matter it placed. Item 7 is complete: the mechanism (overhead matter buffers) and the emergent build (a being raises its own roof) both stand.

MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE FORCE-AND-MANIPULATION PRIMITIVE-COMPLETENESS CHECK (the owner's addendum, reframed by the steering discipline; the arc's last piece). Per the owner's steering (primitives coded, techniques emergent), the addendum is a COMPLETENESS CHECK on the manipulation primitive substrate, not a verb-build list. The audit of the surface: the manipulation primitives cover ACQUIRING matter (GRASP loose matter strength-bounded, EXTRACT bonded matter fracture-gated, DIG excavate-and-lower, GEOPHAGE eat-for-composition), PLACING matter (RELEASE set-down-and-mound, SHELTER deposit-overhead-as-roof), CONSUMING matter (INGEST forage, GEOPHAGE), SHAPING matter (CRAFT knap-a-tool), and DAMAGING with matter (STRIKE natural-weapon). Each is body-grounded (a limb, a mouth, a natural weapon) and physics-gated (strength versus weight for the carry, force versus fracture for extract and dig, edibility satisfaction for the ingests), so each is correctly a coded PRIMITIVE. The owner's gap-list classifies cleanly: WEAVE, DAM, MIX, STACK, CACHE, GIVE, FORGE, FERMENT, CAST are TECHNIQUES that must EMERGE from sequencing these primitives against real physics, never coded as verbs, and the arc already proves the pattern (terracing emerges from dig-then-release, the mining loop from mine-craft-mine, self-built shelter from carry-then-deposit-overhead, a dam from releasing matter into a watercourse the hydrology already reads). FINDING: the material-substrate arc's manipulation primitive set is COMPLETE, and its techniques emerge from the primitives, so no new verb is needed to land the arc. THE ONE GENUINE PRIMITIVE GAP is the FORCE-APPLICATION family: a being applying its muscle force to matter it does NOT first acquire, or through a held object (PUSH/SHOVE/DRAG/ROLL a boulder, THROW a carried object as a projectile, LEVER for mechanical advantage, STRIKE-WITH-A-HELD-OBJECT reading the wielded tool's geometry rather than only the natural weapon, the owner's top pick). This family is body-grounded (muscle force) and physics-gated (the mechanical floor's force, lever, friction, and ballistics laws), absent from the substrate today, and coherent as a FOLLOW-ON ARC (it needs a facing direction, cross-cell matter motion or projectile travel, and the force-versus-resistance contest), named and scoped rather than faked. THREE CONSOLIDATION DEBTS are the walk-back toward emergence (the direction of travel, not blockers, each a signed-off first cut): the DEPOSIT verbs (RELEASE underfoot-mound, SHELTER overhead-roof, the carry put-down) should collapse into ONE DEPOSIT primitive with a target/direction parameter (AffordanceParam::Directional already exists), not a verb per direction (the gate's twice-flagged note); DIG and EXTRACT are near-duplicate ground-working verbs to unify into one primitive with a selective-versus-bulk parameter (TODOS #60); CRAFT/knapping is a coded technique that should emerge from strike-a-core-and-the-fracture-throws-flakes (TODOS #61). So the completeness check lands as its finding: the primitive substrate is complete for the arc, the force-application family is the next primitive arc, and the three consolidations are the emergence direction. THE MATERIAL-SUBSTRATE CASCADE ARC IS COMPLETE (items 1 through 8 plus the overhead-deposit technique and this check); ready for the whole-arc blind concept-verify and the gate's close-out.

A gap survey on the owner's local models (two Qwen workers split across mechanical, ingestive, body, locomotive, constructive, and social modes) surfaced a FORCE-AND-MANIPULATION extension to build after item 4, each held to the one rule (need plus grown physics-derived affordance plus structured matter, founder-zero, physics-gated): the force affordances (THROW, PUSH/DRAG, LEVER, DAM, and STRIKE-WITH-A-HELD-OBJECT, the biggest unbuilt rider, with strike-with-a-held-object the top pick since it is the recursive tool loop that rides the crafting seam), INGEST-FOR-COMPOSITION (geophagy, the need-side complement to harm-learning), FLOAT/RAFT, BURROW, MIX/KNEAD, STACK/ASSEMBLE, WEAVE/BIND, CACHE/HOARD, and GIVE/TRANSFER. ARC SEQUENCING UPDATE and the ideation / organ-flux decisions (owner, 2026-07-05). A local-model survey audited the other arcs (emergent anatomy, biosphere-into-run, communication-reach) for holes, and two deeper design explorations (ideation, organ interdependence) were run. Findings and the owner's calls:

Other-arcs audit: all three arcs want expansion. Anatomy and biosphere both surfaced the same keystone, a GROWN CONTROL / SIGNAL substrate: the arcs grow the body and derive its function, but the controller that connects a sensor to an actuator is an abstract genome-keyed network wired by canonical-index slot, with no signal-propagation substrate (confirmed in controller.rs). Whether to grow the control (a signal-propagation substrate where the wiring emerges) or keep it as a level-of-detail abstraction is an owner-call. Biosphere also carries sharp steering catches in its own scope language, to fix before it builds: "per-race physiology vector" is a per-race table (derive per-genome instead), "food-web closure" validation authors the web topology (validate on energy-persistence instead, let the web emerge), "species set" is a catalog (seed a stream of genomes, species emerges as a cluster), and "trait axes" must be morphogen/physiology scalars, not functional categories. Communication-reach as scoped is transport-only and needs three substrate primitives to carry information (modulation, receiver filtering, medium persistence), all physics, not a lexicon.

THE IDEATION ARC IS NEXT (owner-directed). Q1, how a being comes up with the idea to do a thing (learn it can chop a tree for wood), is the piece that makes every built affordance stop being dormant: today grasp, extract, craft, dig, geophage, and release are founder-zero with only blind evolutionary search to discover them, so behaviour barely steps out of the substrate. The ideation arc extends the harm-learning associative engine from its aversive side to the appetitive side (credit a primitive sequence when a reserve rises), adds an action-as-hypothesis representation (affordance-bound sampling of primitive sequences, no coded verb), a forward-model prediction-error exploration drive (curiosity as surprise-minimization), and belief-graph planning in the cognition tier. Owner ruling: implement it as the very next arc after materials, or we never see behaviour emerge from the work. It is scoped in docs/working/IDEATION_DISCOVERY_HANDOFF.md (grounded against the tree; the appetitive learner extends the harm engine verbatim, the one new mechanism is an eligibility trace; recommended first slice 1a, the reward twin of is_harm_tick).

THE ORGAN-FLUX / CONTROL arc is deferred but added. Q2, organs operable and interdependent, resolves elegantly: the flux graph is the grown body's own geometry adjacency, edge-weighted by conductance derived from tissue permeability and geometry, carrying gradient-driven fluxes (fluids, heat, and signals) so interdependence emerges from path-dependency (an organ operates only if its delivered supply meets demand; damage collapses a downstream gradient and cascades), the whole-body aggregates become supply-limited reads rather than pure sums, and the flux solve is a fixed-point, order-independent, LOD-collapsible fine tier that reverts to today's sums when zoomed out. The key unification: a nervous SIGNAL is one more flux on the same derived graph, so this arc IS the R-ORGAN-FLUX item AND the answer to the grown-control keystone above, one derived-transport network over the grown body. Deferred behind ideation, but queued as a planned arc.

Revised arc order: materials (in progress, PR #93), then the IDEATION arc (next), then biosphere-into-run (with the steering fixes) and communication-reach (with the three substrate primitives), with the ORGAN-FLUX / CONTROL arc slotted where the owner prefers after ideation. The full survey material lives in the session scratchpad pending a decision on persisting it as research-backlog flags.

FIDELITY GOALS ADDED, object/organism spatial extent and per-part structure-level matter (owner, 2026-07-05). Probing the fire model surfaced that combustion is per-cell (per-substance ignition within a tile, one aggregate intensity per cell, cell-to-cell spread), with no multi-tile object and no sub-tile spread. The owner ruled that the fidelity pieces named should be goals on an arc if not already scoped. Audit: object IDENTITY is scoped (a tool or relic mints a StableId with a single-Coord3 location, MATERIAL_SUBSTRATE_HANDOFF.md object-identity rider), and biosphere-as-organisms is the biosphere-into-run arc. Two sub-parts are NOT yet scoped and are added here as explicit goals, both held to emergence (derive from the grown structure, never authored):

- OBJECT AND ORGANISM SPATIAL EXTENT. A thing (an identified object or a grown organism) may occupy MULTIPLE cells as one entity, its footprint DERIVED from its geometry against the cell size (a boulder's volume, a tree's grown height and canopy spread from the morphogen anatomy and plant.max_height), never an authored "trees are 3x3". Extends the object-identity rider's single-Coord3 location to a derived multi-cell extent, and rides the biosphere arc for a living organism's extent. Deferred, queued behind ideation.

- PER-PART STRUCTURE-LEVEL MATTER AND FIRE. The materials and fire model reads a thing's STRUCTURE (its parts, each with its own geometry and tissue composition from the per-part body), so combustion, wear, and damage happen per part with intra-object spread (a tree's dense trunk and light canopy ignite at their own therm.ignition_temperature and burn by their own therm.fuel_value), rather than the current aggregate where a corpse or object collapses to one cell Composition. The per-part body already exists (anatomy, R-BUILD-PHYS) and the fire model already reads per-substance ignition at the cell level; this extends that read from the cell aggregate to the grown per-part structure. Couples object-identity (materials), the biosphere (an organism's parts as harvestable and combustible matter), the matter cycle (a corpse decaying per part), and the anatomy structure tier. Deferred, queued.

Both are fidelity increases, not blockers: the per-cell-with-per-substance model is a sound resolution and the current arcs proceed on it. These goals reserve the object-and-structure-level fidelity as an explicit target on the object-identity, biosphere, and anatomy arcs, so it is built when those arcs reach it rather than lost.

IDEATION VIABILITY ARC, REWARD-CREDIT TIMING FIX (2026-07-06, branch claude/viability-world, PR #96, owner-ruled path 1, commit 9c0912c). Building the owner's ruling-B demonstration (a free founder-zero population evolving the eat-the-oilseed technique on its own) surfaced a latent off-by-one in the ideation piece-1 reward-credit path (slice 1c). GATE: crates/sim/src/runner.rs couple_conversation, the eligibility-trace record versus the reward-credit read. The bug: the trace recorded a being's decided affordance AFTER the reward-credit read, so an IMMEDIATE reserve rise (geophage and ingest refill the reserve the tick they are enacted) credited the PREVIOUS tick's action, not the one that caused it; the just-enacted action got zero eligibility for its own reward. It was masked because every controlled proof (the mechanism test, the piece-1 reward tests) eats every tick, so the prior action is the same action, and it inverted the "eating pays off" belief to NEUTRAL for a free being that eats intermittently. Found by instrumenting the reward pass (reward ticks about 1 to 4 percent, GEOPHAGE credited REWARDS to NEUTRAL about 1:6 to 1:36), traced to the tick order, held rather than touched until the owner ruled. THE FIX: move the trace decay-and-record to BEFORE the credit read (the standard TD-lambda order), so an immediate reward credits the action that caused it and a truly lagged reward still rides the decayed trace. Scoped to the reward-credit path; the harm learner (feature_observations, trace-free) is untouched. RE-PROVED: the_viability_loop_closes still forms REWARDS; the piece-1 reward tests hold; every harm test unchanged; crucible world_build 17 + world_determinism 3 byte-identical; the default unarmed run_world byte-identical at a465919e (the reward learner is inert without arming); fmt and clippy clean. The armed discovery and viability scenarios re-baseline (expected). The fix WORKS: with it a free run forms the reward belief and the reader's reward-belief count RISES OFF ZERO (was flat zero before). HONEST LIMIT ON THE FULL SWEEP: the reward is a recovery-from-hunger signal, so a large competitive population stays hungry and the belief forms and rises, but the lethal seed-hunger selection that would spread it to the whole population crashes the population and the crash removes the food competition that made beings hungry (reported to the gate with the curve and two paths for the sweep, comment 4896477737). SIBLING (not yet built, will land in this pass): the belief-key bucket-consistency bug across candidate_bindings/candidate_weight (discovery.rs), the reward credit (runner.rs), and appetitive_salience (learn.rs), plus the generalization-granularity owner-call (bucket over the target's perceived physics at a just-noticeable difference, not the primitive alone).

IDEATION VIABILITY ARC, GRADED REPRODUCTIVE-VIGOR COUPLING and BELIEF-KEY FIX (2026-07-06, branch claude/viability-world, PR #96, owner-ruled path 2, commits 8472cdc and 330df54). The owner ruled path 2 for the ruling-B spread: couple the seed-hunger to a GRADED reproductive cost rather than a hard death, so an eater out-reproduces a non-eater and selection spreads the eating lineage without the mass-starvation crash that the lethal variant caused. LANDED (opt-in, byte-identical unarmed): World carries a per-being reproductive_vigor map (a probability the reproduce beat reads as pairing eligibility, gated by a MATE_CHOICE-phase draw on a dedicated slot); the Runner feeds it from a coupled reserve level each tick through an opt-in ReproductiveVigorCalib (vigor = floor + (1 - floor) * reserve_level, floor reserved with basis). Proven by a new reproduction test (the gradient is monotone, byte-identical at full vigor, replays bit for bit), the viability primed test still forms REWARDS, the crucible byte-identical, the default run byte-identical at a465919e. The BELIEF-KEY consistency bug was folded in the same pass: candidate_weight (discovery.rs) now looks up the reward belief on the primitive-only subject, consistent with the reward credit, appetitive_salience, the planner, and the surprise read (it had keyed on the affordance channel, which never matched the primitive-keyed belief except on channel zero). THE DEMONSTRATION (commit 330df54, opt-in --scenario viability, seed 11, 6 races, 10 bands, 100 generations): the population stays large and stable (57 to 75, NO crash); the heritable exploration propensity SWEEPS off founder-zero to about 65 percent of the population (2 to 49 beings); the reward-belief count rises off zero, peaks near 30 percent around generation 40, then FADES as the swept-in eater population becomes well-fed and stops feeling the reward rise (reward-as-recovery from the satiation side). THE FINDING reported to the gate: the durable form of the discovered technique is the SELECTED behavioural disposition (the heritable exploration propensity), not the momentary reward belief (a transient learning scaffold that fades into habit); the belief COUNT cannot climb to the whole population under the current substrate because a reward is a felt rise and a satiated being feels none, so making it sweep would need belief PERSISTENCE or HERITABILITY (design decisions surfaced to the gate). TWO BLIND-PANEL FINDINGS DEFERRED (handoff note only): a nutrition/edibility affordance-percept, and keying the reward belief on the target's quantized perceived-scalar value at a just-noticeable difference rather than the affordance channel or the primitive alone.
