ARC 2 (RELATIONAL-BELIEF SUBSTRATE) LANDED (2026-07-07, branch claude/agent-handoff-audit-ikmsdy). A belief whose HEAD is another belief's SUBJECT: a Mind.relations store of (head, relation, tail) edges over {RELATES, UNRELATED}, inferred by the SAME evidence engine as a first-order belief (a relation is LEARNED from correlated evidence, never handed), folded into state_hash empty-neutral (agent.rs). The vocabulary (learn.rs): RELATES/UNRELATED and YIELDS (the one built-in causal relation kind, a reserved-high attr disjoint from HARM/REWARD). The MULTI-HOP planner plan_chain (planning.rs): seeds from the one-hop plan_toward frontier (kept as the primitive, tests intact) then traverses relations_into BACKWARD from each goal subject, prepending the antecedent that brings it about, up to a reserved hop_cap (STEPS; a k-step plan chains k-1 edges), ranked weakest-link-confidence desc / shorter-first / support desc / canonical (a strict total order). A being with no relation degenerates to the one-hop lookup exactly. Wired on the run-path deliberation (runner.rs), byte-identical for a relationless being (the only kind today, so run_world is unchanged). This is the seed of tool-reasoning: a being that believes "cutting pays off" and "striking yields cutting" chains them to strike first, a goal one hop cannot reach (falsifier a_being_chains_two_beliefs_to_reach_a_goal_a_single_hop_cannot). DEEP BLIND AUDIT (the owner-flagged planner spot): a three-skeptic repo-walled panel on a tests-and-docs-stripped packet confirmed byte-neutrality and determinism (no off-by-one on chain length, strict total order, no ties, safe against both crash targets), and caught on TWO independent lenses ONE real seam: the planner traversed ANY committed-RELATES edge as a causal means-ends edge regardless of relation KIND, an authored universal that turns wrong the moment a non-causal relation kind is added. HARDENED per Principle 9 and the "harden the closed list one level down" discipline: plan_chain now takes a DATA-defined reachable causal-kind set (learn::builtin_reachable_relations, today {YIELDS}); a kind absent from the set is inert to the planner (default-off), proven by a_non_causal_relation_kind_is_inert_to_the_planner_by_default. Reserved planning.hop_cap surfaced-with-basis (manifest + dev fixture 4), never fabricated. Byte-neutral (run_world a465919e, crucible world_build 17 + world_determinism 3 green, 692 lib + 886 integration green, fmt/clippy clean). FLAGGED, both to take BEFORE arc 3 forms dense relation graphs: (1) plan_chain enumerates every simple path to a goal with no cross-chain dedup (~b^(hop_cap-1) chains for a dense graph, terminating and deterministic and INERT today since no relation is formed on the run path yet; remediation a best-first widest-path traversal bounded by edges); (2) the SEQ_FIELD_BITS 16-value bound. Also noted: DiscoveryCalib has no from_manifest yet, so plan_hop_cap/plan_depth_cap live in the dev fixture until that wiring reads them fail-loud. NEXT: arc 3 the made world (matter that affords a USE; tool-use, then composition, then artifacts; start with the simplest usable tool), where relations get FORMED on the run path (consider_relation is the clean seam); then arc 4 (GPU blueprint + Rayon). The richer-observability thread (now including a per-relation reader) is parallel.

ARC 3 (THE MADE WORLD) OPENED; TOOL-USE AUTHORING PURGED, DERIVED FROM PHYSICS (2026-07-07, branch claude/agent-handoff-audit-ikmsdy). Slice 1a (afford-from-tool) landed: a wielded tool's capability enters the same affordance derivation a body part's does, so a keen edge grants a CUT the barehanded forager lacks (crates/sim/src/{affordance_percept,homeostasis,runner}.rs), opt-in, byte-neutral, unit-proven. Then a SIX-AGENT completely-blind sweep (three authoring lenses, three gap lenses, each fed only the tool surface under the rule "the physics substrate is the ONLY authored place, everything else derived, no exceptions") found the tool system authoring what a tool does, and found two structural roots (WieldedTool too thin to carry mass/wear/geometry; the CapabilityKernel enum closed at Pierce so no non-piercing action is expressible). The complete list and the derive-from-physics sections A through I are in docs/working/TOOL_SUBSTRATE_PLAN.md. Landed (each byte-neutral, run_world a465919e and crucible unchanged, falsifier-backed, checkpoint-audited): Section A (the derived cut, no cut_yields map: cut_underfoot severs the cell's own composite constituents per each one's mat.fracture_strength, freeing the strength-bounded carry, distinct from EXTRACT's aggregate gate); Section B (the derived craft edge, no edge_area constant: new law civsim_physics::laws::edge_area_at, the inverse of contact_pressure, derives the finest edge from the worked stone's fracture strength, the fittest stone chosen by the derived cutting power min(fracture,hardness)); Section C (the tool as matter: WieldedTool retains its volume so mass=density*volume is recoverable, enabling wear/impact). A two-agent checkpoint blind panel (physics-only seat + correctness; determinism + crash) confirmed the two CRITICAL authoring defects genuinely fixed and determinism/byte-neutrality intact, and drove three applied fixes (mass checked_mul; craft fitness by min(fracture,hardness) not Pierce-argmax; the cut's pressure cap made an overflow guard not a borrowed pressure_max, decoupling cut from extraction). THREE physics refinements surfaced and recorded (not yet fixed, they need the deeper substrate): R-EDGE-INTRINSIC (the edge is force-derived so cutting is force-insensitive and maker-dependent; the correct edge is an intrinsic material length scale, a new axis), R-CUT-DEPTH (the cut is carry-bounded not depth-sized; needs cut_penetrate + a mat.specific_cut_energy axis), R-CUT-SHEAR (the sever gate is normal-stress not shear; needs a shear capability kernel, root R1). Commits a9eb09f (A), eb6012c (B), 48a2bc4 (C), plus the checkpoint fixes. NEXT: Sections D (wear), E (breakage), F (kernel expansion, root R1), G (new derived actions), H (composite tools), I (identity/thermal), per the plan; then the biosphere wiring (organisms made of usable material stuff; decomposition as emergence, docs/working/BIOSPHERE_WIRING_NOTES.md); then arc 4 (GPU + Rayon). The SEQ_FIELD_BITS 16-value belief-subject bound and the plan_chain simple-path bound both come due as arc 3 densifies.

PERFORMANCE: PROFILED FIRST, REGROW ALLOCATION CHURN FIXED (2026-07-07, branch claude/perf-regrow-profiling). Before wiring any GPU offload, PROFILED where a tick's wall-clock goes, swept across grid size and population, with real numbers (crate::profile, behind CIVSIM_PROFILE, timing-only so determinism is untouched; a CIVSIM_W/CIVSIM_H grid knob added to run_world for the sweep). The data OVERTURNED the GPU blueprint's ranking. The field-diffusion stencil the blueprint ranks target 1 is 0.4 to 1.6 percent at every scale (worthless to offload). At the current small grid (32x24) per-being EMBODIMENT dominates (54 to 59 percent), and arming tools/social/biosphere grows exactly that. At large grids ENV+REGROW explodes to 89 to 99 percent, and within it regrow_supply is nearly the whole cost (82 to 90 percent). Root cause: regrow_supply rebuilt a fresh Composition (two String key allocations, two map allocations, a struct, a BTreeMap<Coord3> insert) for every cell every tick, millions of heap allocations per tick at scale. FIXED byte-neutral, because the stored values fold into state_hash, not the allocation path that builds them: Composition::set_nutrient / set_toxin update in place with the key interned once, and ResourceField::composition_mut gives one tree access per cell, so regrow writes food/water/salinity in place and allocates nothing after the first tick. Result: 35 percent faster at 256x192 (22.5s to 14.6s), byte-identical PROVEN at both scales (crucible 254bc17c and a before/after 256x192 hash diff, both 310bc447), determinism harness 14/14, 36 sim tests green. REMAINING: regrow is still about 70 percent of a large-grid tick, now the BTreeMap<Coord3, Composition> tree ops rather than the allocations; a dense-field representation is the next large-grid lever but an invasive core refactor. The GPU field pipeline (blueprint target 1) is DE-PRIORITIZED by the data. Open fork for the owner: large-grid scaling (regrow, then a dense field) versus dense-population scaling (per-being embodiment, which arming the mechanisms grows), which decides the next optimization target.

PERFORMANCE: RAYON WAS A NET LOSS AT REALISTIC SCALE, NOW THRESHOLDED (2026-07-07, branch claude/perf-regrow-profiling). Benchmarked the arc-4 Rayon per-being parallelization (which had been verified for determinism but never for speed). It is SLOWER than serial below about 8000 founders: at 16x20 founders the embodiment phase is 1.46s serial versus 2.44s at 18 threads, and body_exchange is 6x slower parallel. The per-being work per item is too small to amortize Rayon's work-stealing overhead until the population is enormous. FIXED byte-neutral with a PAR_MIN_LEN=4096 threshold via with_min_len on the seven per-being par_iter sites in runner.rs, so a par_iter runs as a single job below the crossover (no split, no overhead) and hands Rayon only populations large enough to pay; the result stays bit-identical at any thread count (each item writes a fixed position and draws RNG by id, never by thread). At 18 threads body_exchange dropped 37x (0.48s to 0.013s), the Rayon penalty removed; crucible 254bc17c, determinism harness 14/14 with the one-versus-many invariance intact, 36 sim tests green. The evolve and genome per-generation par_iters are left parallel (heavy per-genome episode scoring amortizes the overhead there). PAR_MIN_LEN is a performance threshold, not a canonical value: it cannot move the state hash. The env stencils (6 to 11 percent, per-tick full-grid allocations) and the dense-field refactor are deferred per the owner's cheap-wins-first call.

GPU FIELD OFFLOAD WIRED (behind --features gpu), EMPIRICALLY CONFIRMED DEAD WEIGHT AT CURRENT SCALE (2026-07-07, docs/working/GPU_BLUEPRINT.md, branch claude/gpu-field-offload). On the owner's call to wire the GPU in, the field-stencil cross-tick pipeline is implemented and proven bit-identical on the 5090, then measured to have no point at any current scale. Built: crates/gpu FieldResident (the split form of gpu_field_step; dispatch uploads and launches async, readback is the single CUDA-event fence, both on one owning thread debug-asserted; both handles held until the fence; a test-only readback-delay for timing invariance). crates/sim: a `gpu` cargo feature (optional civsim-gpu dep, off by default so the default build stays device-free and byte-identical), a cfg-gated Runner.gpu_field armed via arm_gpu_field, Field temp_bits/set_temp_from_bits, and the step_field splice (readback replaces the sync Field::step at the head; dispatch after step_combustion over the frozen post-combustion field). run_world arms it behind CIVSIM_GPU_FIELD. A de-risk workflow (CubeCL async API map, adversarial determinism verify, synthesized plan) grounded every call and cleared all five determinism probes: Field.temp is private with only step and add_heat writing it (neither in the overlap window), the kernel is a pure disjoint-write map, the fence changes only park time, a dropped final dispatch is host-inert, and no thresholded par_iter wraps a GPU call. PROVEN bit-identical: default crucible 254bc17c and default run_world 30d2358c unchanged with the feature off; the feature-on armed run 30d2358c matches the CPU path. EMPIRICAL VERDICT, a 5000-pop 512x384 world over 3 gens: CPU 22.5s versus GPU 21.7s (within noise), both hash f0f8b917; field.step is 1.7 to 3.2 percent while regrow is 77 to 79 percent, so no current scale rewards offloading the field, and the GPU field phase is itself slower (0.58s versus 0.33s, the transfer tax exceeding the stencil). Banked as a proven, determinism-safe GPU-in-the-tick foundation the next offload (a dense regrow kernel, or the per-being matvec at huge population) reuses wholesale; the field offload stays off.

RAYON THRESHOLD RECALIBRATED (PAR_MIN_LEN 4096 to 2048, same branch). The earlier "net loss below 8000 founders" rested on a CAPPED-grid sweep: the 32x24 grid limited the sustained population, so founding count mislabelled the crossover. A grid-sized sweep (grid scaled to the population) shows the heavy per-being embodiment maps WIN parallel from a low sustained walker count (1.36x at roughly ten thousand walkers, marginal by a few thousand), while the tiny-work body_exchange never benefits (0.44x even at big population). PAR_MIN_LEN set to 2048; a per-phase serial pin for body_exchange is a noted refinement. Byte-neutral (with_min_len value cannot move the hash); crucible 254bc17c, harness 14/14.

PERF STACK BLIND-AUDITED OPEN-ENDED (2026-07-07, owner corrected a confirmation-bias defect in the method). The first perf audit was CONFIRMATORY: it handed the panel my three conclusions (byte-neutral, timing-only, threshold-safe) and asked them to verify, which manufactured agreement and a blind spot. Re-run NEUTRAL (Fable biology-stripped and repo-walled, plus repo-access Haiku and local Qwen, packet carrying only code + access pattern + the determinism invariant, NO conclusions or hints). The neutral panel converged on real improvements the confirmatory one never surfaced, ranked by impact: (1) DOMINANT: ResourceField is BTreeMap<Coord3, Composition> with String-keyed per-cell maps, but regrow writes every cell every tick so it is DENSE; blind Fable found this independently (the biased packet had to be told "dense"). Fix: dense structure-of-arrays indexed y*w+x plus interned class ids; ~10x-50x on the sweep, speeds every supply/take/source. (2) ResourceField::axes() is O(axes x cells), a full-grid rescan per axis, called per-walker per-tick inside perceive/step_with_field_dirs; fix by loop inversion or an incremental per-class nonzero counter (Fable + Haiku converged). (3) the GPU offload does NOT overlap in practice: create_from_slice may block, it allocates two device buffers and round-trips the whole field plus a .to_vec() copy every tick, no residency (Fable + Haiku + the empirical 0.8s/22.5s converge). (4) FieldResident::dispatch has NO guard against overwriting a pending pair (latent use-after-free of a dropped handle under a queued kernel); not reachable in the current readback-then-dispatch wiring but unenforced; fix an assert (Fable). (5) phase_body_exchange rebuilds the insulation map from a full material scan every tick (Haiku); cache and invalidate. (6) body_exchange never benefits from parallel (0.44x even at big pop) yet is parallelized at PAR_MIN_LEN; per-phase serial pin wanted (converged). (7) axes_here allocates a Vec per item per tick. FIXED HERE: the profiler had a DEAD "other" bucket (index 8 never written, always 0.0 percent, silently omitting the unwrapped phases); Fable caught it; now a P_TICK scope wraps the whole tick as the real denominator and the remainder prints as an honest "unwrapped" line (byte-identical, crucible 254bc17c). The rest are the next perf arc: dense-field SoA + interning is the dominant one and is now independently validated, not just my prior claim.

PERF AUDIT CHEAP HARDENINGS LANDED (2026-07-07, branch claude/audit-profiler-fix). Two byte-neutral fixes from the neutral open-ended audit: (1) FieldResident::dispatch now asserts pending.is_none() before overwriting, a fail-loud guard (kept in release, one Option check per tick) against the latent use-after-free Fable flagged (a double dispatch would drop a live device handle under a queued kernel); not reachable in the current readback-then-dispatch wiring but now enforced. (2) phase_body_exchange runs SERIAL (plain iter, not the thresholded par_iter): the audit measured it never benefits from Rayon (0.44x even at big pop), and the pin drops its 18-thread cost from 0.48s to 0.01s, matching serial. Byte-identical (crucible 254bc17c, harness 14/14). STILL OPEN as the next perf arc (bigger, alongside the GPU interleave rework): the dense-field SoA + class-id interning (dominant), axes() hoisted out of the per-walker loop (its result is field-global but recomputed per walker), and the per-tick insulation-map rebuild cache.

GPU INTERLEAVE NOW OVERLAPS (flush fix, 2026-07-07, same branch). The neutral audit found the cross-tick offload did not overlap: nothing flushed the stream after the async launch, so the kernel sat queued until the readback fence triggered it (no concurrency), and the empirical 0.8s/22.5s and the field.step readback at 0.58s versus the CPU's 0.33s both showed it. FIX: FieldResident::dispatch now calls client.flush() after the launch, submitting the kernel to the device without waiting, so it BEGINS executing concurrently with this tick's CPU tail. Measured: field.step (the readback) dropped 0.58s to 0.32s at 512x384, now matching the CPU stencil, so the kernel plus transfer is hidden under the tail. Byte-identical (armed run still f0f8b917, default crucible 254bc17c, feature-gated off). HONEST VERDICT unchanged at current scale: the total is still 22.5s because the field is under 2 percent (regrow dominates at 78 percent), so hiding the field latency is invisible in the wall-clock. The machinery is now correct and overlapping and ready for a target that matters (a dense regrow kernel, or the per-being matvec at huge population); the field offload itself stays off. Fable's blind serial-stencil audit (same run) additionally flagged, for the perf arc: the env stencils allocate four n-sized buffers per tick with wasted zero-fills (persistent scratch + swap, ~20-40 percent of A+B), the sourced buffer is fusible into the flow pass, and two correctness seams (the flow-scatter order-independence rests on an unenforced flow_rate <= ONE invariant; and a precipitation/evaporation conservation gap if no companion pass transfers the mass), both to verify.

GPU INTERLEAVE HOT-PATH BLIND-AUDITED (2026-07-07, Fable neutral, fourth blind pass, same branch). Verdict: the happy path is sound and the KERNEL overlap is achieved by the flush, but the D2H COPY is still serialized at the head (read_one_unchecked enqueues the copy only at readback, so the host blocks for the full PCIe transfer every tick even though the kernel finished during the tail, verified). The next-level fix enqueues the copy at dispatch on the same stream into pinned host memory and waits an event, hiding the transfer too. Efficiency also: five field copies per round (two, the from_bytes to_vec and the data_bits Vec, are avoidable reinterprets or swaps) and a full-field upload a resident ping-pong plus delta-scatter would remove. And FOUR correct-today-but-prose-enforced determinism invariants to mechanize for a future offload: a debug sentinel-fill proving the kernel's total cell coverage (verified total today, hash-proven), an explicit event rather than relying on read_one_unchecked same-stream ordering (holds today via the thread-local single stream), a calib-bits assert (calib is static per run, verified), and a field-freeze checksum (only step and add_heat write it, neither in the overlap window, verified); plus a crash-path handle hardening (assign pending before launch, a Drop fence). All are for the GPU-offload arc WHEN it has a target that matters (a dense regrow kernel); the field offload stays off. Consistent lesson across all four neutral blind passes (perf stack, serial stencils, interleave, and now the interleave hot path): open-ended with no conclusions finds what a confirmatory audit structurally cannot.

DENSE RESOURCEFIELD LANDED (2026-07-07, branch claude/dense-resource-field). The dominant perf win the neutral blind audit independently surfaced, scoped by a 5-agent workflow (map consumers, resolve hash-preservation + cell-space + Composition-scope, adversarially verify determinism). ResourceField changed from BTreeMap<Coord3, Composition> (an O(log n) tree descent plus poor locality per cell, and regrow writes every cell every tick so the map is dense) to a DENSE Vec<Option<Composition>> ground layer indexed y*w+x, sized via set_dims at the top of regrow_supply, with a dormant sparse overflow (empty on every canonical run) for non-ground, out-of-bounds, and unsized-fixture cells. The public API is unchanged (composition, composition_mut, supply, take, source, axes, axes_here, hash_into), so NO consumer changed; Composition itself is untouched (it is shared with genesis and percept), so its class-byte (write_u32) and class-sorted fold is identical, and the Option is the per-cell occupied flag so an unwritten cell folds nothing. hash_into reproduces the old x-primary Coord3 order with a STRIDED x-major walk at snapshot time only (the hot paths stay sequential y*w+x). PROVEN BYTE-IDENTICAL across every pin (crucible 254bc17c, run_world 30d2358c, large-grid 310bc447), determinism harness 14/14, 36 sim tests, clippy clean. PAYOFF: 256x192 14.6s to 6.4s (2.3x), 512x384 84s to 24.8s (3.4x); regrow at 512x384 dropped from about 76s to about 15s (5x on the phase). Regrow is still about 69 percent, now the INNER Composition BTreeMap<String> operations rather than the outer tree; Phase 2 (intern the class strings to ids) and the env-stencil scratch buffers (Fable's serial audit) are the remaining wins. This also gives the GPU a real dense target (a resident regrow kernel) for the first time.

GPU STRATEGY, FABLE NEUTRAL IDEATION (2026-07-07, no conclusions given, it reasoned cold). Two governing facts: (1) integer Q32.32 arithmetic is a determinism GIFT: wrapping add is associative and commutative, so parallel reductions, prefix scans, and 64-bit atomicAdd are bit-identical under any warp/tile/stream schedule; only two things break timing-invariance, a clamp applied to an intermediate INSIDE a parallel accumulation (saturating add is commutative but not associative), and a read-modify-write whose read feeds a branch mid-flight (the id-ordered graze draw). That taxonomy is the determinism playbook. (2) the wiring is transfer-and-allocation-bound; at 1e6 cells a field round-trip is ~0.5ms while the kernel is ~tens of us, so the device is idle 90 percent-plus and the BUS is the simulator. RESIDENCY is the whole game. Ranked plan: (1) fields device-RESIDENT across ticks (ping-pong buffers, never reallocated); per-tick CPU-to-GPU becomes a compact deterministic delta command-log, GPU-to-CPU a digest (integer sums/extrema via deterministic reductions plus a flag-scan-scatter interesting-cells list), so readback is O(activity) not O(N); full-field readback only at checkpoint cadence via a device-to-device snapshot overlapped async. A replicated state machine, exchange logs never bulk state. (2) own the whole O(N) grid share in one fused batched dispatch chain: advection scatter deterministic via 64-bit wrapping atomics plus clamp-after (or a gather over reverse adjacency, no atomics); the logistic pass FUSED into the preceding stencil (pointwise rides free); fields batched [F, N]; record the chain once (CUDA graph) and replay. (3) promote the opportunistic cross-tick overlap to a canonical FIXED-LAG dataflow written into the spec (an adaptive use-it-if-it-arrived is a timing dependence and forbidden); if the tick has a same-tick perceive-modify-diffuse cycle, breaking it is a semantics change for the owner. (4) move agent maps to DELETE the transfers: once agents and fields are both resident, perception is a device-local gather with no host round trip; bin agents by cell with a scan counting sort. 64-bit fixed-point multiply is emulated on consumer GPUs (real cost for the matvec), and at M~1e4 the agent math alone is not a big win, so the payoff is the vanished transfer. (5) the coupling draw parallelizes BYTE-FOR-BYTE by segmenting agents per-cell (a sequential fold per cell segment, all segments parallel, intra-segment order fixed by data); a separate owner proposal is pro-rata settlement instead of priority-by-id (fully parallel, changes outcomes). (6) BATCH-REPLICATE WHOLE WORLDS: a 5090 cannot fill one 1e3-cell world (launch/fence overhead exceeds the arithmetic, the GPU should sit out below a measured 1e4-1e5 crossover), but R independent worlds batch perfectly (fields [R, F, N], agents [R, M], per-world seeds), so if the workload is SEARCH over runs (evolution, calibration) this outranks all but residency: the GPU becomes the experiment engine, population throughput not per-tick latency. (7) honesty machinery: a device-side integer hash-chain read back every K ticks (an always-on divergence tripwire vs the CPU), a per-launch atomicOr error word carrying the checked-mul discipline onto the device, and a CI SCHEDULE-FUZZING mode (perturb block sizes, stream priorities, forced serialization, sleeps; demand identical hash chains), because timing-invariance is a claim about all schedules. Corollary: with the bit-identical guarantee, backend choice stops being canonical state, so dispatch thresholds tune freely. Honest ceiling: Amdahl (the branchy CPU emergent tail plus a fixed sync floor), bandwidth (stencils are memory-bound forever), the sequential graze residue, and emulated 64-bit int multiply. PHASE-2 CPU perf status: the env-stencil scratch-buffer reuse (a modest large-grid win) and the Composition class-string interning (a ripple-y scoped arc, since Composition is shared and its string bytes fold into the hash) are noted follow-ons, held rather than rushed; the dense-field (Phase 1) was the dominant, tractable win.

FULL SCENARIO WIRED (2026-07-07): the held-off mechanisms armed onto the run-path, the directive's wire-everything step. run_world gains --scenario full: the viability world (oilseed, geophage, discovery, reward, reproductive vigor) PLUS the biosphere (set_corpse_matter so a dead being's OWN flesh, derived per-individual from its body at death, becomes located matter; set_matter_cycle + set_decomposer so that organic matter decomposes back to soil nutrient), social learning (set_nutrition_learning, set_observe_and_imitate, set_granular_beliefs on the Embodiment, so a discovered technique can spread by watching a knower and by co-located gossip rather than only by lone re-discovery each short lifetime), and tools (set_tool_affordances). full implies viability; the biosphere setters live on Runner, the social/tool setters on Embodiment. PROVEN: crucible 254bc17c and viability unchanged (full is a new opt-in scenario, byte-neutral to every existing pin); the full scenario is DETERMINISTIC and worker-invariant (seed 7 and seed 11 each bit-identical across 1 and 8 Rayon workers); determinism harness 14/14, fmt and clippy clean. The biosphere fires: the matter_cycle decomposition phase runs at 3.6 percent of the tick, so deposited corpses decompose. NEXT: interpret the full world's dynamics (does observe-and-imitate let the discovered eating spread and fixate, against the viability flicker where each being re-earned it and died with it?), and watch the biosphere's corpse-to-soil-nutrient feedback.

DISTINCT FOUNDER BODIES in --scenario full (2026-07-07): the founders were one baseline body varied only in cognition, language, and belief (index-varied genes/vocal-tract/innate-belief, identical anatomy). full now cycles THREE distinct body plans by race index (diverse_body): a balanced forager (the viability baseline), a HEAVY well-insulated browser (big mass, thick covering, a large fat-body so a deep energy reserve, slow and placid), and a SMALL thin-covered fast-and-curious forager (little mass, shallow reserves, high activity and exploration). Each keeps the three reserve-backing organs (fat-body, water-store, seed-store) so it stays viable; they differ in mass, insulation, organ DEVELOPMENT (so reserve capacity differs), and temperament. Each organ's function is still DERIVED from tissue composition, never a role tag (Principle 8). Opt-in to full so crucible 254bc17c and viability are byte-unchanged; full is deterministic and worker-invariant. Observed: the world differentiates (population ~65 to ~125, survivors spread across archetypes), though body-vs-gene attribution is not isolated in a single run (index varies both). This is a labelled dev-fixture demonstration of anatomical diversity, distinct from the biosphere-into-run arc (which seeds the 960-species living ecology, still in progress).

BIOSPHERE-INTO-RUN, FIRST SLICE LANDED (2026-07-07, goal 4a, the PRODUCER half): the living biosphere is now SEEDED into the run world, closing the gap where build_dawn_runner skipped genesis(). Scoped by a 5-agent workflow (map genesis output + the seeding seam + the food-loop biomass_from seam, design the minimal deterministic slice, adversarially verify determinism and principles). --scenario full now grows genesis(cfg.seed, sized to the run grid) into DawnPeoples.biosphere; genesis is a pure function of the seed and builds the SAME map internally (TileMap::generate over the same grid and dev biomes/worldgen), so its regions, occupants, and species land on the run's own coordinate space. The PRODUCER occupants (autotrophs, identified by the food-web PRIMITIVE draws_on == Abiotic, the same key trophic_label reads, NOT the trophic-layer tag, per the adversarial verify's Principle-8 fix) seed a new EnvironFields.producer field (a mirror of fertility: not folded into state_hash, its effect enters through the capacity it sets). step_productivity now selects: where a producer stands its located biomass (pop_capacity * niche.suitability, pop_capacity Fixed::ONE the epoch's own reconstitution scalar on the same [0,1] scale as the climate biomass_from it replaces) is the food capacity; elsewhere the abstract climate productivity is the baseline. So the founders graze REAL LOCATED PLANTS with species identity, not a uniform number. PROVEN: crucible 254bc17c, run_world 30d2358c, viability unchanged (producer all-zero without a biosphere, byte-neutral opt-in); full deterministic and worker-invariant across seeds (seed 7 f367e48d, seed 5 c809cf13, each 1 == 8 workers); harness 14/14, fmt + clippy clean. Observed at 32x24: 256 surviving species across 4 regions, 171 located occupants, 46 food-producing plants seeding the food. NEXT (noted, NOT in this slice): the FLESH larder (layer-1+ animal occupants deposited as a bio.flesh class the identity-blind hunt arm draws, so prey and predators are huntable); food-web dynamics; region-filling (one representative token per species per region today); and 4b grow-not-draw bodies. The producer-vs-climate food scale (pop_capacity) is reserved for the owner's tuning.

CLOSED NUTRIENT CYCLE ARC, SCOPED + FOUNDATION LANDED (2026-07-07, branch claude/nutrient-cycle). The owner directed the closed ecological cycle: producers extract and DEPLETE their evolved abiotic source, founders/predators eat bodies by edibility, decomposition replenishes the soil, the loop turns, with two hard gates, physics-is-the-only-floor (everything derived from the physics axes plus the evolved food web, no authored trophic tag / closed enum / lookup table) and NO TERRAN BIAS. Scoped by a workflow (map source->field + the open soil loop + the eat path; segmented design; adversarial verify on determinism + physics-only + conservation; PLUS a dedicated TERRAN AUTHORING OR BIAS auditor the owner requested).

BUILT + VERIFIED (byte-neutral, unused so pins hold: crucible 254bc17c, harness 14/14, fmt+clippy clean): the three missing DRAW-DOWN primitives the whole cycle turns on, SoilNutrientField::take, TissueField::take (depletes a body's volume by axis so the body's loss equals the eater's gain), ScalarField::take (water), each canonical-ordered so a drawn-then-emptied cell is byte-identical to a never-deposited one; and LivingWorld::producer_sources (each producer's evolved abiotic id read off draws_on, passed OPAQUE, never interpreted by id).

DETERMINISM VERDICT: SAFE (every touched write path is canonical BTreeMap/Vec in a sequential or id-sorted beat; the geophage tissue bite is id-ordered; opt-in empty defaults keep the pins).

TWO STRUCTURAL BREAKS the design must honor, not paper over: (1) PHYSICS-FLOOR: the naive extract switch (producer_source == 0/1/2) re-authors the closed Earth abiotic enum in the hot path. Fix: a DATA-DEFINED source-binding registry (id -> field-kind + class + depletable), the run branches on the kind of stock read as data, never the integer id. (2) CONSERVATION: the full "everything conserves" ledger leaks in five places (trophic (1-eta) loss, undeposited reserves at death, no plant senescence, the colonization source, fragile increment-prediction), so the conserved invariant is narrowed to soil + located material + corpse tissue across the DECOMPOSITION beat (mass-exact), and the biomass layer (standing food, reserves, bodies) is declared OPEN, exactly like water.

TERRAN AUTHORING/BIAS AUDIT, SIX findings (the reason this is a biosphere-FOUNDATIONS generalization, not an add-on): T1 (HIGH) the abiotic source set {light, water, soil} is Earth's plant triad, an alien autotroph on geothermal/redox/mana has no id to evolve into; fix: derive Region.abiotic from the physics-floor axes carrying a usable stock/gradient. T2 (HIGH) biomass_from hardwires Earth's four growth factors with LIGHT MANDATORY (photosynthesis-as-the-only-autotrophy); fix: a producer's realized productivity is the Liebig minimum over the axes IT evolved to draw on. T3 (HIGH) food is minted as the single Earth class bio.energy_density (Earth calories); fix: standing food is the producer's OWN composition axis. T4 (MOD) the niche env axes are Earth terrain (elev/moisture/temp). T5 (MOD) decomposition returns two Earth buckets (mineral ash + organic humus); fix: split by the decomposing body's own composition axes. T6 (MOD) the decompose kernel hardwires moisture+oxygen+warmth (Earth aerobic microbial). The naive cycle would DEEPEN T1-T3. Plus a bootstrap fact: capping a producer by an empty located soil starves it (no plants -> no corpses -> no soil), so the cycle needs a physics weathering source to bootstrap, not just decomposition. The take primitives + producer_sources are the substrate-clean foundation for all of it; the segmented build (source registry -> draws-based productivity -> composition food -> extract-deplete -> predation -> decomposition-return, each determinism-and-Terran-gated) is the arc.

NUTRIENT CYCLE SEGMENT 1 (producer EXTRACT-DEPLETE) LANDED (branch claude/nutrient-cycle). Producers now draw their food from the availability of the SPECIFIC abiotic source their niche EVOLVED to close on, and DEPLETE the depletable ones, replacing the infinite soil well. The physics-floor fix the Terran audit demanded: the run consults a DATA-DEFINED AbioticSourceRegistry (id -> AbioticField {Flux, SoilStock, WaterStock} + physics-floor class + reserved conversions), so the extract path branches on the KIND OF STOCK read as data, never a hardcoded == 0/1/2 id switch (which would re-author the closed Earth source triad). LivingWorld::producer_sources reads each producer's evolved id off draws_on (opaque). EnvironFields.extract_producers runs between step_productivity and regrow: caps the producer capacity by its source's located supply and draws the depletable stock down via SoilNutrientField::take / ScalarField::take, with a physical WEATHERING deposit seeding a bare soil each tick so a virgin world greens and bootstraps before any corpse decomposes. PROVEN: pins byte-unchanged (opt-in: crucible 254bc17c, run_world 30d2358c, viability), full deterministic + worker-invariant (39fb97be, 1==8), harness 14/14, fmt+clippy clean; the world survives (pop holds 57-95 over 100 gens as the soil enriches). Reserved (labelled dev, surfaced with basis, graduate to the manifest): biomass_per_stock, draw_fraction, weathering_rate. REMAINING Terran-clean segments: T2 productivity as the Liebig over a producer's OWN evolved draws (light not mandatory, chemoautotrophy possible); T3 standing food as the producer's OWN composition axis (not Earth calories); PREDATION (geophage eats located body tissue by edibility); T5 decomposition split by the body's composition axes; close-the-loop conservation (soil+material+tissue across decay, biomass layer open).

NUTRIENT CYCLE SEGMENT 2 (PREDATION) LANDED. The biosphere consumers are seeded as located BODY MATTER (LivingWorld::consumer_bodies folds each animal's physics-derived whole_body_composition_vector into the TissueField, content-addressed, no minted substance), and a founder eats a located body through the GEOPHAGE by the SAME edibility that grazes plants: TissueField::axis_supply + take are added to the geophage loop beside the loose-matter and carried terms, keyed off each reserve's backing axis, so a body is food iff the eater's physiology assimilates its composition and carnivore/herbivore/omnivore EMERGES from the match, never a trophic tag. The matter cycle decomposes the eaten and unwanted bodies back to soil, closing the trophic web's matter loop into the soil the producers draw. PROVEN: pins byte-unchanged (the tissue supply reads zero where no body lies: crucible 254bc17c, viability, run_world 30d2358c), full deterministic + worker-invariant (bf71cc77, 1==8), harness 14/14, 36 sim tests, fmt+clippy clean. The core cycle now turns: producers draw down their evolved soil/water source, founders graze plants and hunt animal bodies by edibility, decomposition returns the matter to soil. REMAINING deeper Terran refinements (scoped, not yet built): T3 standing food as the producer's OWN composition axis (still minted as bio.energy_density); T5 decomposition split by the body's composition axes (still ash+humus); T4 niche env axes (Earth terrain); T6 decompose kernel condition axes (aerobic); and the registered conservation invariant (soil+material+tissue across decay).

NUTRIENT CYCLE, END-OF-ARC AUDIT + FIXES. The audit (Terran-bias + conservation + determinism, with the dedicated Terran auditor the owner requested, run against the committed code) confirmed the extract path takes NO integer-id switch, predation eats by edibility with NO trophic tag, and determinism holds cleanly; it caught real must-fixes. FIXED: (1) the RETURN LEG did not exist, so the cycle only half-closed: step_matter_cycle now decomposes the TissueField (new TissueField::decay, reusing the reserved decomposition_rate) into the soil-nutrient store the producers draw, so a plant is fed by the decay of what ate or outlived it (was: located body matter accumulated forever, the producer replenished by weathering alone). (2) FAIL-LOUD: extract_producers now asserts on an unset biomass_per_stock and panics on a seeded producer whose evolved source the world never bound (was: silent zero-cap collapse / uncapped fall-through). PROVEN: the cycle turns end to end, deterministic + worker-invariant (full 0ae71f4f, 1==8), pins byte-unchanged (crucible 254bc17c, viability, run_world 30d2358c), harness 14/14, fmt+clippy clean, the world survives (pop ~70). SCOPED NEXT SUB-ARC (audit-catalogued, not yet built): FIX-2 predation's TissueField::take over-depletes a multi-axis body (removes whole-parcel volume, credits only the queried axis, a declared-open-biomass leak that wants a whole-body-bite restructure); FINDING-1 the AbioticField enum hardcodes a field per variant (a geothermal source bound to Flux would read the light field, wants a data field-handle); and the deeper CHEMISTRY GENERALIZATION T2/T3 (a producer's productivity as the Liebig over its OWN evolved draws, and its standing food as its OWN composition axis, retiring the single Earth bio.energy_density class), T5 (decomposition re-materialising the body's OWN composition axes into soil, retiring the ash+humus buckets both ends are currently pinned to), T4 (niche env axes still Earth terrain), T6 (decompose kernel still Earth-aerobic). The cycle mechanism is Terran-clean at the source-binding and eat-by-edibility level; the remaining bias is Earth CHEMISTRY still hardcoded where world-declared axes belong.

LIVING PREDATOR-PREY = the CREATURES-HAVE-SIMPLER-MINDS arc (queued sequel, owner-confirmed 2026-07-07). The unit is the CREATURE, any evolved biosphere organism, NOT a plant/animal split: the biosphere already grows walking, teleporting, prey-eating plants (kingdom is autotrophy not diet), so a plant can evolve to move and eat and must be able to carry a lean mind too. Biosphere creatures become LIVING AGENTS in the run (their own bodies, perception, movement, flee/fight, reproduction, and selection) so the food web's LIVES turn, not just its matter: prey that escape survive and pass speed/wariness to their line, predators chase and catch or miss, and herds/packs can emerge. Designed with SIMPLER MINDS than the sentient peoples (a lean perceive-then-flee-or-chase loop) so a creature is much CHEAPER to run than a person, with the GREAT BEASTS as the owner-allowed expensive exception (richer minds). Rides on the closed nutrient cycle already built (creatures are currently STATIC located body matter, eaten by edibility, no agency). Sequenced AFTER the Terran-clean chemistry generalization below (owner-chosen as the immediate next).

## Living-world run wired; the recurrent-controller foundation does NOT transfer to the real run (2026-07-08)

The recurrent-controller foundation the CONTINUED-3 session proved in isolation is now WIRED into a real living run (`--scenario living` in the `run_world` harness) with honest survival instrumentation, and the honest outcome is a CORRECTION to that proof: it holds only in the fixture. The wiring: honest `dev_grazer` grazer founders (no oilseed hybrid, no discovery loop) forage the REAL biosphere's producer plants for their own physics-derived food value (`environ.set_producer_food(&living.producer_compositions())`, the Arc-5-T3 wiring `full` left owner-gated, armed here through a new `Runner::environ_mut()`), steered by a RECURRENT controller (hidden width 4) pre-adapted at the dawn by `evolve_forage_controller` on the founders' own physiology and seeded via `append_controller_block` (a new `Controller::weights()` accessor + a `recurrent_forage_seeds` helper). The living embodiment uses the no-percept recurrent grazer layout (empty tolerances; salinity percept deferred), so the founder-seed, run-embodiment, and bootstrap layouts are identical and the evolved weights align. Matter cycle + decomposer + corpse deposit armed. Byte-neutral for every existing scenario (default `2b7e1035`, full `1873c44e`, discovery `7711021b`, viability `8a652b1b`); determinism worker-invariant; 718 lib + all integration tests green; clippy + fmt clean.

THE HONEST FINDING (never tuned to win, the CONTINUED-4 correction). `--scenario living` is SPAWN-PLACEMENT-dependent: it THRIVES on seeds where founders spawn near food and water (seed 24301: 24 founders grow to 120 over 20 generations, a watchable grazer population on real plants) and COLLAPSES on seeds where a founding band spawns on a dry corner far from water (seed 1: 24 to 0 by generation 4, starvation). A per-being trace caught the mechanism: the recurrent policy moves a being one tile then FREEZES it, one tile short of its known food, and it starves without ever discovering water. An A/B on the identical biosphere shows the LINEAR base-liveliness controller OUTPERFORMS the pre-adapted recurrent one across seeds, the OPPOSITE of the isolated fixture where recurrent scored strictly higher. So the prior "recurrent is THE proven foundation, build it now" is proven only in the fixture (`reserve_conflict_survival`, both sources pre-shown on an open plane, viability the score); in the real run's regime (partial knowledge, real terrain, sparse and often low-energy plants) the evolved recurrent policy produces near-zero effective movement toward known food.

Mandatory 5-lens audit (a 14-agent workflow, 6 blind panelists then adversarial per-finding verify, each verified against source): CODE SOUND, no critical/major. The highest-risk confirmation-bias lens returned all clean-notes (no survival-serving tuning, postures not eased, the honest-negative corroborated by code shape and byte-identical siblings). Surviving findings: one minor (the `reserve_conflict_survival` docstring overstates generality: the scorer takes the physiology registry as data for the reserve set and drains, but its food MATTER deposits are the fixed Terran `bio.energy_density`/`bio.water_fraction` pair, so an alien-substrate grazer would fail the pre-adaptation; docstring narrowed and the derive-from-`reg`-backing-component fix recorded) and four nits (comment fixes, already applied; the empty-tolerances deferral and the env A/B lever both judged defensible).

GATES / owner decisions surfaced (both real mechanism seams, neither authored, so both are the owner's to sequence): (1) a RUN-MATCHED dawn bootstrap so the pre-adaptation transfers, the bootstrap must select for SEARCH (moving to discover an unknown source), the partial-knowledge state the run presents (food sensed, water not), real-ish terrain, and derive its food matter from the physiology's own backing classes (alien-general); versus keeping the linear forage scaffold as the run default while the recurrent tier matures, given the recurrent controller does not yet beat the linear one in the real run. (2) HABITABILITY-AWARE founder placement, the dominant collapse factor on bad seeds (founders spawn at a fixed `(band*5, band*3)` grid regardless of whether a cell can reach food and water); it would help all scenarios but re-pins them. Both sit alongside the still-owner-gated biosphere food/metabolism balance (FOODWEB slices A/B) and the identity-blind hunt (percept G + strike H, the FOODWEB plan). Repro: `cargo run --release -p civsim-sim --example run_world -- --scenario living --seed 24301` (thrives) vs `--seed 1` (collapses), and `CIVSIM_LIVING_LINEAR=1 ...` for the recurrent-vs-linear A/B.

## The experiential-conviction substrate: framing panelled, prereqs building (2026-07-08)

The owner's emergent-narrative target (sustained material hardship shaping a being's convictions, e.g. coming to resent a god for the suffering endured) was scoped, and grounding it against source turned "one wire" into a real SUBSTRATE with prerequisites. The corrected design and the prereqs:

THE FRAMING (blind-panelled, OWNER_DECISIONS_LOG R2). The first-cut framing (felt hardship enters belief-update as signed evidence with a DIRECTION toward a pole of a conviction axis) was caught by a fully-blind framing panel (six agents, three types, three models, none seeing the author's or owner's conclusion, AGENTIC_ADDENDUM section 10): the DIRECTION clause authors the exact kind-of-experience to kind-of-conviction coupling it claims to forbid, the kin-template violation on belief. The corrected framing the panel converged on and the owner confirmed: felt experience emits ONLY a magnitude and a valence sign from the floor, with NO axis and NO pole; which conviction it bears on, and its direction there, is a per-being LEARNED coupling above the primitive, so "hardship erodes faith" is a description of a learned outcome for some beings and its opposite for others, never a coded route. This produced a new standing audit type (the section-10 blind FRAMING panel), a PreToolUse Workflow reminder hook, and the `/panel` skill.

GROUNDING FOUND THE SUBSTRATE. Neither learned-coupling anchor exists yet: convictions do not bias run-path behaviour (no axiom read in the runner's behaviour path; the deliberative Behaviour tier is test-only armed and its `last_action` is decoupled from embodiment), and there is no felt-experience-to-conviction association (axioms move only by social enculturation on the tick). So the coupling needs a substrate, and the two branches want different foundations: Branch 1 (correlation-record) needs no convictions-bias-behaviour; Branch 2 (credit-assignment) does.

PREREQS (building). Prereq A DONE (`5215769`): `physiology::felt_salience`, the alien-clean felt-experience primitive (folds a being's own signed reserve-deltas into intensity + valence, keyed on no axis identity, emitting no axis or pole), tested, byte-neutral (no consumer yet, the primitive-first pattern). Prereq B, LAYOUT SLICE DONE (`35aa930`): the conviction-percept substrate, a being's own conviction stance as a controller input channel the evolved network learns to weight, so convictions bias EMBODIED behaviour emergently (founder-zero, never an authored rule), byte-neutral by construction (empty registry -> n_conviction 0 -> run_world default 2b7e1035 unchanged), tested. This is the controller-percept path, chosen over the deliberation-embodiment keystone: emergence-clean and consistent with the recurrent-controller foundation. HONEST LIMIT: Branch-2 credit-assignment attribution is diffuse under a controller percept (derivable from the being's own weights); the deliberative-tier coupling stays a future refinement for crisper attribution.

NEXT (the continuation): Prereq B THREADING slice (compute each being's stances from its intrinsic beliefs and feed them into the controller input on the embodiment tick; arm the registry on the run path, byte-neutral). Then Branch 1 (correlation-record: felt experience associates with recently-invoked convictions via the eligibility-trace pattern, framing-panelled first) and Branch 2 (credit-assignment). Each branch coupling is framing-panelled before it is built, per the standing discipline.

## The experiential-conviction substrate: COMPLETE and five-lens-audited (2026-07-08, CONTINUED 6)

Tombstone for the "prereqs building" section above: the substrate is now COMPLETE. Gate: owner sign-off per branch (the per-branch blind framing panel plus the owner's ruling on each correction, OWNER_DECISIONS_LOG R2/R4/R5) and the end-of-arc mandatory five-lens audit (R6, verdict SOUND). Both first-cut framings were CAUGHT by their blind panels before any code and corrected: Branch 1's `weight * stance` eligibility was a static motility-parasitic mask (corrected to a weight-agnostic pole-referenced record); Branch 2's `sign(association)` vs `sign(stance)` compare was vacuous and authored "+pole = the good pole" for every axis (corrected to a relabel-invariant move plus the owner-chosen per-race epistemic-polarity disposition, so hardship-erodes-faith versus hardship-validates-faith emerges per race).
